# cond-mat.stat-mech [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Markov state models revisited: Principles and algorithms for unbiased observables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19452)
*David Aristof,Robert J. Webber,Daniel M. Zuckerman*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出用双转移矩阵框架替代标准马尔可夫状态模型（Markov state model, MSM）中的单一矩阵方法，以实现在任意固定滞后期和粗粒化下获得无偏的粗粒化可观测量，避免标准方法中由长滞后期引入的模型偏差并保留短时间尺度动力学信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准MSM框架使用单一转移矩阵，要求选取足够长的滞后期（lag time）以近似满足马尔可夫性（Markovian），但这会导致可避免的模型偏差并掩盖短时间尺度的动力学过程。本文旨在解决这一问题，使得可在任意固定滞后期和粗粒化下获得无偏的粗粒化可观测量。

Method: 用两个转移矩阵替代单一矩阵框架：一个表示平衡动力学（equilibrium dynamics），另一个表示源-汇循环动力学（source-sink recycling dynamics）。在无限、适当加权的数据极限下，使用正确的矩阵来估计匹配的动力学可观测量。

Result: 在无限、适当加权数据的极限下，该方法能够在任意固定滞后期和任意固定粗粒化下获得无偏的粗粒化可观测量。

Conclusion: 双转移矩阵框架可以避免标准MSM由长滞后期引入的模型偏差，并保留短时间尺度动力学信息，为分析分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）模拟提供更灵活、更精确的建模策略。

Abstract: Markov state models (MSMs) have become ubiquitous tools for analyzing molecular dynamics (MD) simulations because of their simple, powerful premise: although complete MD sampling may be impossible, the MSM can "stitch together" transition probabilities derived from local sampling to provide a global picture of kinetics and mechanisms. In the standard MSM framework, the available MD data is organized into a single transition matrix, which is then used to estimate all observables at a lag time chosen so the coarse-grained dynamics are approximately Markovian. This approach leads to avoidable model bias and motivates long lag times that obscure short-timescale processes of interest. In contrast, this paper shows how to obtain unbiased coarse-grained observables at any fixed lag time and for any fixed coarse-graining in the limit of infinite, properly weighted data. The central idea is to replace the single-matrix framework with two transition matrices -- one representing equilibrium dynamics and another representing source-sink recycling dynamics -- and use the correct matrix or matrices to estimate the matched dynamical observables.

</details>


### [2] [Localization transitions of diffusion dynamics in physical networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19486)
*Jun Yamamoto,Ivan Bonamassa,Márton Pósfai*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文揭示了物理网络（physical networks）中节点体积（node volumes）导致的局部驻留时间（local dwell times）会重塑拓扑驱动的局域化（topology-driven localization），并提出度-体积比（degree-volume ratio）作为关键无序参数（disorder parameter），通过解析模型和实证网络证明了该机制如何改变拉普拉斯谱（Laplacian spectrum）和特征模（eigenmodes）的局域化行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 网络扩散（network diffusion）是许多输运现象的基础，传统研究仅关注拓扑连通性，但物理网络中节点体积引入了局部驻留时间，调节了流量在传播前的存储过程。现有理论尚未充分解释物理异质性（physical heterogeneity）如何影响扩散动力学。

Method: 构建了一个解析模型（analytical model），以度-体积比作为无序参数，研究其在拉普拉斯谱上引起的定性重排（qualitative reorganization）；同时在多个实证网络（empirical networks）中分析度-体积相关性对极值特征模（extremal eigenmodes）局域化位置的影响。

Result: 度-体积比的失谐（ratio detuning）能够定性重组拉普拉斯谱；实证网络中的度-体积相关性将极值特征模从纯拓扑选择（topology alone）的节点上移开，表明物理性（physicality）非平凡地重塑了控制网络动力学的无序景观（disorder landscape）。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了一种普遍的、由特征丰富驱动（feature-rich-driven）的局域化控制机制，表明物理异质性以非平凡方式改变了网络动力学的无序结构，为理解和调控扩散过程提供了新视角。

Abstract: Network diffusion underlies many transport phenomena, with Laplacian modes setting how information spreads and relaxes. In physical networks, however, connectivity alone is not enough: node volumes introduce local dwell times that regulate how flow is stored before being propagated. Here we show that physical heterogeneity reshapes topology-driven localization, with the degree-volume ratio emerging as the relevant disorder parameter. We solve an analytical model in which ratio detuning qualitatively reorganizes the Laplacian spectrum, and demonstrate in empirical networks how degree-volume correlations shift extremal eigenmodes away from the nodes selected by topology alone. Our results reveal a general feature-rich-driven mechanism for localization control, showing that physicality non-trivially reshapes the disorder landscape governing network dynamics.

</details>


### [3] [Random walks in Dirichlet random environment in dimension $d+1$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20279)
*Guillaume Barraquand,Alexander K. Hartmann,Pierre Le Doussal*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟研究了时间依赖随机环境中随机游走的非典型行为与Kardar-Parisi-Zhang（KPZ）增长之间的联系，重点分析了在d=1,2,3维度下具有Dirichlet分布转移概率的离散模型，验证了KPZ增长在d=1和d=2中的适用性，并在d=3中确认了相变的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机游走在时间依赖随机环境（time-dependent random environment）中的非典型行为最近被发现与Kardar-Parisi-Zhang（KPZ）增长相关。虽然d=1维度下的这一关系已得到较好理解，但在更高维度（d>1）下，这些联系仍需进一步研究。本文旨在通过数值方法填补这一空白。

Method: 本文采用数值模拟方法，研究d=1,2,3维度下的离散模型，该模型的转移概率服从Dirichlet分布（Dirichlet distribution）。该模型是d=1中一个可积模型（integrable model）的推广，其优点在于具有显式的乘积形式平稳测度（product-form stationary measure）。

Result: 在d=1和d=2中，从原点到位置x在时间t的点到点概率（point-to-point probability）的对数方差的增长与KPZ增长相容。在d=3中，随着角度|x|/t增大存在一个相变（phase transition），并基于精确二阶矩计算给出了下界。弱无序相（weak disorder phase）中点到点概率具有重尾分布（heavy tailed distribution），强无序相（strong disorder phase）中其对数累积量随时间增长。此外，热平均（thermal average）的样本间方差可精确计算，并与近期提出的极端扩散系数（extreme diffusion coefficient）相关。

Conclusion: 本文的数值结果验证了KPZ增长在d=1和d=2中的适用性，并在d=3中确认了弱无序与强无序之间的相变。该模型允许精确计算某些关键量，为理解高维随机环境中的KPZ增长提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: The atypical behaviour of random walks in time-dependent random environment was recently related to Kardar-Parisi-Zhang (KPZ) growth. While this is now well-understood in spatial dimension $d=1$, further efforts are necessary to better understand these connections in dimensions $d>1$. In this paper, we study this problem numerically for $d=1, 2$ and $3$, focusing on a discrete model with Dirichlet distributed transition probabilities. This model is a generalization of an integrable model in $d=1$, and it has the advantage of admitting an explicit, product-form, stationary measure. We verify that the growth of the variance of the logarithm of point-to-point probabilities, namely from the origin to position $x$ in time $t$, is compatible with KPZ growth in dimension $d=1$ and $d=2$. In spatial dimension $d=3$, we confirm the existence of a phase transition as the angle $\vert x\vert /t$ increases and we obtain a lower bound based on an exact second moment calculation. We find that in the weak disorder phase the point-to-point probability acquires a heavy tailed distribution, and that in the strong disorder phase the cumulants of its logarithm grow with time. Further, we show that for this model, we can compute exactly the sample to sample variance of the thermal average $\overline{ \langle x \rangle^2}$ and that it is related to the extreme diffusion coefficient introduced recently.

</details>


### [4] [Weakly Nonlinear Dynamics of Unstable Modes in Jammed Amorphous Solids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19818)
*Kota Noto,Harukuni Ikeda,Kuniyasu Saitoh,Hisao Hayakawa*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过分析广义Hessian矩阵（generalized Hessian matrix）的本征模态（eigenmodes），研究堵塞非晶态固体（jammed amorphous solids）中的结构演化。该矩阵利用波数（wave numbers）引入空间调制，通过基于傅里叶（Fourier）的扩展能够捕捉力学不稳定模态（unstable modes）。研究表明，不稳定本征模态的激发会导致与初始扰动无关的结构重排，并推导出类似朗道方程（Landau equation）的弱非线性振幅方程（weakly nonlinear amplitude equation）来描述不稳定模态的增长与饱和，为理解无序固体（disordered solids）中失稳驱动的构型变化提供了框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的Hessian矩阵仅能描述力学稳定（mechanically stable）区域的响应，无法研究失稳后的结构演化。本文旨在提出一个广义Hessian矩阵，使其能够捕捉线性不稳定模态，从而突破这一限制，深入理解堵塞非晶态固体中由失稳驱动的结构重排机制。

Method: 构建一个包含波数空间调制（spatial modulation via wave numbers）的广义Hessian矩阵，通过傅里叶扩展引入对线性不稳定模态的分析能力。利用该矩阵的本征模态分析结构演化，并推导与朗道方程形式类似的弱非线性振幅方程，用以描述不稳定模态的增长和饱和行为。

Result: 模拟结果表明，激发不稳定本征模态能够导致结构重排，且该重排独立于初始扰动。此外，推导出的弱非线性振幅方程可以描述不稳定模态从增长到饱和的完整演化过程。

Conclusion: 本文提出的广义Hessian矩阵框架为理解无序固体中失稳驱动的构型变化提供了系统性的理论途径，为后续研究堵塞体系中非平衡演化和结构转变奠定了基础。

Abstract: We investigate the structural evolution in jammed amorphous solids by analyzing the eigenmodes of a generalized Hessian matrix that incorporates spatial modulation via wave numbers. Unlike the conventional Hessian, this generalized formulation captures linearly unstable modes through a Fourier-based extension of the Hessian matrix, enabling us to study responses beyond the mechanically stable regime. We demonstrate that the excitation of unstable eigenmodes leads to structural rearrangements independent of the initial perturbation by the simulation. Furthermore, we derive a weakly nonlinear amplitude equation to describe the growth and saturation of these unstable modes, analogous to the Landau equation. Our framework provides a pathway to understand instability-driven configuration changes in disordered solids.

</details>


### [5] [Motility destabilizes an absorbing-state flock](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20034)
*Narayan Dutt Sharma,Subroto Mukerjee,Chandan Dasgupta,Sriram Ramaswamy*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过一维晶格模型发现，非运动极限下的吸收铁磁态在引入偏向运动（biased motility）后失稳，系统随有序强度降低经历从有序群集（ordered flock）到无序状态的连续相变。有限尺寸标度分析显示临界指数满足一维超标度关系（hyperscaling relation），为活动性诱导无序提供了定量证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究普遍认为运动性（motility）活动可促进多体系统有序性，本文旨在考察运动性是否可能相反地引入无序，通过建立一维晶格模型来检验活动性（activity）对有序相变的影响。

Method: 提出一维晶格模型，在非运动极限下具有吸收铁磁态（absorbing ferromagnetic states）；引入偏向运动作为活动性，并改变有序强度（alignment strength）进行数值模拟；采用有限尺寸标度分析（finite-size scaling analysis）对物理量的临界行为进行定量表征。

Result: 偏向运动使吸收铁磁态失稳；系统随有序强度降低经历从有序群集态到无序态的连续相变（continuous transition）；临界指数满足一维超標度关系。

Conclusion: 活动性可以诱导无序，并支持临界行为满足一维超標度关系，提供了活动性导致无序的定量证据。

Abstract: Activity, when it takes the form of motility, is generally seen to promote order in many-body systems. Here we present a one-dimensional lattice model that, in the non-motile limit, exhibits absorbing ferromagnetic states. When activity is introduced through biased motility, these absorbing state are destabilised and the system instead undergoes a transition from an ordered flock to a disordered state as the alignment strength is decreased. A finite-size scaling analysis of physical quantities reveals a continuous transition with critical exponents satisfying the hyperscaling relation in one dimension, providing quantitative evidence for the activity-induced disorder.

</details>


### [6] [Logarithmic scaling correction in quench dynamics of the J1-J2 Potts model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20081)
*Kun Li,Wanzhou Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究J1-J2反铁磁Potts模型在热淬火过程中的动力学标度行为，发现终止于准长程序（QLRO）相的淬火表现出含对数修正的Kibble-Zurek机制（KZM）标度，而终止于长程序（LRO）相的淬火则遵循传统幂律标度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已知二维XY模型在拓扑相变中KZM标度存在显著的对数修正，但在具有两个连续拓扑相变的离散自旋系统中，这种对数标度修正是否出现尚不明确。

Method: 研究以J1-J2反铁磁Potts模型为对象，首先构建其平衡相图；然后根据顺磁相、准长程序（quasi-long-range ordered, QLRO）相、长程序（long-range ordered, LRO）相及零温基态的温度区间，设计了四种具有不同温度间隔的淬火方案。

Result: 终止于QLRO相的淬火显示出含对数修正的KZM标度，过剩能量密度（excess energy density）随淬火速率的变化符合二维XY模型的动力学普适类；终止于LRO相（包括有限温度和零温协议）的淬火则遵循传统幂律标度。

Conclusion: 结果清晰揭示了J1-J2 Potts模型的特征标度修正，为未来通过光子模拟平台对KZM进行实验研究提供了理论指导。

Abstract: In conventional quench dynamics governed by the Kibble-Zurek mechanism (KZM), the defect density generally decays as a pure power law of the quench rate. However, the KZM scaling of the two-dimensional (2D) XY model with topological phase transitions features prominent logarithmic corrections. Nevertheless, it remains unclear whether such logarithmic scaling corrections emerge in discrete-spin systems that host two successive topological phase transitions under thermal quenches. This work investigates the J1-J2 antiferromagnetic Potts model and constructs its equilibrium phase diagram. Based on the temperature ranges of the paramagnetic phase, quasi-long-range ordered (QLRO) phase, long-range ordered phase, and zero-temperature ground state, we design four quench protocols with distinct temperature intervals. Our results demonstrate that quenches terminating in the QLRO phase exhibit logarithmically corrected KZM scaling of the excess energy density, consistent with the dynamical universality class of the 2D XY model. In contrast, quenches ending in the LRO phase, including both finite-temperature and zero-temperature protocols, follow conventional power-law scaling. Our results clearly uncover the characteristic scaling corrections of the J1-J2 Potts model and offer theoretical guidance for future experimental investigations of KZM via photonic simulation platforms.

</details>


### [7] [Derivation of the Boltzmann equation with no "molecular chaos"-type approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20134)
*Victor F. Los*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从刘维尔方程（Liouville equation）出发，在不借助“分子混沌（molecular chaos）”近似的前提下，严格推导出了s粒子分布函数$F_s(t)$的完全封闭演化方程；通过投影算子将非齐次Nakajima-Zwanzig广义主方程（GME）转化为齐次形式，并在密度线性近似下得到了单粒子和两粒子分布函数的方程，最终在大时间尺度下恢复为线性乃至非线性玻尔兹曼方程（Boltzmann equation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有从刘维尔方程推导多粒子分布函数封闭演化方程的方法通常依赖“分子混沌”类近似，限制了其适用范围。本文旨在不引入此类假设，并从任意初始条件出发，严格推导出s粒子分布函数的完全封闭演化方程。

Method: 引入一种特殊的投影算子（projection operator），将非齐次的Nakajima-Zwanzig广义主方程中的无关初始条件项精确变换为齐次形式，从而使初始关联（initial correlations）通过核函数（kernel）纳入对$F_s(t)$演化的影响；随后在粒子密度$n$的线性近似下对核函数进行简化，并分别导出单粒子与两粒子分布函数的方程。

Result: 在密度线性近似下得到了$F_1(t)$和$F_2(t)$的演化方程；初始关联对$F_1(t)$的影响在时间尺度$t \sim t_{\text{rel}} \gg t_{\text{cor}}$上消失，从而得到线性玻尔兹曼方程；在$t_{\text{cor}} \ll t \ll t_{\text{rel}}$区间可表示为非线性玻尔兹曼方程；当$t_{\text{rel}} \to \infty$（即平均自由程$l \to \infty$）时，玻尔兹曼方程对所有有限时间$t \gg t_{\text{cor}}$均成立。

Conclusion: 本文在不使用分子混沌近似的前提下，从刘维尔方程出发成功地封闭了s粒子分布函数的演化方程，并严格证明了在大时间尺度下初始关联效应衰减，最终恢复为经典的玻尔兹曼方程，为非平衡统计力学（nonequilibrium statistical mechanics）提供了更严格的微观基础。

Abstract: The paper resolves the problem of the derivation of a completely closed evolution equation for $s$-particle distribution function $F_s(t)$ ($s \le N$) from the Liouville equation for $N \gg 1$-particle distribution function $F_N(t)$ with arbitrary initial condition $F_N(0)$ and without any use of the "molecular chaos" type approximation. The initial correlations are accounted for in this equation in the kernel governing the evolution of $F_s(t)$ via the special projection operator which exactly transforms the inhomogeneous Nakajima-Zwanzig Generalized Master Equation (GME) with an irrelevant initial condition term into the homogenous one. This equation is further simplified by presenting its kernel in the linear in the particles' density $n$ approximation. In this approximation the equations for one-particle $F_1(t)$ and two-particle $F_2(t)$ distribution functions are derived. It is shown that the terms describing the influence of initial correlations in the equation for $F_1(t)$ disappear at the large timescale $t \sim t_{\text{rel}} \gg t_{\text{cor}}$ ($t_{\text{cor}}$ is a short correlation time as compared to a relaxation time $t_{\text{rel}}$ of $F_1(t)$) resulting in the linear Boltzmann equation. This equation can be presented as the nonlinear Boltzmann equation in the time interval $t_{\text{cor}} \ll t \ll t_{\text{rel}}$. At $t_{\text{rel}} \to \infty$ (mean free path $l \to \infty$) the Boltzmann equation holds for all finite times $t \gg t_{\text{cor}}$.

</details>


### [8] [Optimal Finite-Time Control of Nonreciprocal Brownian Dimers: Thermodynamic Anomaly and Multiple Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20420)
*Ruicheng Bao*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文精确求解了两个受谐波势阱牵引的非互易布朗粒子的有限时间热力学最优控制问题，发现存在一个有限临界时间，超过该时间后外部功的下确界为负无穷，即可提取功和输出功率无上界；物理正则化（如有限阱程和力饱和）可恢复有限最优解，并将奇点转化为类似一级或二级相变的最优协议转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非互易相互作用（nonreciprocal interaction）下两个布朗粒子（Brownian particles）的有限时间热力学最优控制（finite-time thermodynamic optimal control）问题，探索非互易性如何通过内禀主动力（internal active force）耦合两个控制通道（center and separation），以及由此产生的异常热力学行为。

Method: 采用精确求解方法，对两个受谐波势阱（harmonic traps）牵引的非互易耦合布朗粒子，同时操控质心（center）和间距（separation）两个自由度，求解有限时间热力学最优控制问题。

Result: 最优协议呈现振荡行为；即使目标间距不变，协议也会主动打开二聚体；非互易性可在输运过程中提取功。核心发现是存在一个有限临界时间（finite critical time），超过该阈值时外部功的下确界（infimum）为负无穷。引入有限阱程（finite trap range）或力饱和（force saturation）等物理正则化后，奇点消失：零目标间距下，硬性有限阱程导致从零协议到最大阱程协议的一级相变式跃迁（first-order-like jump）；平滑力饱和则产生连续二级相变式（second-order-like）转变。有限阱程约束下，最优协议可出现多次有限时间转变，产生多个功-持续时间扭结（work-duration kinks）。

Conclusion: 非互易相互作用可导致有限时间热力学控制中出现异常的发散行为，物理正则化不仅恢复有限最优解，还将奇点转化为类似相变的最优协议转变，揭示了非互易系统在有限时间热力学中独特的相变结构和临界现象。

Abstract: We solve exactly a finite-time thermodynamic optimal control problem for two nonreciprocally interacting Brownian particles translated by two harmonic traps. The controller manipulates both the center and separation of the pair. Nonreciprocal interactions generate an internal active force that couples these two channels. The optimal protocol is oscillatory, deliberately opens the dimer even when the target separation is unchanged, and can extract work during transport. A central finding is a finite critical time beyond which the external-work infimum is $-\infty$: at any prescribed duration beyond this threshold, both extractable work and output power are unbounded. Physical regularizations such as finite trap range and force saturation restore a finite optimum and convert the anomaly into optimal-protocol transitions: in the zero-target case, a hard finite range produces a first-order-like jump from the zero protocol to a maximum-range protocol, whereas smooth force saturation gives a continuous, second-order-like onset. Under finite-range constraints, the optimal protocol can further undergo multiple finite-time transitions, producing multiple work-duration kinks with no qualitative analog in prior studies.

</details>


### [9] [Stable valleys in the glassy landscape of a low-density parity-check (LDPC) code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20421)
*Grace M. Sommers,David A. Huse*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究定义在膨胀图（expander graphs）上的经典低密度奇偶校验码（cLDPC codes）所对应的统计力学模型，发现其在低温下存在多种稳定且不一致的能谷（valleys），并揭示了微正则系综（microcanonical ensemble）与正则系综（canonical ensemble）在某些能谷中的不等价性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典低密度奇偶校验码（classical low-density parity-check, cLDPC codes）不仅是构建优质量子低密度奇偶校验码（quantum LDPC codes）的基础，其本身还定义了有趣的统计力学模型，能够在不引入淬火无序（quenched randomness）或阻挫（frustration）的情况下展现自旋玻璃序（spin glass order）。本文旨在通过具体案例系统地研究这一现象。

Method: 以定义在局部树状膨胀图（locally tree-like expander graph）上的cLDPC码为案例，利用局部树状性质采用树上的递归技术（recursive techniques on trees），探测由低温下不同边界条件诱导的多种稳定且不一致的能谷。同时在封闭有限图上对这些能谷进行数值研究。

Result: 递归分析揭示了多种稳定的、不相容的能谷由不同的边界条件在低温下诱导产生。封闭有限图上的数值研究表明，某些能谷中微正则系综与正则系综不等价。

Conclusion: cLDPC码对应的统计力学模型展现出丰富的低温能谷结构，且不同系综在部分能谷中不等价，这表明该类模型具有非平凡的统计力学行为。

Abstract: Classical low-density parity-check (cLDPC) codes defined on expander graphs are a fundamental ingredient in the construction of good quantum LDPC codes, a recent milestone in quantum error correction. They also define interesting statistical mechanics models in their own right, as they include examples of spin glass order without quenched randomness or frustration. We investigate this via a case study of a cLDPC code on a locally tree-like expander graph. Recursive techniques on trees, made possible by the locally tree-like property, probe a menagerie of stable, incongruent valleys induced by imposing different boundary conditions at low temperature. A complementary numerical study of the valleys on closed finite graphs reveals the inequivalence of the microcanonical and canonical ensemble for certain valleys.

</details>

### [10] [Anticoncentration of the Permanent in Ginibre Ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20329)
*Frederic Koehler,Pui Kuen Leung*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了标准Ginibre矩阵的行序化永久的径向密度上界，证明了其L∞范数以n^{(β+2)/4}增长，并由此解决了Aaronson与Arkhipov提出的永久反集中猜想（Permanent Anticoncentration Conjecture）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 永久反集中猜想（Permanent Anticoncentration Conjecture）由Aaronson与Arkhipov在量子计算复杂性理论中提出，其成立与否直接关系到玻色采样（BosonSampling）问题是否能够展示量子优越性。本文旨在严格证明该猜想在复数域上的成立。

Method: 设$\mathbb{K}\in\{\mathbb{R},\mathbb{C},\mathbb{H}\}$（实数、复数、四元数），记$\beta=\dim_{\mathbb{R}}\mathbb{K}$，$G_n^{\mathbb{K}}$为标准$\mathbb{K}$-Ginibre矩阵。定义归一化行序化永久$W_n^{\mathbb{K}}=\operatorname{per}_{\mathbb{K}}G_n^{\mathbb{K}}/\sqrt{n!}$。通过将高斯永久平方与平方Study行列式（squared (Study) determinant）在拉普拉斯变换序（Laplace-transform order）下进行比较，推导出径向密度$p_n^{\mathbb{K}}$的显式上界。

Result: 证明了归一化行序化永久$W_n^{\mathbb{K}}$具有径向密度$p_n^{\mathbb{K}}$，且满足$\|p_n^{\mathbb{K}}\|_\infty=p_n^{\mathbb{K}}(0)\lesssim_βn^{(β+2)/4}$以及$\sup_{z\in\mathbb{K}}\mathbb{P}(|W_n^{\mathbb{K}}-z|\leq\varepsilon)\lesssim_βn^{(β+2)/4}\varepsilon^β$。特别地，当$\mathbb{K}=\mathbb{C}$（即$\beta=2$）时，该结果证明了Aaronson与Arkhipov的永久反集中猜想。

Conclusion: 本文通过拉普拉斯变换序的比较方法，给出了多种域上Ginibre矩阵永久的反集中上界，并在复数域情形下彻底解决了著名的永久反集中猜想，为量子计算复杂性理论中的玻色采样问题提供了关键的理论支撑。

Abstract: Let $\mathbb{K}\in\{\mathbb{R},\mathbb{C},\mathbb{H}\}$, put $β=\dim_{\mathbb{R}}\mathbb{K}$, and let $G_n^{\mathbb{K}}$ be an $n\times n$ matrix with i.i.d. standard $\mathbb{K}$-Gaussian entries, namely a standard $\mathbb{K}$-Ginibre matrix. We prove that the normalized row-ordered permanent $W_n^{\mathbb{K}}=\operatorname{per}_{\mathbb{K}}G_n^{\mathbb{K}}/\sqrt{n!}$ has a radial density $p_n^{\mathbb{K}}$ satisfying $\|p_n^{\mathbb{K}}\|_\infty=p_n^{\mathbb{K}}(0)\lesssim_βn^{(β+2)/4}$ and $\sup_{z\in\mathbb{K}}\mathbb{P}(|W_n^{\mathbb{K}}-z|\leq\varepsilon)\lesssim_βn^{(β+2)/4}\varepsilon^β$. In particular, for $\mathbb{K}=\mathbb{C}$, this resolves the Permanent Anticoncentration Conjecture of Aaronson and Arkhipov. The proof compares the squared Gaussian permanent with the squared (Study) determinant in Laplace-transform order.

</details>

### [11] [Neutrino t-channels at Colliders: When Light Neutrinos Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19461)
*Claudia Garcia-Garcia,Manuel González-López,Xabier Marcano,Daniel Naredo-Tuero*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了重中性轻子（HNL）介导的t-道过程，以LHC上的矢量玻色子散射通道WW→ℓℓ为例，指出轻中微子在恢复散射振幅高能幺正性中的关键作用，并强调完整 seesaw 谱的一致处理会显著改变 HNL 寻找的唯象学，进而提出 pp→eμjj 通道可作为探测 TeV 标度 HNL 的新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用重中性轻子（Heavy Neutral Lepton, HNL）介导的t-道过程，探索超出高能对撞机直接产生运动学可达范围的质量标度，并纠正此前研究中忽略轻中微子作用所导致的唯象学偏差。

Method: 以LHC上矢量玻色子散射（vector boson scattering）通道 WW→ℓℓ 为案例，纳入完整 seesaw 谱（包括轻中微子），分析散射振幅的高能幺正性（unitarity）行为，并研究 pp→eμjj 通道中轻子数守恒但轻子味破坏（lepton flavor violating）的末态信号。

Result: 轻中微子的引入导致相消干涉（destructive interference），强烈压制了轻子数破坏（lepton number violating）信号；而 pp→eμjj 通道在低标度 seesaw 模型（low-scale seesaw scenarios）且具有显著主动-惰性混合（active-sterile mixing）时，可有效探测 TeV 标度的 HNL，灵敏度超越现有直接搜寻。

Conclusion: 一致处理完整 seesaw 谱对 HNL 唯象学至关重要；轻子数守恒但轻子味破坏的末态是更有前景的搜索方向，pp→eμjj 通道可拓展 LHC 对 TeV 标度 HNL 的探测能力。

Abstract: Heavy Neutral Lepton (HNL)-mediated t-channel processes provide a unique opportunity to probe mass scales beyond the kinematic reach of direct production at high-energy colliders. We revisit these processes using the vector boson scattering channel $WW\to\ell\ell$ at the LHC as a case study, highlighting the essential role of the light neutrinos in restoring the proper high-energy unitary behavior of the scattering amplitude. Their inclusion, overlooked in some previous studies, leads to destructive interference that strongly suppresses lepton number violating signatures, demonstrating that a consistent treatment of the full seesaw spectrum qualitatively alters the phenomenology of t-channel HNL searches. This motivates the exploration of lepton number conserving but lepton flavor violating final states instead. We present a detailed analysis of the $pp\to eμjj$ channel and show that it provides a promising probe of TeV-scale HNLs in low-scale seesaw scenarios with sizable active-sterile mixing, extending the LHC sensitivity beyond existing direct searches.

### [12] [PDF at small $x$ in the non-perturbative region](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.12489)
*M. L. Nekrasov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在包含部分子劈裂（branching cascades）与部分子融合（parton fusion）的升级部分子模型中，研究快速运动质子中在小x区域的parton distribution function (PDF)行为：在中等小x区域得到幂律行为，在极小x区域发现部分子密度饱和现象，并与微扰QCD（perturbative QCD）对数近似结果进行了比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的部分子分布函数（PDF）在小x区域的研究主要基于微扰QCD的对数近似方程，但对部分子劈裂与融合过程的统一处理尚不充分。本文旨在通过引入包含分支级联（branching cascades）和部分子融合的升级部分子模型，更全面地刻画PDF在小x区域的动力学行为。

Method: 采用升级的部分子模型（upgraded parton model），同时纳入部分子劈裂引起分支级联和部分子融合效应。部分子融合的引入导致PDF满足非线性方程。在中等小x和极小x区域分别进行解析分析，并在饱和 regime 下给出模型估计。

Result: 在中等小x区域，部分子密度 x f(x) 呈现幂律行为，其指数与部分子劈裂概率的对数（logarithm of the probability of parton splitting）成正比。在极小x区域，观察到部分子密度饱和现象（saturation of the parton density），并得到了该 regime 下饱和值的模型估计。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，部分子融合效应在小x区域不可忽略，它导致PDF满足非线性方程并引致部分子密度饱和。所得结果与先前基于微扰QCD对数近似（logarithmic approximations）方程的分析结果具有可比性。

Abstract: Parton distribution function (PDF) at small $x$ in a fast-moving proton is investigated within an upgraded parton model that includes parton splitting with branching cascades and parton fusion. In the region of moderately small $x$, we obtain a power-law behavior of the parton density $x f(x)$ with an exponent proportional to the logarithm of the probability of parton splitting. Taking into account parton fusion leads to a nonlinear equation for the PDF. In the region of very small $x$, the phenomenon of saturation of the parton density is detected and a model estimate of its value in this regime is obtained. The results are compared with those obtained previously based on the analysis of equations in logarithmic approximations of perturbative QCD.

### [13] [Monopoles, Strings, Walls and Gravitational waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20340)
*Rinku Maji,Qaisar Shafi*

TL;DR: 本文研究了规范对称性逐级破缺（SU(2)→U(1)→Z₂→1 与 SU(3)→SO(3)→Z₂→1）产生的单极子、弦以及由弦束缚的畴壁（WBS）所发射的引力波谱，并分析了复合弦在有效稳定、准稳定和亚稳态三种演化场景下的引力波特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索多步规范对称性破缺（gauge symmetry breaking）产生的拓扑缺陷（单极子、弦、畴壁）及其衰变过程中的引力波辐射，以揭示宇宙早期相变（phase transition）的物理信号。

Method: 通过分析 SU(2)→U(1)→Z₂→1 破缺链中单极子（monopole）、弦（string）和由弦束缚的畴壁（domain walls bounded by strings, WBS）的拓扑结构，计算基本弦和 WBS 发射的引力波谱，并结合复合弦（composite strings）的有效稳定（stable）、准稳定（quasistable）或亚稳态（metastable）演化场景给出引力波频谱。

Result: 基本弦和 WBS 在衰变过程中会发射引力波，且 WBS 衰变产生与单极子承载相同 U(1) 磁通量的复合弦网络。研究表明，复合弦的稳定性影响最终的引力波谱；SU(3)→SO(3)→Z₂→1 破缺链也能实现类似的三种场景。

Conclusion: 基于 SU(2) 和 SU(3) 味规范对称性（flavor gauge symmetries）的破缺链可产生具有不同稳定性的复合弦，其引力波信号为探测早期宇宙拓扑缺陷演化提供了可观测的途径。

Abstract: The gauge symmetry breaking $SU(2) \to U(1) \to Z_2 \to 1$ successively produces monopoles, strings and domain walls bounded by strings (WBS), with the elementary monopole carrying a $U(1)$ magnetic flux twice as large as the elementary string. The elementary strings and subsequently WBS emit gravitational waves, and during their decay, the WBS yield a network of composite strings that carry the same $U(1)$ flux as the monopoles. Depending on the cosmological evolution, we provide the gravitational wave spectra generated by the elementary strings and WBS, in combination with the composite strings which are either effectively stable, quasistable, or metastable. These three scenarios are also realized in the symmetry breaking chain $SU(3) \to SO(3) \to Z_2 \to 1$. Both $SU(2)$ and $SU(3)$ have appeared in the literature as flavor gauge symmetries.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有线性关系（linear relations）中单参数半群（one-parameter semigroups）的理论尚不完整，缺乏对生成元（generator）系统性的刻画与推广。

Method: 通过引入域-多值正交关系（domain-multivalued orthogonal relations，简称 d.m.o. relations）这一核心概念，建立线性关系上单参数半群的统一理论框架，并利用该框架扩展经典半群理论中的必要与充分条件。

Result: 完整刻画了一致连续半群（uniformly continuous semigroups）与强连续半群（strongly continuous semigroups）的生成元，分别证明了它们为极大 d.m.o. 关系与稠密 d.m.o. 关系。将 Hille-Yosida 定理与 Lumer-Phillips 定理推广至该设定，给出了压缩 C₀-半群（maximal anti-accumulative relations）与酉算子半群（anti-selfadjoint relations）的生成条件。

Conclusion: 该严格框架为理解线性关系中单参数半群的独特性质提供了新的视角，填补了该领域生成元理论系统化的空白。

Abstract: This article develops a theory of one-parameter semigroups for linear relations, introducing the notion of domain-multivalued orthogonal (d.m.o.) relations. We establish complete characterizations for generators of uniformly and strongly continuous semigroups, showing them to be maximal and densely d.m.o. relations, respectively. Furthermore, the Hille-Yosida and Lumer-Phillips theorems are extended to this general setting, providing necessary and sufficient conditions for generating $C_0$-semigroups of contractions (identified as maximal anti-accumulative relations) and unitary operators (anti-selfadjoint relations). This rigorous framework sheds new light on the peculiarities of one-parameter semigroups for linear relations.

### [15] [Recurrence Coefficients of the Orthogonal Polynomials for Oscillatory Jacobi-type Weight Functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19797)
*Shulin Lyu,Xun Zhou*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究两类振荡型雅可比权函数（oscillatory Jacobi-type weight functions）及其关联的正交多项式（orthogonal polynomials），通过阶梯算子（ladder operators）与相容性条件推导出三项递推系数（three-term recurrence coefficients）所满足的耦合差分方程，并据此推测系数的符号形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于振荡型雅可比权函数关联正交多项式的结果中，三向递推系数的差分方程结构复杂且阶数较高，本文旨在推导结构更简单、阶数更低的耦合差分方程，以简化系数的计算与符号形式的推测。

Method: 采用近期文献中为单首正交多项式（monic orthogonal polynomials）建立的阶梯算子，并结合三个相容性条件（compatibility conditions），推导出两类振荡型雅可比权函数对应的三向递推系数所满足的耦合差分方程。

Result: 得到了两条耦合的差分方程，相比已有结果结构更简单且阶数更低。在确定初始值后，可通过这些差分方程逐步计算任意阶段的递推系数，并由此推测系数的符号形式。

Conclusion: 本文提出的方法有效简化了振荡型雅可比权函数正交多项式递推系数的计算，所获表达式为符号形式的猜想提供了依据。

Abstract: We study two classes of oscillatory Jacobi-type weight functions $x^c(1-x^2)^{λ-1/2}\exp(iζx)$, $x\in[-1,1], λ>-1/2, c\in\{0,1\}$. Other restrictions are imposed on $λ$ and $ζ$ to guarantee the existence of the associated orthogonal polynomials. By using the ladder operators established in the recent literature for monic orthogonal polynomials associated with Jacobi-type weight functions and three compatibility conditions, we derive two coupled difference equations satisfied by the three-term recurrence coefficients. Compared with the existing results, these equations are structurally simpler and of lower order. Once the initial values are determined, the recurrence coefficients can be computed at any stage through the difference equations. The obtained expressions enable us to conjecture the symbolic forms for the recurrence coefficients.

### [16] [Explicit Hamiltonian structure of the Flaschka-Newell Painlevé II hierarchy via symmetry reduction of the Painlevé IV hierarchy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20106)
*Olivier Marchal,Mohamad Alameddine,Sergej Laub*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本论文通过亚纯联络空间（space of meromorphic connections）的对称约化，研究了 Flaschka-Newell 第二类潘勒韦层级（Painlevé II hierarchy）的哈密顿结构，构建了适应对合（involution）的达布坐标（Darboux coordinates），并导出了约化后的哈密顿量（Hamiltonians）与 Lax 矩阵的显式表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在揭示 Flaschka-Newell Painlevé II 层级的哈密顿结构，并展示如何通过对称性约化从 Painlevé IV 层级导出该层级，以阐明等单调系统（isomonodromic systems）在辛几何（symplectic geometry）层面上的显式约化机制。

Method: 基于 Painlevé IV 层级通过 $\mathbb{Z}_2$-对称性约化为 Painlevé II 层级的实现，构建一组适应对合的达布坐标；通过适当改变平凡化（trivialization），使对称性在这些坐标中对角作用，从而将不动点集（fixed-point locus）显式描述为一个辛子流形（symplectic submanifold），进而导出约化后的哈密顿量与Lax矩阵。

Result: 获得了 Flaschka-Newell Painlevé II 层级的哈密顿量与 Lax 矩阵的显式表达式，并展示了对称性适配的规范达布坐标（symmetry-adapted canonical Darboux coordinates）如何使等单调系统在辛几何层面的显式约化成为可能。

Conclusion: 对称性适配的达布坐标是进行等单调系统辛几何约化的有效工具；该策略为理解 Painlevé 层级之间的约化关系提供了清晰的哈密顿框架。

Abstract: We study the Hamiltonian structure of the Flaschka-Newell Painlevé II hierarchy via symmetry reduction of the associated space of meromorphic connections. Building on the realization of this hierarchy as a reduction of the Painlevé IV hierarchy via a $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetry, we construct a set of Darboux coordinates adapted to the involution. After a suitable change of trivialization, the symmetry acts diagonally in these coordinates, allowing the fixed-point locus to be explicitly described as a symplectic submanifold. This enables us to derive the reduced Hamiltonians after symmetry, thereby obtaining explicit expressions for the Hamiltonians and the Lax matrices of the Flaschka-Newell Painlevé II hierarchy. This strategy also illustrates how symmetry-adapted canonical Darboux coordinates enable explicit reductions of isomonodromic systems at the level of their underlying symplectic geometry.

</details>


### [17] [A perturbative microscopic derivation of the focusing $Φ^6_1$ measure with rough cut-off](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20400)
*Shahnaz Farhat,Andrew Rout*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文推导了具有粗糙截断的聚焦非线性薛定谔方程（focusing nonlinear Schrödinger equation, NLS）在圆环上的吉布斯测度（Gibbs measure），扩展了先前关于光滑截断的结果，并给出了近期文献中推导的替代证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将早先针对光滑截断的吉布斯测度推导结果推广到粗糙截断情形，并解决因截断缺乏光滑性所带来的技术困难。

Method: 基于Fröhlich、Knowles、Schlein和Sohinger（2017）发展的微扰展开（perturbative expansion）；采用Wigner测度方法（Wigner measure approach）和归纳论证（inductive argument）来克服截断缺乏光滑性的问题。

Result: 成功推导了具有粗糙截断的聚焦非线性薛定谔方程在圆环上的吉布斯测度，并给出了聚焦五次NLS在最优截断下吉布斯测度的推导。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一种替代性证明路径，验证了Lü、Nam和Zhu（2026）的最新推导结果，并推广了Sohinger与合作者关于光滑截断的早期工作。

Abstract: We give a derivation of the Gibbs measure for the focusing nonlinear Schrödinger equation (NLS) on the circle with rough cut-off. This extends earlier work by Sohinger and the second author, which proved analogous results for smooth cut-offs. Our proof is based on the perturbative expansion developed by Fröhlich, Knowles, Schlein, and Sohinger (2017), and provides an alternative proof of the recent derivation given in Lü, Nam, and Zhu (2026). To prove convergence of the explicit terms, we employ a Wigner measure approach and an inductive argument to overcome the lack of smoothness for the cut-off. In particular, we give a derivation of the Gibbs measure for the focusing quintic NLS with the optimal cut-off from Oh, Sosoe, and Tolomeo (2022).

</details>

### [18] [How many degrees of freedom describe a quantum N-particle state?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16988)
*Matthew J. Lake,Marek L. Miller*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文指出，在经典牛顿时空中，N粒子系统有3(N-1)个关系性（relational）物理自由度；但在量子力学中，所有3N个正则自由度都是物理的，非关系性自由度会导致广义不确定性关系（GURs），并影响量子参考系（QRF）的描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典力学中，净动量守恒允许通过约束消除非物理的质心变量，从而将物理自由度缩减为3(N-1)个关系性自由度。作者试图检验这一逻辑在量子力学中是否仍然成立，并探究其物理后果。

Method: 通过构造量子算符类比经典净动量，尝试在量子理论中施加同类约束，并检验是否会导致物理信息的丢失。以此为基础，分析非关系性变量带来的修正项，并推导广义不确定性关系（GURs）。

Result: 在量子力学中，净动量算符不能像经典情形那样用于施加约束而不丢失物理信息，因此所有3N个正则自由度都是物理的，其中只有3(N-1)个是关系性的。非关系性变量会导致广义不确定性关系（GURs），其中非海森堡项定义了量子参考系（QRF）在实空间和动量空间中的伽利略不变展宽（Galilean-invariant spreads）。

Conclusion: 该结果对近期关系性模型（relational models）和量子参考系（QRF）的“视角中立”（perspective neutral）框架具有启示意义，并批判性评估了关系性纲领在量子引力研究中的相关性。

Abstract: In Newtonian spacetime, the canonical description of a classical $N$-particle system requires $3N$ degrees of freedom. Not all of these are physical, however, since the conservation of the net momentum implies that only $3(N-1)$ accelerations are independent. Hence, three constraints can be used to eliminate the unphysical centre-of-mass variables, at the level of the Lagrangian, leaving only the subset of observable displacements and momenta, which are relational. Imposing the constraints does not change the dynamics of these variables, at the classical level, and is analogous to a gauge-fixing procedure, which removes redundancy in the description of the system. In classical physics, therefore, the number of physical degrees of freedom equals the number of independent relational degrees of freedom. Here, we show that this is not the case in quantum mechanics. While an operator-analogue of the classical net momentum exists, it cannot be used to impose constraints that restrict the degrees of freedom in the theory, without a loss of physical information. This means that all $3N$ canonical degrees of freedom are physical, even though only $3(N-1)$ of them are relational. We explore the physical consequences of the non-relational variables and show that they give rise to generalised uncertainty relations (GURs), for the relational quantities that define the quantum reference frame (QRF). Hence, it is shown that the non-relational degrees of freedom refer to the frame itself and that the non-Heisenberg terms in the GURs define its Galilean-invariant spreads, in both real space and momentum space. The implications of this result for recent work on relational models, including the ``perspective neutral'' framework for QRFs, are discussed. Its implications for the wider relational program, and, in particular, the relevance of the latter to quantum gravity research, are also critically assessed

</details>


### [19] [Quantum Gravity Simulation: Quantum simulation with a minimum length based on the generalised uncertainty principle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19602)
*Jack Keable-Elliott,David J. Bacon,Andrew Burbanks,Jaewoo Joo*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种在第一次量子化（first quantisation）框架下，利用L个量子比特（qubits）模拟一维量子系统低能与高能态的通用方法。从有限差分法中的最小网格间距ΔL出发，解析推导出广义不确定性原理（GUP），并揭示其在低能与高能区域的不同性质；进一步导出高能动量表达式，探讨其与狭义相对论动量及海森堡不确定性原理（HUP）的兼容性问题，为利用量子模拟工具研究高能量子引力现象提供了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子模拟中，如何有效覆盖从低能到高能的不同能量区间，并且将离散网格带来的有限分辨率效应纳入量子力学基本原理（如不确定性原理）的修正中，是当前研究的关键问题。作者旨在建立一个系统的理论框架，以衔接量子模拟（有限网格）与量子引力理论（最小长度、修正色散关系）之间的鸿沟。

Method: 采用第一次量子化框架，以L个量子比特编码一维量子系统；利用有限差分法（finite-difference method）设定最小网格间距ΔL；从该离散化假设出发，解析推导出广义不确定性原理（GUP）；基于平均动量的大小，对GUP在低能与高能区域进行分区域分析；在高能区域，进一步导出新的动量表达式，并检验其与海森堡不确定性原理（HUP）及狭义相对论动量的一致性。

Result: 低能区域下，当ΔL ≪ ħ时，GUP退化为标准海森堡不确定性原理（HUP）；当ΔL ≠ 0时，GUP数学上给出三个不同区域，且波函数可能因网格分辨率不足而在有限动量不确定性下呈现单点局域化（single-point localisation）。高能区域：若放松HUP并使高能动量匹配狭义相对论动量，则GUP预言存在一个具有非零质量的最小长度（minimum length），且该结果在连续极限ΔL = 0下依然成立；若强制要求与HUP一致，则可恢复无最小长度的标准高能表示，但该要求与狭义相对论动量不兼容，需引入修正的能量-动量关系（modified energy-momentum equation）。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一种从有限网格量子模拟出发、统一描述低能与高能量子系统的新理论配方。所提出的动量公式为利用量子模拟工具（quantum simulation tools）探索高能量子引力（quantum gravity）现象（如最小长度、修正色散关系）提供了可行途径。

Abstract: We present a recipe for simulating one-dimensional quantum systems for low and high energies with $L$ qubits within the framework of first quantisation. Assuming a minimum grid spacing $ΔL$ in the finite-difference method, the generalised uncertainty principle (GUP) is derived analytically and shows distinct properties for low- and high-energy quantum systems. In the low-energy regime, the GUP approaches to the standard Heisenberg uncertainty principle (HUP) for $ ΔL \ll \hbar$. However, for finite $ΔL \neq 0$, the GUP mathematically provides three different regions dependent on the average momentum and suggests that a wavefunction can exhibit a single-point localisation at the finite momentum uncertainty due to lack of grid resolution. We then derive a new expression for the high-energy momentum and focus on two specific cases relevant to relativistic aspects. First, if the HUP is relaxed and the high-energy momentum is matched to the special-relativistic one, the resulting GUP predicts the existence of a minimum length with non-zero mass for high energy despite the continuous limit $ΔL = 0$. Second, enforcing consistency with the HUP allows the recovery of a canonical high-energy representation with no minimum length. But this requirement brings incompatibility with the special-relativistic momentum and suggests a modified energy-momentum equation. Therefore, we believe that the proposed momentum formulation provides a novel pathway to investigate quantum gravity phenomena for high energy using quantum simulation tools.

</details>


### [20] [Quantum resonance-enhanced performance of quantum battery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19477)
*Ankita Mazumdar,Shashi C. L. Srivastava,Sanku Paul*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文证明了量子共振（quantum resonance）可作为量子电池（quantum batteries）的强大资源，在共振条件下充电功率随时间线性增长，且提取效率接近单位一，该增强效应在高阶共振中依然存在，并在相互作用型 kicked top 模型中验证了其普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已知量子共振在系统本征频率与驱动频率之比为有理数时出现，能产生超线性纠缠、增强输运、量子计量性能与通信，但其在量子电池中的潜力尚未被探索。本研究旨在验证量子共振是否可作为量子电池的有效充电资源。

Method: 将量子电池建模为自由转子（free rotors），通过踢动协议（kicked protocol）进行充电。分别在单个电池处于共振条件时，从解析和数值两个层面分析充电功率与效率；同时考察高阶共振（higher-order resonances）的表现，并在相互作用型 kicked top 模型中验证该机制的普适性。

Result: 共振条件下，充电功率随时间线性增长，存储能量的可提取效率（efficiency）接近单位一，尽管此时存在强纠缠生成。该增强性能在高阶共振中依然保持。在与相互作用型 kicked top 模型的对比中，类似的性能提升也被观察到。

Conclusion: 共振充电机制对储能、量子计算资源（quantum computational resources）和量子热力学（quantum thermodynamics）具有重要启示，且具有实验实现可行性。

Abstract: Quantum resonance arising whenever the ratio of the intrinsic system frequency to the driving frequency becomes a rational number has been demonstrated to generate super-linear entanglement, enhance transport, quantum metrology performance and communication. Here, we demonstrate that quantum resonance can also serve as a powerful resource for quantum batteries. We model the batteries as free rotors charged via a kicked protocol. When the individual batteries are at resonance, we show both analytically and numerically that charging power increases linearly with time while efficiency (defined as the fraction of stored energy that can be extracted) remains near unity despite strong entanglement generation. Furthermore, we demonstrate that this enhanced performance persists at higher-order resonances. Demonstrating the universality of this mechanism, we show that similar enhancements arise in the interacting kicked top model, and briefly note the feasibility of its experimental realization. In a broader context, resonant charging holds significant implications for energy storage, quantum computational resources, and quantum thermodynamics.

</details>


### [21] [High-purity entanglement mediated by magnons despite weak coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19533)
*Sanchar Sharma*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通过共享磁振子总线（magnonic bus）纠缠远距离自旋的新协议，打破了传统中自旋-磁振子耦合强度与纠缠保真度（fidelity）之间的权衡：弱耦合不会降低保真度，仅降低成功概率。基于氮-空位（NV）色心与磁线系统的模拟表明，在无退相干时可达单位保真度，在有限退相干下仍可达到高保真度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方案中，通过共享磁振子总线纠缠远距离自旋面临一个权衡（tradeoff）：更强的自旋-磁振子耦合虽能提高纠缠保真度，但同时也会增大自旋的衰减率（decay rate）。本文旨在打破这一固有权衡。

Method: 提出一种概率性（probabilistic）协议，其中磁振子仅耦合到计算基（computational basis）之外的一个跃迁，在该跃迁上生成贝尔态（Bell state）。分析两种氮-空位（NV）色心靠近磁线的设置，并采用蒙特卡洛波函数方法（Monte-Carlo wavefunction approach）进行模拟。

Result: 在无NV退相位（dephasing）时，协议可在任意弱耦合下达到与最大纠缠态对应的单位保真度（unit fidelity）。NV-磁振子耦合取为磁振子线宽（linewidth）的三分之一时，考虑有限NV退相位，在先进退相干率下保真度>0.99，在中等退相干率下最优保真度为0.91，两者的成功概率均为0.6%。

Conclusion: 该协议有效解耦了纠缠保真度与耦合强度的依赖关系，弱耦合仅降低成功概率而不牺牲保真度，为实验实现高保真远程纠缠提供了一条可行路径。

Abstract: Entangling distant spins via a shared magnonic bus typically faces a tradeoff: stronger spin-magnon coupling increases the entanglement fidelity, but also the spin decay rate. We propose a protocol that breaks this tradeoff. The magnons couple only to a transition outside the computational basis, in which the Bell state is created. Our protocol is probabilistic, and weak coupling reduces the success probability but not the fidelity. We analyze a setup where the spins are two nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centers near a magnetic wire. In the absence of NV dephasing, the protocol reaches unit fidelity with a maximally entangled state, for arbitrarily weak coupling. In our simulations via the Monte-Carlo wavefunction approach, the NV-magnon coupling is taken to be one-third of the magnon linewidth. Considering finite NV dephasing, we predict a fidelity of >0.99 for a state-of-the-art rate, and an optimal fidelity of 0.91 for a moderate rate, both at 0.6% success probability.

</details>


### [22] [Structured-light-mediated hybrid entanglement between photon polarization and electronic orbital angular momentum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19715)
*Hiroaki Saito,Nobuhiko Yokoshi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种最小量子光学方案，在半导体量子盘中产生光子偏振与电子轨道角动量之间的混合纠缠（hybrid entanglement）。通过自旋-轨道结构化的双光子态激发两个通道，并利用主方程分析证明，在理想相干极限下，基于单光子条件的事件触发态可逼近目标纠缠态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的量子纠缠方案多集中于光子之间或固态量子比特之间，而光子与电子自由度之间的混合纠缠，特别是涉及轨道角动量（orbital angular momentum, OAM）的纠缠，尚未有简洁有效的实现方案。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 方案基于一个半导体量子盘（semiconductor quantum disk），采用自旋-轨道结构化的双光子态激发两个通道：一个辐射复合的零轨道角动量通道，以及一个存储电子轨道量子比特（qubit）的有限轨道角动量通道。通过有效的相干映射（coherent mapping）制备一个双激发态，随后发射一个光子，其偏振与残留的电子轨道态形成纠缠。采用主方程分析（master-equation analysis）来评估方案性能。

Result: 主方程分析表明，在理想相干极限下，以选定输出模的单光子占据为条件的事件触发态（heralded state）可以趋近目标纠缠态。文章还讨论了轨道弛豫（orbital relaxation）、支路依赖的库仑移位（Coulomb shifts）的微扰有效性条件、轨道角动量混合（OAM mixing）以及有限轨道角动量辐射泄漏（radiative leakage）等效应。

Conclusion: 该原理验证模型表明，在半导体纳米结构中，通过结构化光（structured light）可以实现光子-电子混合纠缠，为发展新型混合量子信息处理平台提供了可行路径。

Abstract: We propose a minimal quantum-optical scheme for generating hybrid entanglement between photon polarization and electronic orbital angular momentum in a semiconductor quantum disk. A spin--orbit structured two-photon state excites two channels in the same disk: a radiatively recombining zero-orbital-angular-momentum channel and a finite-orbital-angular-momentum channel that stores the electronic orbital qubit. An effective coherent mapping prepares a selected two-excitation state, followed by emission of a photon whose polarization is entangled with the residual electronic orbital state. A master-equation analysis shows that the heralded state conditioned on single-photon occupation of the selected output mode approaches the target entangled state in the ideal coherent limit. We also discuss orbital relaxation and perturbative validity conditions for branch-dependent Coulomb shifts, orbital-angular-momentum mixing, and finite-orbital-angular-momentum radiative leakage. This proof-of-principle effective model suggests a route toward structured-light-mediated photon--electron hybrid entanglement in semiconductor nanostructures.

</details>


### [23] [Coupling phase interference effects in a multimode cavity magnonics system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20234)
*M. Avicena,G. Bourcin,V. Vlaminck,J. Bourhill,V. Castel*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文揭示了腔体磁子学（cavity magnonics）中耦合相位（coupling phase）在多功能系统中的决定性作用，通过引入同时考虑内部与外部耦合相位的输入-输出模型（input-output model），实验与理论一致地观察到由干涉效应引起的位置依赖的未耦合模式以及反共振频率处的强非互易性（nonreciprocity），从而确立耦合相位工程（coupling-phase engineering）作为设计和建模多模腔体磁子器件的核心原理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在腔体磁子学中，耦合相位对系统行为具有决定性影响，但在复杂的多模系统中常常被忽视。本文旨在系统研究相位介导的干涉效应，并阐明其在多模腔体磁子系统中的物理机制。

Method: 采用一个明确考虑内部（腔光子-磁子）耦合相位与外部（腔光子-探针）耦合相位的输入-输出模型，并与四柱重入式微波腔（four-post re-entrant microwave cavity）与钇铁石榴石（YIG）球体耦合的实验微波透射测量结果进行对比验证。

Result: 发现由于腔光子-磁子内部耦合相位的干涉，会产生一种依赖于位置的非耦合模式（uncoupled mode）；实验观察到在反共振频率（antiresonance frequencies）处存在显著的强非互易性，并证明这一特征源于远失谐模式（far-detuned modes）的奇宇称腔光子-探针外部耦合相位与内部耦合相位的干涉。

Conclusion: 通过融合理论、模拟与实验，本文证明耦合相位工程是精确建模与设计多模腔体磁子器件的关键原则，为相关器件的优化设计提供了新的理论指导。

Abstract: Coupling phases play a decisive yet often overlooked role in cavity magnonics, particularly in complex multimode systems. Here, we investigate phase-mediated interference effects in a cavity magnonics system comprising a four-post re-entrant microwave cavity coupled to Yttrium Iron Garnet (YIG) spheres. Using an input-output model that explicitly accounts for both internal and external coupling phases, we achieve agreement with experimental microwave transmission measurements. Our results unravel the emergence of a positionally-dependent uncoupled mode due to interference of cavity photon-magnon (internal) coupling phases. Further, we experimentally observed large nonreciprocity at the antiresonance frequencies and show that this feature arises due to the far-detuned modes' odd parity cavity photon-probe (external) coupling phase interfering with the internal coupling phases. Bridging theory, simulation and experiment, these results establish coupling-phase engineering as a key principle for accurately modeling and designing multimode cavity magnonics devices.

</details>

### [24] [The quantum loop algebra of $sl_2$ and $q$-Racah type bivariate functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20043)
*Pascal Baseilhac,Nicolas Crampe*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文基于量子环代数 $\mathcal{L} U_q sl_2$ 的表示理论，建立了一个统一的代数框架来描述两类六参数双变量 $q$-Racah 型函数，并将其解释为张量积表示中不同本征基之间的重叠系数，同时揭示其与 tridiagonal 对和因子化 Leonard 对的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双变量 $q$-Racah 型函数存在两种不同的六参数族，但缺乏统一的代数描述。本文旨在利用量子环代数 $\mathcal{L} U_q sl_2$ 的表示理论，为这两类函数提供一个统一的代数框架。

Method: 从 $\mathcal{L} U_q sl_2$ 的两个左/右余理想子代数（left and right coideal subalgebras）出发，在 $\mathcal{L} U_q sl_2 \otimes \mathcal{L} U_q sl_2$ 中构造八个依赖于两个标量 $a,b \in {\mathbb C}^*$ 的元素，进而生成六个交换子代数（commutative subalgebras）。这些元素在有限维向量空间上可对角化，双变量 $q$-Racah 型函数被解释为张量积（evaluation）表示中六种由 $a,b$ 参数化的“ distinguished”本征基之间的重叠系数。

Result: 在 $a,b,u_1,u_2$ 满足特定条件时，部分元素对表现为 I 型 tridiagonal 对（tridiagonal pairs of type I），也称为 $q$-Racah 型。当 $u_1/u_2=1$ 时，另一部分元素对被推测为因子化 Leonard 对（factorized Leonard pairs）。两种情形下均获得了不同本征基之间的重叠系数，并讨论了其与 Tratnik 型双变量多项式及 rank 2 Askey-Wilson 代数的关系。

Conclusion: 本文成功构建了一个统一的代数框架，将两类六参数双变量 $q$-Racah 型函数纳入量子环代数的表示理论之中，建立了其与 tridiagonal 对和 Leonard 对的联系，并揭示了与已知双变量正交多项式及高阶 Askey-Wilson 代数的关联。

Abstract: A unified algebraic framework for two different six-parameter families of bivariate $q$-Racah type functions is given using the representation theory of the quantum loop algebra $\mathcal{L} U_q sl_2$ of $sl_2$. The starting point of the analysis is two left and right coideal subalgebras of $\mathcal{L} U_q sl_2$ and six commutative subalgebras, built from eight elements in $\mathcal{L} U_q sl_2 \otimes \mathcal{L} U_q sl_2$. The eight elements depend on two scalars $a,b \in {\mathbb C}^*$, and are diagonalized on a finite-dimensional vector space. The bivariate $q$-Racah type functions are interpreted as the overlap coefficients relating six `distinguished' eigenbases parametrized by $a,b$ of the tensor product (evaluation) representations of $\mathcal{L} U_q sl_2$ labeled by the evaluation parameters $u_1,u_2$. Upon certain conditions on $a,b,u_1,u_2$, it is shown that a subset of pairs of elements act as tridiagonal pairs of type I (also called $q$-Racah type). For $u_1/u_2=1$, another subset of pairs of elements are conjectured to act as factorized Leonard pairs. Thus, in both cases corresponding overlap coefficients relating the various eigenbases associated with different pairs are obtained. Some of their properties are also discussed, as well as their relation with known bivariate polynomials of Tratnik type and the rank 2 Askey--Wilson algebra.

</details>

### [25] [Scattering Dynamics and Chaotic Motions in a Relativistic Two-Centre Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20099)
*Stefano Baranzini,Gian Marco Canneori*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文研究了固定能量下平面相对论性双中心问题（relativistic two-centre problem），包含对开普勒势（Keplerian potential）的一类微扰。通过时间重参数化，相对论动力学等价于一个带有临界强力奇点（critical strong-force singularities）的经典双中心系统，进而应用基于莫培督泛函（Maupertuis functional）的变分方法，构建了具有指定符号路径（prescribed symbolic itineraries）的无碰撞相对论轨迹，并通过对动力学进行可允许序列（admissible sequences）编码，证明了有界轨道、具有指定渐进方向的散射解以及在一个时间方向上渐进自由、另一方向上具有指定符号行为的有界轨迹的存在性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将相对论性双中心问题约化为带有临界强力奇点的经典双中心系统，从而利用经典变分方法处理相对论动力学中轨迹的全局存在性与分类问题。

Method: 通过时间重参数化将相对论动力学等价地转化为经典双中心系统；基于莫培督泛函（Maupertuis functional）应用变分方法。

Result: 构建了具有指定符号路径的无碰撞相对论轨迹；获得了由可允许序列（admissible sequences）对动力学进行编码的结果；证明了有界轨道、具有指定渐进方向的散射解以及单向渐进自由的有界轨迹的存在性。

Conclusion: 相对论性双中心问题的动力学可以通过符号动力学（symbolic dynamics）进行系统性编码，并存在多种类型的轨道（有界、散射及混合行为轨迹）。

Abstract: We study the planar relativistic two-centre problem at fixed energy, including a class of perturbations of the Keplerian potential. Up to a reparametrisation of time, the relativistic dynamics is equivalent to a classical two-centre system with critical strong-force singularities. This reduction allows us to apply variational methods based on the Maupertuis functional. We construct collision-free relativistic trajectories with prescribed symbolic itineraries and obtain a coding of the dynamics by admissible sequences. In particular, we prove the existence of bounded orbits, scattering solutions with prescribed asymptotic directions, and trapped trajectories that are asymptotically free in one time direction and exhibit prescribed symbolic behaviour in the other.

### [26] [Null distance on cosmological spacetimes and monotone convergence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20063)
*Miguel Prados-Abad,Omar Zoghlami*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究具有紧致空间切片的宇宙学时空中Gromov-Hausdorff型收敛性，利用零距离（null distance）作为工具，在适当的紧化条件和单调序列假设下建立了时空度量收敛与极限度量张量的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Sakovich与Sormani近期开创了利用零距离研究时空的Gromov-Hausdorff型收敛的纲领，本文旨在将该理论应用于具有紧致切片的宇宙学时空（cosmological spacetimes with compact slices），即形如$(a,b)\times M$、配备度量$-dt^2+h_t$的时空，以建立此类时空在适当条件下的收敛理论。

Method: 首先假设度量族$h_t$具备温和的延拓性质（mild extension properties），证明此类时空是因果-零可紧化（causally-null compactifiable）且未来发展的（future developed）。随后研究具有空间直径一致上界的单调序列，获得零距离的一致收敛（uniform convergence）以及相关时间度量空间（timed metric spaces）在未来发展Gromov-Hausdorff意义下的收敛。最后证明满足温和因果可达性条件（causal accessibility condition）的因果-零可紧化时空是因果-零的（causally-null），并建立极限距离诱导的因果-零距离与（可能非光滑的）极限度量张量诱导的零距离之间的关系。

Result: 在所述假设下，得到了零距离的一致收敛性以及时间度量空间在未来发展Gromov-Hausdorff意义下的收敛性；建立了因果-零可紧化时空的因果-零性质与极限距离-极限度量张量之间的对应关系。

Conclusion: 本文为宇宙学时空中Gromov-Hausdorff型收敛提供了理论基础，并给出了实例说明所提假设的必要性。

Abstract: The metric theory of spacetimes studies Lorentzian manifolds using tools of metric geometry. This is achieved via the null distance, which is a definite distance constructed from a time function on a spacetime. This enables the study of Gromov-Hausdorff-type convergence of spacetimes, a program recently initiated by Sakovich and Sormani. In this paper we study such notions of convergence for cosmological spacetimes with compact slices, i.e., $(a,b)\times M$ endowed with a Lorentzian metric $-dt^2+h_t$, where $h_t$ is a family of Riemannian metrics on the compact manifold $M$. Assuming mild extension properties of $h_t$, we first establish that these spacetimes are causally-null compactifiable and future developed. We then study monotone sequences with a uniform upper bound on the spatial diameter, obtaining uniform convergence of the null distances, as well as convergence of the associated timed metric spaces in the future developed Gromov-Hausdorff sense. Finally, we prove that causally-null compactifiable spacetimes satisfying a mild causal accessibility condition are causally-null, and relate the causally-null distance induced by the limit distance with the null distance induced by the (possibly non-smooth) limit metric tensor. Examples are provided to motivate the necessity of our hypotheses.

### [27] [Quantum Simulation of Semiconductor Excitons in Ultracold Dipolar Fermi Gases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19467)
*Florian Hirsch,Oriana K. Diessel,Rafał Ołdziejewski,Richard Schmidt*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出在六角光学晶格中的超冷原子体系中实现半导体激子（excitons）的量子模拟，涵盖从弱耦合到强相互作用的完整区间，并给出了实验观测与波函数测量的可行方案，为模拟更复杂的电子态（如三子、极化子、激子绝缘体）奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从原子薄层过渡金属二硫族化物（TMD）半导体中激子物理学的研究进展中获得启发，探索在冷原子体系中构建类似于激子的准粒子态。

Method: 考虑由超冷基态分子或偶极原子构成的单组分费米子（single-component fermions）装载于六角光学晶格（hexagonal optical lattice）中。通过引入三角子晶格之间的能量偏移打开能隙，在 K/K' 点产生简并，形成与 TMD 相似的能带结构。

Result: 预言了冷原子激子（cold atomic excitons）的存在，指出冷原子体系能够从弱耦合（有效质量模型适用）到强相互作用（平带模型描述）的全范围内研究激子。展示了如何通过晶格调制光谱学（lattice modulation spectroscopy）观测这些激子，以及如何利用量子气体显微镜（quantum gas microscopy）描绘其波函数。

Conclusion: 牢固确立了半导体物理学的量子模拟（quantum simulation）这一思想，为模拟三子（trions）、极化子（polarons）和激子绝缘体（excitonic insulators）等复杂电子态奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: Inspired by the progress on the study of exciton physics in atomically thin transition metal dichalcogenide (TMD) semiconductors, we investigate the formation of analogs of excitons in cold atomic systems. To this end, we consider single-component fermions comprised of ultracold ground-state molecules or dipolar atoms in a hexagonal optical lattice. An energy offset between triangular sublattices opens up a band gap with degeneracies at the K/K' points as in TMDs. We predict the existence of cold atomic excitons and show that cold atoms allow us to study excitons from the weak-coupling regime, where effective mass models apply, to the strong-interaction regime, described by flat-band models. We demonstrate how these excitons can be observed using lattice modulation spectroscopy, and how their wave functions can be mapped out using quantum gas microscopy. Firmly establishing the idea of quantum simulation of semiconductor physics, this work lays the foundation for simulating complex electronic states such as trions, polarons and excitonic insulators.

### [28] [Real-time probing of quadrupolar contributions to the absorption cross section of non-periodic systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19828)
*Anvar Khujakulov,Michele Guerrini,Carlo Andrea Rozzi,Caterina Cocchi*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本论文以氢原子为基准，通过实时映射瞬时电场梯度驱动的四极相互作用，对多极截面进行非微扰评估，并分析了均匀场与纯空间梯度两种相互作用机制下的四极响应，为近场区分子与纳米结构的非微扰多极模拟奠定了理论与计算基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在纳米尺度环境中，传统的偶极近似（dipole approximation）失效，需要非微扰（non-perturbative）地评估多极截面（multipolar cross sections），以探测原子和分子对空间非均匀电场的响应。

Method: 以氢原子作为解析与数值基准，实时映射由瞬时电场梯度驱动的四极相互作用（quadrupole interactions），探索均匀场和纯空间梯度两种相互作用机制下的系统动力学。

Result: 均匀场下，四极响应通过多步偶极跃迁（multi-step dipole transitions）激活，产生亚1 eV的激发态吸收；纯空间梯度下，弱场响应以12.1 eV处的单光子1s→3d四极共振（quadrupole resonance）为主，强梯度则通过瞬态驱动的相干布居诱导低能受激发射（stimulated emission）。

Conclusion: 该动态分析结合了四极响应与外电场对称性的严格评估，为未来近场区（near-field regime）分子与纳米结构的非微扰多极模拟建立了理论与计算基础。

Abstract: The non-perturbative evaluation of multipolar cross sections is essential for probing atomic and molecular responses to spatially inhomogeneous electric fields characteristic of nanoscale environments where the conventional dipole approximation breaks down. Taking the hydrogen atom as an analytical and numerical benchmark, we map in real time quadrupole interactions driven by instantaneous electric field gradients. Our study explores two distinct interaction regimes. Under a uniform field, quadrupolar responses are activated by multi-step dipole transitions, responsible for sub-1~eV excited-state absorption. Conversely, under pure spatial gradients, the weak-field response is dominated by the single-photon $1s \to 3d$ quadrupole resonance at 12.1~eV, while strong gradients induce low-energy stimulated emission via transiently driven coherent populations. This dynamical analysis is complemented by a rigorous evaluation of the symmetry aspects of the quadrupole response and the applied electric field. This methodology establishes the theoretical and computational foundation for future non-perturbative multipole simulations of molecules and nanostructures in the near-field regime.

### [29] [Emergence of giant vortices under nonlinear rotation with attractive interactions in a toroidal condensate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19840)
*Rony Boral,Swarup K. Sarkar,Matthew Edmonds,Paulsamy Muruganandam,Pankaj Kumar Mishra*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过数值方法研究环形阱中玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）在密度依赖规范势（density-dependent gauge potential）诱导的非线性旋转下的效应，发现非线性旋转增强会导致涡旋晶格（vortex lattice）从环形结构转变为巨涡旋态（giant vortex state），并分析了该转变对量子环流、托马斯-费米密度廓线（Thomas-Fermi density profile）、集体激发谱（collective excitation spectrum）及多量子化涡旋稳定性的影响。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用数值模拟方法研究密度依赖规范势（density-dependent gauge potential）的作用；基于Bogoliubov-de Gennes分析考察集体激发谱（collective excitation spectrum）；通过流体力学分析（hydrodynamic analysis）进一步验证结果；并系统地映射参数空间以确定托马斯-费米近似（Thomas-Fermi approximation）的适用范围。

Result: 非线性旋转强度增大会导致环形涡旋晶格向巨涡旋态（giant vortex state）的结构转变；巨涡旋的量子环流（quantum circulation）对非线性旋转强度高度敏感，且该态出现在负化学势（negative chemical potential）区域；观测到Kohn定理（Kohn theorem）的违反及呼吸模式频率（breathing mode frequency）的变化，表明凝聚体发生径向形变；非线性旋转可增强多量子化涡旋的全局稳定性但未必保证其局部稳定性。

Conclusion: 非线性旋转是调控环形玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中涡旋结构的关键参数，可诱导拓扑转变并显著改变凝聚体的动力学性质与激发谱特征，为理解超流涡旋态（superfluid vortex states）的稳定性和操控提供了新途径。

Abstract: We numerically investigate the effects of a density-dependent gauge potential which induces nonlinear rotation on a Bose-Einstein condensate confined in a toroidal trapping geometry. By focusing on the resulting vortex lattice configurations, we demonstrate that increasing the strength of the nonlinear rotation leads to a structural transition from a ring-shaped vortex lattice to a giant vortex state. The quantum circulation associated with the giant vortex is found to be highly sensitive to the strength of the nonlinear rotation and the giant vortex appears in the regime of negative chemical potential. Additionally, we identify the parameter regime in which the Thomas-Fermi density profile remains valid by mapping the solution space based on the strength of the nonlinear rotation and the radius of the confining potential. Based on the Bogoliubov de Gennes analysis, we investigate the impact of nonlinear rotation on the collective excitation spectrum. Our results reveal a violation of the Kohn theorem, accompanied by changes in the breathing mode frequency that indicate radial deformation of the condensate. Our findings are further substantiated through a comprehensive hydrodynamic analysis. Finally, we analyze the stability of multiply quantized vortices under nonlinear rotation. Our findings indicate that while nonlinear rotation can enhance the global stability of these states, it does not necessarily ensure their local stability.

</details>


### [30] [A framework for separating dephasing from decoherence in matter-wave Bell interferometers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19984)
*S. Kannan,Y. S. Athreya,X. T. Yan,S. S. Hodgman,A. G. Truscott*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于Schwinger SU(2)映射的框架，用于分离物质波贝尔干涉仪（matter-wave Bell interferometer）中贝尔关联幅度（Bell-correlation amplitude）降低的三个来源（几何退相位、环境退相干和技术稀释），并证明通过零光程差测量可提取与源分布无关的幅度降低，进而为双种类贝尔干涉仪探测质量依赖退相干（mass-dependent decoherence）提供定量界标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物质波贝尔干涉仪能够灵敏地探测纠缠量子系统中质量依赖的退相干效应。然而，为了可靠地解释观测到的贝尔关联幅度降低，需要区分几何退相位（geometric dephasing）、环境退相干（environmental decoherence）以及源与探测统计带来的技术稀释（technical dilution）这三个因素。

Method: 基于Schwinger SU(2)映射（Schwinger SU(2) mapping）构建理论框架，将贝尔关联幅度降低的贡献分别归因于局部幺正演化（local unitaries）或耗散通道（dissipative channels）。通过在零干涉仪光程差处评价贝尔关联，提取与源分布无关的幅度降低。

Result: 在现有灵敏度下，不同质量原子间的已知差分退相干通道（differential decoherence channels）可忽略不计。该框架给出了一个具体界标，超过此界标时双种类贝尔干涉仪将开始指示超出已知系统学的差分退相干。

Conclusion: 该工作为利用双种类贝尔干涉仪探测质量依赖退相干等新物理机制铺平了道路。

Abstract: Matter-wave Bell interferometers provide a sensitive probe of mass-dependent decoherence in entangled quantum systems. The degree of entanglement is obtained from the Bell-correlation amplitude of this interferometer. For observing potential mass-dependent decoherence, a reliable interpretation of any observed reduction in the Bell correlation amplitude is required, which depends on three factors: geometric dephasing, environmental decoherence, and technical dilution from source and detection statistics. In this work, we present a framework based on the Schwinger SU(2) mapping to separate these contributions into local unitaries or dissipative channels. We show that by evaluating the Bell correlation at zero interferometer path difference, it is possible to extract a source-distribution-independent Bell correlation amplitude reduction. When this framework is extended to involve atoms of different mass, we show that the known differential decoherence channels are negligible at current sensitivity. This yields a concrete bound at which a dual-species Bell interferometer would begin to signal differential decoherence beyond the known systematics, opening the way for such systems to probe new physics, such as mass-dependent decoherence mechanisms.

</details>


### [31] [Two- and three-body bound states in one-dimensional Fermi bipolaron with three-body interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20075)

### [32] [Fermionic pairs, from the surface to the bulk](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20412)
*Sandra Brandstetter,Carl Heintze,Fabian Brauneis,Stephanie M. Reimann,Georg Bruun,Maciej Gałka,Selim Jochim*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该论文通过高分辨率成像技术，在有限、可调控的费米子少体体系中直接观测到了配对关联（pair correlations）的实空间分布，揭示了约束效应和壳层结构如何重新组织配对行为：弱相互作用、约束主导的闭壳层体系中，高温区抑制关联，配对主要出现在低密度表面；开壳层体系则支持更强的中心配对。随着相互作用或粒子数增加，体系中心逐渐恢复类似大块体系的库珀对（Cooper pair）轮廓，而边缘区域仍维持类似紧束缚二聚体（dimer）的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在有限体系（如原子核、超导颗粒、量子点）中，费米子配对与约束效应、壳层填充和空间不均匀性相互竞争，使得配对微观结构难以直接获取。该研究旨在通过可调控的少体费米子体系，以单粒子分辨和全计数统计方法直接成像配对的实空间结构。

Method: 构建了一个有限、可调控的少体费米原子体系，采用单粒子分辨（single-particle resolution）和全计数统计（full counting statistics）技术，对配对关联进行实空间成像。

Result: 约束和壳层结构在实空间中重新组织配对：弱相互作用的约束主导区，闭壳层构型抑制高密度中心的关联，配对主要出现在低密度表面；开壳层体系则呈现更强的中心配对。即使体系很小，增加相互作用或粒子数都能使中心区域恢复类似大块体系的库珀对轮廓，而边缘区域仍保持二聚体状关联。

Conclusion: 该测量提供了有限费米子体系中配对形成的微观视角，揭示了配对位置及其从局域二聚体到重叠库珀对的特性转变，从而将介观冷原子物理与原子核及超导纳米结构中的配对现象联系起来。

Abstract: Fermion pairing underlies collective quantum phenomena across widely different forms of matter. In extended systems such as ultracold Fermi gases, pairing is commonly understood through the BCS--BEC crossover, where the pair size evolves from large, overlapping Cooper pairs to tightly bound dimers. In finite systems such as atomic nuclei, superconducting grains and quantum dots, however, the same pairing tendency competes with confinement, shell filling and spatial inhomogeneity, making the microscopic structure of pairs much harder to access. Here, we image pair correlations in a finite, tunable system of few fermionic atoms with single-particle resolution and full counting statistics. We observe that confinement and shell structure re-organize pairing in real space: In the weakly interacting, confinement-dominated regime, closed-shell configurations suppress correlations in the high-density trap center. Pairing is mainly observed toward the low-density surface. Open-shell systems, however, support substantially stronger central pairing. Already for surprisingly small systems, increasing either interaction strength or particle number restores a locally bulk-like Cooper-pair profile in the trap center, whereas the edge retains dimer-like correlations. By resolving where pairs form and how their character changes from localized dimers to overlapping Cooper pairs, our measurements provide a microscopic view of pairing in finite fermionic matter and connect the physics of mesoscopic cold atoms to pairing phenomena in nuclei and superconducting nanostructures.

</details>

# cs.AI [[Back]](#toc)

### [33] [Reading and Steering Representations of Materials-Science Mechanisms in an Open-Weight Language Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20058)
*Markus J. Buehler*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究通过结合直接读出（direct readout）、雅可比读出（Jacobian readout）、无选项状态几何（option-free state geometry）、60条本构定律的反事实基准（counterfactual benchmark）及因果干预（causal intervention），系统验证了开放权重大语言模型 google/gemma-4-E4B-it 中材料科学机制信息存在的三种实验可分离形式：概念存在于单个隐藏状态（hidden state）、本构取向由状态间的受控变换承载、选定的内部表征因果性地控制工程答案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型能够回答科学问题，但正确的输出并不能揭示模型是否真正表征或使用了底层的物理规律。因此，需要设计实验方法来分离并验证模型内部是否存在可操作的物理机制信息。

Method: 结合匹配的直接读出与雅可比读出、无选项状态几何、包含60条本构定律的反事实基准以及因果干预手段。在50条保留的材料描述上，用三个独立拟合的雅可比透镜（Jacobian lens）复现概念排序；用两种读出的无目标词集实现10个机制家族中9个的盲识别。通过72条提示的基准测试获得机制特定的隐藏状态邻域，并对比同一提示中物理输入方向反转后隐藏状态的运动是否遵循本构定律。

Result: 60条冻结关系中，状态变换正确排序了直接、物理中性与逆向定律，并正确定向了40条有向定律中的39条，而词汇控制接近随机。双向干预在所有12个匹配案例中均使答案概率朝向或偏离物理正确结果，反事实状态补丁（counterfactual state patch）跨机制与答案格式传递了对立的决策信号。

Conclusion: 物理关系在受控的状态变化中比在绝对状态本身中更可见。模型内部确实存在可分离的机制信息形式：概念可读出、本构取向可通过状态变换承载、内部表征因果性地控制答案，但静态隐藏状态的组织也可能被简单的数值比较所解释。

Abstract: Large language models can answer scientific questions, yet a correct output does not reveal whether the model represents or uses the governing physics. Here we show that materials science mechanism information in the open-weight google/gemma-4-E4B-it model has three experimentally separable forms: concepts are readable in individual hidden states, constitutive orientation is carried by controlled transformations between states, and selected internal representations causally control engineering answers. We combine matched direct and Jacobian vocabulary readouts, option-free state geometry, a 60-law counterfactual benchmark and causal interventions. In 50 held-out materials descriptions, three independently fitted Jacobian lenses reproduced concept ranks, and target-free word sets from both readouts enabled blinded identification of 9 of 10 mechanism families. A separate 72-prompt benchmark produced mechanism-specific hidden-state neighborhoods, but an exact graph audit showed that this apparent physical organization was equally explained by numerical comparison. We therefore compared otherwise identical prompts in which only the direction of the physical input was reversed, asking whether the resulting hidden-state movement followed the supplied constitutive law. These state transformations ordered direct, physically neutral and inverse laws across 60 frozen relations and correctly oriented 39 of 40 directional laws, whereas lexical controls were near chance. Bidirectional interventions shifted answer probabilities toward or away from the physically appropriate outcome across all 12 matched cases, while counterfactual state patches transferred opposing decision signals across mechanisms and answer formats. Physical relationships were therefore more visible in controlled state changes than in absolute states alone.

</details>

### [34] [Sensing, Traffic, and Construction in Termites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19594)
*Yufei Xiao,Qinglin Wu,Kukhyun Lim,Nan-Yao Su,Paul Bardunias,Atanu Chatterjee,Saad Bhamla*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本文综合分析了白蚁（termites）在颗粒基质（granular substrate）中进行挖掘、运输和建造的多尺度反馈过程，涵盖触角尺度的接触、个体尺度的交通流到米级尺度的蚁巢结构，并提出了一个定量化的生命物理学（physics-of-life）框架来研究白蚁群体如何通过持续改造自身所处的介质来影响感知、移动和建造行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地下和筑丘白蚁在同一颗粒基质中进行挖掘、运输和建造，而该基质反过来又调节它们感知、移动和沉积材料的方式。本文旨在综合跨越触角尺度接触、个体尺度交通流和米级尺度建筑结构这三个相互关联的问题，并强调哪些方面已有实验证据、哪些方面证据不足或仅限于少数模式系统。

Method: 本文是一篇综述（review），通过综合已有的实验发现，并结合新兴的成像、追踪和建模工具，对白蚁行为中的多尺度反馈机制进行系统整合与分析。

Result: 在不同长度尺度上，噪声性的局部相互作用（noisy local interactions）通过共享的材料介质将感知、运输和建造耦合在一起，从而在群体尺度上产生涌现秩序（emergent order）。文中指出了已通过实验确证的发现，也明确了证据尚不充分或仅局限于少数模式系统的领域。

Conclusion: 本文的综述工作旨在推动建立一个定量化的生命物理学框架，用于研究白蚁群体如何持续改造它们赖以感知、移动和建造的介质。

Abstract: Subterranean and mound-building termites excavate, transport, and build within the same granular substrate that later regulates how they sense, move, and deposit material. From antennal-scale contacts through body-scale traffic to meter-scale architecture, this review synthesizes three linked problems: how workers sense local geometry and physical cues during search and excavation; how traffic moves through narrow, evolving conduits; and how excavation and deposition remodel the substrate that guides later behavior. Across these length scales, noisy local interactions couple sensing, transport, and construction through a shared material medium, leading to emergent order at the colony scale. We emphasize what is established experimentally, where evidence remains sparse or limited to a few model systems, and how emerging imaging, tracking, and modeling tools are making these feedbacks quantitatively accessible. We use this synthesis to motivate a quantitative physics-of-life framework for termite colonies that continually rewrite the medium through which they sense, move, and build.

</details>

### [35] [Nuclear Quantum Effects as a Denoising Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19680)
*Weizhou Wang,Jonathan Weare,Aaron R. Dinner*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，仅基于经典玻尔兹曼统计（classical Boltzmann statistics）训练的降噪器（denoiser），在采样时与一个解析高斯分量（analytic Gaussian component）组合，即可精确生成原子核的量子玻尔兹曼分布（quantum Boltzmann distribution），且该组合在温度、同位素质量、耗散强度及路径边界条件（boundary conditions）等所有量子上下文（quantum context）下具有不变性，无需重新训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虚时路径积分（imaginary-time path integrals）将量子玻尔兹曼分布映射为经典环聚合物（ring polymer），但现有模拟或训练模型将核质量、环境耦合及路径边界条件等量子上下文硬编码其中，而在路径测度中这些信息仅通过一个已知闭式的二次作用量（quadratic action）进入。作者希望利用这一结构实现跨量子上下文的精确迁移，无需重新训练。

Method: 构建一个生成模型（generative model），其中降噪器仅从经典玻尔兹曼统计中训练，而整个量子上下文由一个解析的、从目标系综（target ensemble）内禀量子不确定性（intrinsic quantum uncertainty）导出的高斯分量携带。两者在采样时组合，条件为训练噪声不超过该量子不确定性上界。

Result: 在理论上证明该组合对所有满足上界的量子上下文具有不变性；在数值实验中展示了跨温度、同位素质量、耗散强度以及路径边界条件的精确迁移，无需要重新训练；从开放虚时路径（open imaginary-time paths）中得到了标记原子核的端到端位移和动量分布；指出该不变性原则上可扩展至玻色子交换（bosonic exchange）的置换边界条件。

Conclusion: 生成建模（generative modeling）中的噪声与原子核的量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）本质上是同一个二次结构的两个面向。这意味着核量子效应的模拟可以解耦为经典训练与解析量子上下文的组合，大幅提升迁移效率与泛化能力。

Abstract: Nuclear quantum effects are rigorously captured by imaginary-time path integrals, which map the quantum Boltzmann distribution onto a ring polymer of classical replicas. Yet the nuclear masses, the coupling to the environment, and the boundary conditions of the path remain hard-wired in the simulation or the trained model, even though this quantum context enters the path measure only through a quadratic action known in closed form. Here we show that a denoiser trained on classical Boltzmann statistics alone, composed at sampling time with an analytic Gaussian component carrying the entire quantum context, yields the quantum Boltzmann distribution of the nuclei. Such a composition exists and is exact whenever the training noise does not exceed the intrinsic quantum uncertainty of the target ensemble, and it is invariant across all quantum contexts admitted by this bound. We show exact transfer across temperature, isotopic mass, dissipation strength, and the boundary conditions of the path in theory and in numerical experiments, without retraining. The last yields the end-to-end displacement and momentum distributions of a tagged nucleus from open imaginary-time paths. The same invariance extends in principle to the permuted boundary conditions of bosonic exchange, with the identical denoiser. In this view, the noise of generative modeling and the quantum fluctuations of the nuclei are two faces of the same quadratic structure.

</details>
