### [36] [A T-Fold Black Hole in Doubled Type IIB](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19443)
*Mir Faizal,Arshid Shabir*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在双场IIB型弦论（doubled type-IIB theory）中构造了一个渐近平坦的T-折叠（T-fold）表示，用于描述四维双荷黑洞（dyonic black hole）的电荷轨道。通过引入整体抛物线型T-对偶单值性（parabolic T-duality monodromy），非几何数据仅通过全局拼接（global patching）进入理论，而非依赖内部代数Q-流（Q-flux）。该构造保留了局域方程、BPS指数（BPS index）以及熵所对应的O(6,6)不变量（O(6,6)-invariant），并展示了极端近视界区域为局域AdS₂×S²几何，紧致因子具有全局T-对偶拼接结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在弦论（string theory）中，非几何背景（non-geometric backgrounds）是理解弦论对偶性（T-duality）推广的重要课题。本文旨在构建一个明确的可解例子，将四维双荷黑洞与非几何的T-折叠结构相联系起来，从而考察非几何数据如何通过全局整体性质影响黑洞解。

Method: 从环面种子解（toroidal seed）F1-P-NS5-KKM出发，对活跃的双重三维环面（doubled three-torus）施加一个积分抛物线型T-对偶单值性（integral parabolic T-duality monodromy）。非几何数据仅通过这一整体拼接方式进入体系，而非由单一的代数Q-流产生。

Result: 在双场Kaluza-Klein/winding局域系统中，Reissner-Nordström型（Reissner-Nordström-type）项由守恒的四维电场强度和磁场强度共同贡献，而非仅由内部代数Q-流提供。精确对偶性保留了局域运动方程、BPS指数以及熵相关的NS-NS/N=4电荷子格点上的O(6,6)不变量。最小Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton部分包含一个标量场演化分支和一个等电荷Reissner-Nordström极限；极端近视界区域局域为AdS₂×S²几何，其紧致因子具有全局T-对偶拼接结构。

Conclusion: 成功构造了一个渐近平坦的四维双荷黑洞T-折叠解，表明非几何整体结构可以与黑洞物理学自洽结合，并且对偶性在局域物理和不变量层面保持严格成立。这为研究非几何背景下的黑洞热力学和可观测效应提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We construct an asymptotically flat T-fold representative of a four-dimensional dyonic black-hole charge orbit in doubled type-IIB theory. Starting from the F1-P-NS5-KKM toroidal seed, an integral parabolic T-duality monodromy is imposed on an active doubled three-torus. The non-geometric data enter only through this global patching: the Reissner-Nordström-type term is sourced by conserved four-dimensional electric and magnetic field strengths in the doubled Kaluza-Klein/winding local system, not by an internal algebraic \(Q\)-flux alone. Exact duality preserves the local equations, the BPS index, and the \(O(6,6)\)-invariant of the NS-NS/\(N=4\) charge sublattice governing the entropy. The minimal Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton slice contains a running-scalar branch and an equal-charge Reissner-Nordström limit; the extremal near-horizon region is locally \(\mathrm{AdS}_2\times S^2\), with the compact factor globally T-duality patched.

</details>


### [37] [The Runkel-Watts string](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19462)
*Mattia Biancotto,Lorenz Eberhardt,Victor A. Rodriguez,Zi-Yue Wang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文引入并求解了一族新的二维弦理论，通过将刘维尔共形场论（Liouville CFT）与广义Runkel-Watts共形场论耦合得到。作者从复刘维尔弦（complex Liouville string）的适当极限推导出全亏格（all-genus）弦振幅公式，并建立了与矩阵积分（matrix integral）的对偶性。该理论可解释为耦合引力的二维SU(2)杨-米尔斯理论（2d SU(2) Yang-Mills theory），并与A系列极小弦（A-series minimal string）等构造直接相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索新的二维弦理论族，通过耦合刘维尔共形场论与广义Runkel-Watts共形场论来扩展弦理论构造的范畴，并揭示其与已有理论（如复刘维尔弦、极小弦、二维杨-米尔斯理论）之间的深层联系。

Method: 采用复刘维尔弦的适当极限方法，推导出全亏格弦振幅的闭合公式；通过建立与矩阵积分（matrix integral）的对偶性来验证理论的一致性。

Result: 获得了该新弦理论族在全亏格下的弦振幅解析表达式；证明了该理论与矩阵积分之间的对偶关系；揭示了该理论可等价地视为耦合引力的二维SU(2)杨-米尔斯理论。

Conclusion: 该新二维弦理论族不仅通过矩阵积分对偶实现了可解性，还统一了多个已有的弦理论构造（包括极小弦与二维杨-米尔斯-引力系统），为二维弦理论提供了更广泛的框架。

Abstract: We introduce and solve a new family of two-dimensional string theories obtained by coupling Liouville CFT to the generalized Runkel-Watts CFT. By taking an appropriate limit of the complex Liouville string, we derive an all-genus formula for its string amplitudes, and formulate a duality with a matrix integral. We explain that it can be interpreted as 2d SU(2) Yang-Mills theory coupled to gravity. We show that it also directly relates to other minimal string constructions such as the A-series minimal string.

</details>


### [38] [On the Origin of Toric Diagrams](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19460)
*Sebastián Franco,Diego Rodríguez-Gómez*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过引入一种为环面规范理论（toric gauge theory）中场的标度维数（scaling dimensions）赋值的方案，证明了当选定原点后，从模空间相干分支（coherent component）导出的希尔伯特级数（Hilbert series）与对偶多面体的埃尔哈特级数（Ehrhart series）精确匹配，从而为广义环面多边形（Generalized Toric Polygons, GTPs）与环面倾斜（brane tiling）之间的深层组合结构提供了证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 五维超共形场论（$5d$ SCFTs）可通过广义环面多边形（GTPs）编码，其中Hanany-Witten转变通过翻转$T$-锥（$T$-cones）赋予原点选择以物理意义；近期猜想指出适当分级的希尔伯特级数等于对偶多面体的埃尔哈特级数（Ehrhart series），且该级数在此类突变下保持不变，但需进一步验证和具体构造。

Method: 提出一种为与底层环面图（toric diagram）相关联的环面规范理论（toric gauge theory）中的场指定标度维数（scaling dimensions）的规则，并计算模空间相干分支（coherent component）的希尔伯特级数（Hilbert series）；通过多个非平凡例子验证该级数与选定原点后对偶多面体的埃尔哈特级数（Ehrhart series）之间的匹配关系，包括涉及多个原点选择导致不同GTPs和膜-网实现的情形。

Result: 构造的希尔伯特级数与对偶多面体的埃尔哈特级数在选定原点后精确匹配，并通过多个非平凡例子（包括多种可接受的原点选择）得到验证。

Conclusion: 普通膜倾斜（brane tiling）保留了关于广义环面多边形（GTPs）的非平凡信息，表明GTPs背后存在更深的组合结构。

Abstract: Five-dimensional superconformal field theories ($5d$ SCFTs) can be encoded by Generalized Toric Polygons (GTPs), where external legs of the dual $(p,q)$ five-brane web correspond to $T$-cones. Hanany-Witten transitions act on these geometries by flipping $T$-cones about their apex, thereby naturally endowing the choice of origin in the polygon with physical significance. It was recently conjectured that a suitably graded Hilbert series equals the Ehrhart series of the dual polytope, which, in turn, is an invariant under such mutations. In this paper, we introduce a prescription for assigning scaling dimensions to fields in the toric gauge theory associated with the underlying toric diagram and show that the resulting Hilbert series of the coherent component of the moduli space matches the geometric Hilbert series given by the Ehrhart series of the dual polytope once an origin is specified. We validate our construction through several non-trivial examples, including cases with multiple admissible choices of origin leading to distinct GTPs and brane-web realizations. Our results provide evidence that ordinary brane tilings retain non-trivial information about generalized toric polygons and suggest the existence of a deeper combinatorial structure underlying GTPs.

</details>


### [39] [Conformal QED in AdS as a BCFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19464)
*Fabiana De Cesare,Simone Giombi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文利用ε-展开（ε-expansion）方法，在d<4的欧几里得反德西特空间（Anti-de Sitter space, AdS）中研究了与无质量费米子或共形耦合标量场相互作用的共形量子电动力学（conformal QED），并通过计算边界共形场论（Boundary Conformal Field Theories, BCFTs）中的自由能和共形数据，指出在d=3时狄利克雷边界条件（Dirichlet boundary condition）可能无法定义稳定的BCFT。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在d<4的AdS空间中研究共形QED及其对应的边界共形场论（BCFT），探索不同边界条件（Dirichlet与Neumann）下系统的稳定性和边界共形性质，特别是边界标量算子的反常维度及其在低维下的边际性（marginality）行为。

Method: 采用围绕d=4的ε-展开（ε-expansion），对规范场施加狄利克雷（Dirichlet）或诺伊曼（Neumann）边界条件，计算相互作用不动点（interacting fixed point）处的重整化AdS自由能至次领头阶（next-to-leading order），并在单圈（one-loop）水平提取边界共形数据，包括最轻单态标量算子的反常维度（anomalous dimensions）。

Result: 在狄利克雷边界条件下，ε-展开结果的外推显示，在d=4附近为无关（irrelevant）的一个标量算子，在3<d<4的范围内达到边际性（marginality），提示该边界条件在d=3时可能无法定义稳定的BCFT。

Conclusion: 狄利克雷边界条件在d=3时可能无法定义稳定的边界共形场论（BCFT）；而诺伊曼边界条件（Neumann boundary condition）的相关稳定性则需进一步分析。

Abstract: We study conformal Quantum Electrodynamics (QED) coupled to either $N_f$ massless fermions or $N_s$ conformally coupled scalars in Euclidean Anti-de Sitter (AdS$_d$) space for $d < 4$. Using the $ε$-expansion around $d=4$, we investigate the associated Boundary Conformal Field Theories (BCFTs) defined by imposing either Dirichlet or Neumann boundary conditions on the gauge field. We compute the regularized AdS free energy at the interacting fixed point up to next-to-leading order and extract some of the boundary conformal data at one loop, including the anomalous dimensions of the lightest singlet scalar operators. For Dirichlet boundary conditions, extrapolation of our $ε$-expansion results indicate that one of these scalar operators, which is irrelevant near $d=4$, reaches marginality within the range $3 < d < 4$. This suggests that the Dirichlet boundary condition may not define a stable BCFT in $d=3$.

</details>


### [40] [Confinement Versus Screening in the Schwinger Model on AdS$_2$ from Bosonization and Tensor Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19468)
*Sriram Bharadwaj,Jack Isen,Zhong-Bo Kang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在二维反德西特时空（AdS₂）中，通过连续理论和格点方法分析了单味量子电动力学（QED₂）的禁闭（confinement）与屏蔽（screening）行为，并利用张量网络模拟验证了解析结果。研究发现，在减去位置依赖的探针自能后，静态势（static potential）在测地线距离趋于无穷时仍保持有限，表明体系处于屏蔽相；此外，还提出了一个协变离散化方案以在弯曲时空格点上放置费米子，并解决了相关文献中的歧义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前关于AdS₂中QED₂的研究在禁闭与屏蔽之间尚存在模糊(ambiguity)，且早期工作将未减除自能的基态能量误判为静态势，导致相图判断不清。因此，本研究旨在通过适当的自能减除(subtraction)以及格点模拟，澄清该体系的屏蔽性质，并建立一套协变的格点费米子离散化方案。

Method: 在连续理论中，利用玻色化(bosonization)在零温和有限温下导出质量极限下外电荷-反电荷对之间的静态势闭式；在格点方面，提出协变离散化方案(covariant discretization)以正确处理弯曲时空中的自旋和规范联络。通过矩阵乘积态(matrix product state, MPS)张量网络模拟，对AdS₂中的相图、静态势以及电通量管(electric flux-tube)轮廓进行了数值验证。

Result: 减除位置依赖的探针自能后，静态势在测地线分离趋于无穷时保持有限，表明该理论处于屏蔽相(screened phase)。该屏蔽行为与动力学费米子对U(1)电一形式对称性(electric one-form symmetry)的显式破缺一致。格点模拟结果吻合连续理论对AdS₂中相图的解析预测，且不同费米子质量下的数值结果与连续预言匹配良好。

Conclusion: AdS₂中的单味QED₂在质量极限下是屏蔽而非禁闭的；早期基于未减除自能的基态能量的判断存在混淆，将静态势等同于未减除的基态能量会导致禁闭/屏蔽的歧义。所提出的协变格点离散化方案有效解决了弯曲背景中格点费米子的已有歧义，并为张量网络模拟提供了可靠基础。

Abstract: We analyze confinement and screening in single-flavor quantum electrodynamics (QED$_2$) on two-dimensional anti-de Sitter space (AdS$_2$), with and without a Schwarzschild black hole, both in the continuum and on the lattice. The theory is formulated in two frames adapted to distinct choices of a preferred time coordinate: the Schwarzschild frame, associated with the Boulware vacuum, and the global AdS$_2$ frame, associated with the $\mathrm{SL}(2,\mathbb{R})$-invariant vacuum. In the massless limit, the static potential between an external charge-anticharge pair is obtained in closed form by bosonization, at both zero and finite temperature. After subtraction of the position-dependent probe self-energies, which, unlike in flat space, are not constant, the potential remains finite as the geodesic separation is taken to infinity, establishing that the theory is screened. This is consistent with the explicit breaking of the $\mathrm{U}(1)$ electric one-form symmetry by the dynamical fermions, and resolves a confining/screening ambiguity in earlier treatments that identify the static potential with the unsubtracted ground-state energy. To validate the continuum analysis, we propose a covariant discretization scheme for placing fermions in curved spacetime on the lattice while ensuring that the continuum properties of the spin and gauge connections are restored in the continuum limit. This construction resolves ambiguities in the existing literature on lattice fermions in curved backgrounds and provides the foundation for our tensor-network simulations. Using a matrix product state ansatz, we confirm our analytical predictions for the phase diagram in AdS$_2$. We perform extensive numerical simulations of the static potential and the electric flux-tube profile for varying fermion masses, which we match to the continuum prediction.

</details>

Method: 在标准Klein-Gordon场论中引入非局域项（non-local term）修改模型；将静态外源建模为点状标量电荷（point-like scalar charges），计算传播子（propagator）和相互作用势；在狄利克雷平面（Dirichlet plane）存在的情形下求解场传播子及边界-电荷相互作用力。

Conclusion: 非局域修正可产生类似Cornell势的粒子间势能，且镜像法不适用于该非局域标量场理论；相关结果与非局域电动力学（non-local electrodynamics）及标准Klein-Gordon场论进行了对比。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate novel classical non-local effects in scalar field theory arising from the presence of external sources and a material boundary. Specifically, we consider a model in which the standard Klein-Gordon field theory is modified by a non-local term. First, we analyze the interaction between stationary field sources modeled as point-like scalar charges. In specific configurations, the resulting interparticle potential reduces to the Cornell form. Then, we examine the model in the presence of a Dirichlet plane, computing both the scalar field propagator and the interaction force between the Dirichlet plane and a point-like scalar charge. Additionally, we demonstrate the failure of the image method in this non-local context and compare our results with those obtained in non-local electrodynamics and in the standard Klein-Gordon field theory.

### [42] [Resolved Maxwell-Boundary Normal Forms and Exact Reentrant Scaling in Accelerating AdS Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19748)
*Ruiliang Li*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过解析求解双相Maxwell转向问题，揭示了加速反德西特黑洞中重入相变（reentrant phase transitions）在微小弦张力（string tension）下不会消失的数学机制，并给出了相变窗口收缩与发散行为的标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 加速反德西特（anti-de Sitter）黑洞的重入相变在数值上已知，但在小弦张力极限下其表观消失缺乏解析解释，本文旨在填补这一理论空白。

Method: 在固定压强、电荷和张力条件下的单弦系综（single-string ensemble）中，求解带电慢加速C度规（C-metric）的无约束双相Maxwell转向问题（unrestricted two-phase Maxwell-turning problem）。通过消除约束迫使两个视界坐标重合，得到闭合单参数轨迹，并穷举剩余平衡态以确立全局相选择。

Result: 该轨迹存在于0<μ<0.202602区间，无正下限。当μ→0时，重入窗口的压强和温度宽度分别以张力的四次方和三次方收缩，而熵间隙（entropy gap）和潜热（latent heat）发散。双图放大（two-chart blow-up）给出了无参数极限轮廓，并识别出热力学体积反转（thermodynamic-volume inversion）作为两种不同非临界相之间的转向机制。

Conclusion: 在Maxwell边界下，热力学跳变的射影牛顿数据（projective Newton data）确定了共存轮廓的领先阶，其正单根（positive simple roots）决定了转向次数、阶次和曲率符号；C度规实现了原始二项式类（primitive binomial class）。

Abstract: Reentrant phase transitions of accelerating anti-de Sitter black holes are known numerically, but their apparent loss at small string tension has lacked an analytic explanation. In the single-string ensemble at fixed pressure, charge, and tension, we solve the unrestricted two-phase Maxwell-turning problem for the charged slowly accelerating C-metric. Elimination forces the two horizon coordinates to coincide and yields a closed one-parameter locus. An exhaustive enumeration of the remaining equilibria establishes global phase selection throughout the physical black-hole sector. The locus exists for $0<μ<0.202602$, with no positive lower threshold. As $μ\to0$, the pressure and temperature widths of the reentrant window contract as the fourth and third powers of the tension, while the entropy gap and latent heat diverge. A two-chart blow-up gives a parameter-free limiting profile and identifies thermodynamic-volume inversion as the turning mechanism between two distinct noncritical phases. At a Maxwell boundary with fixed sheet incidence, projective Newton data of the thermodynamic jumps determine the leading coexistence profile. Their positive simple roots fix the turn count, order, and curvature signs; the C-metric realizes the primitive binomial class.

### [43] [Real Quantum Field Theory, J-Quantization, and Standard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20304)
*I. Aref'eva,I. Volovich*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种完全基于实数构建的量子场论——实量子场论（Real Quantum Field Theory, RQFT），其核心是用满足 J²=-1 的 2×2 实矩阵 J 替代标准复量子场论中的虚数单位 i。论文以标量场为例构造了 RQFT，发展了相应的 J-微积分（J-calculus），并证明该理论与普通量子场论（QFT）的物理预言一致。进一步地，论文展示了粒子物理标准模型（Standard Model）也允许这种纯实数表述，其对称性为 ortho-symplectic 对称性，并指出 J-对称性破缺可能成为超越标准模型的新物理标志。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在探索是否可以用纯实数数学框架重新表述量子场论，从而替代传统的复数表述。这种尝试基于近年来发展的实量子力学（real quantum mechanics）在实 Kähler 空间上的推广，希望将其扩展至具有无穷自由度的场论系统。

Method: 作者通过在全部公式中将虚数单位 i 替换为满足 J²=-1 的实 2×2 矩阵 J，构建了实量子场论（RQFT）。为此发展了相应的 J-微积分，包括直接和逆 J-傅里叶变换（J-Fourier transforms）以及 J-值分布（J-valued distributions）。在标量场情形下，定义了作用于实 Kähler 类比玻色 Fock 空间上的场算符，该算符满足 Klein-Gordon 方程和 J-形式的正则对易关系。

Result: 论文证明了 RQFT 中的物理可观测量与普通标量 QFT 完全一致，因此不改变已有的物理预言，但提供了等价的实数表述。标准模型同样允许纯实数表述，所得理论具有 ortho-symplectic 对称性。J-对称性破缺可能作为超越标准模型的新物理标志。

Conclusion: 论文展示了一种与标准复数量子场论等价的纯实数表述框架 RQFT，并将其成功应用于标量场和标准模型。该工作不仅为量子场论提供了新的数学基础视角，还暗示 J-对称性破缺可能是探索新物理的方向。

Abstract: We present a formulation of quantum field theory based entirely on real numbers, which we call real quantum field theory (RQFT). The construction is obtained from the standard complex-number formulation by replacing the imaginary unit i with a matrix J throughout all formulas. Here J is the real 2x2 matrix satisfying the condition J^2=-1. This extends the recently developed formulation of real quantum mechanics based on the real Kähler space to systems with infinitely many degrees of freedom. As the basic example, we construct the RQFT for a scalar field. We define a field operator acting on the real Kähler analogue of the bosonic Fock space. This operator satisfies the Klein-Gordon equation and the J-form of canonical commutation relation. To construct the RQFT we develop the corresponding J-calculus. In particular, we introduce the direct and inverse J-Fourier transforms and the associated J-valued distributions. In RQFT, the usual unitarity condition for the complex S-matrix is replaced by the statement that the real scattering operator is both orthogonal and symplectic. The physical observables in RQFT coincide with those of ordinary QFT. Thus RQFT does not change the physical predictions of scalar QFT, but provides an equivalent formulation. We explore the possibility of purely real formulations of the Standard Model of elementary particles. We show that it does admit this formulation and the resulting theory has ortho-symplectic symmetry. The choice of the Standard Model as the testbed for exploring the possibility of purely real formulations is related with the fact it provides a realistic description of all known fundamental particles. The real formulation of the Standard Model naturally suggests a possible exit beyond the Standard Model. In particular, we consider the implications of breaking the J-symmetry as a marker for new physics.

### [44] [Three-dimensional TQFTs from Argyres--Douglas theories via the 3d/3d correspondence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20308)
*Cyril Closset,Adam Keyes,Sungjoon Kim*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过 3d/3d 对应（3d/3d correspondence），研究了 4d $\mathcal{N}=2$ Argyres–Douglas 理论的扭化维度约化（twisted dimensional reduction），重点分析 $(A_1, A_{2n})$ 类理论。论证了所得到的 3d $\mathcal{N}=4$ rank-0 超共形场论（superconformal field theory, SCFT）是透镜空间（lens space）$M_3^{(k)}=L(2n+3,2k)$ 上的 Dimofte–Gaiotto–Gukov (DGG) 阿贝尔 Chern–Simons–物质（abelian Chern–Simons-matter, ACSM）理论的红外不动点。通过三角剖分（triangulation）确定 ACSM 理论及其超势（superpotential），并详细检验了该构造与已知结果（如 Gang–Yamazaki 的最小 3d $\mathcal{N}=4$ SCFT 以及 Yang–Lee 拓扑量子场论（TQFT））的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在理解 4d $\mathcal{N}=2$ Argyres–Douglas 理论在扭化维度约化下的 3d 对应物，澄清 3d $\mathcal{N}=4$ rank-0 SCFT 的微观构造，并建立其与 DGG ACSM 理论及透镜空间三角剖分之间的系统联系。

Method: 利用 3d/3d 对应，将 4d 理论在具有一个不规则顶点（irregular puncture）的曲线 $\mathcal{C}$ 上的类 $\mathcal{S}$ 实现（class-$\mathcal{S}$ theory $T[\mathcal{C}]$），通过带扭 $k$ 的圆纤维化得到透镜空间 $M_3^{(k)}$，再基于 4d BPS 谱导出的三角剖分构建 DGG ACSM 理论及其超势。

Result: 当单极子超势（monopole superpotential）在精确意义上接近最大（near-maximal）时，ACSM 理论 $T[M_3^{(k)}]$ 流向预期的 SCFT；而最大超势（maximal superpotential）给出 $T_A[M_3^{(k)}]$，直接流向非酉（non-unitary）TQFT，即 SCFT 的拓扑 $A$-扭（topological $A$-twist）。TQFT 可在其全纯边界（holomorphic boundary）上支持 2d 顶点算子代数（vertex operator algebra, VOA），其中包括 $k=1$ 时 4d SCFT 的 Schur 扇区 VOA。对于 $n=k=1$，构造复现了来自 $L(5,2)$ 的 Gang–Yamazaki 最小 3d $\mathcal{N}=4$ SCFT，其 $T_A[M_3^{(k)}]$ 为 Yang–Lee TQFT，边界上支持 $M(2,5)$ 模型。从 Seifert 流形（Seifert manifolds）上的配分函数重构了 IR TQFT 的模结构（modular structure），并通过相位匹配从 ACSM 数据确定了 VOA 中心荷 $c_{\text{2d}} \bmod 8$ 及引力 Chern–Simons 能级（gravitational Chern–Simons level）。

Conclusion: SCFT 点与 TQFT 点在几何上通过三角剖分边界的锥形奇点（conical singularity）的移动相联系，并提出奇异边界与 SCFT 点之间的对应关系，可用于预测 SCFT 何时为酉 TQFT（unitary TQFT）。该构造在多个层面通过了自洽性检验，建立了 4d 超共形理论、3d SCFT/TQFT 与 2d VOA 之间的统一框架。

Abstract: We study the twisted dimensional reduction of 4d $\mathcal{N}=2$ Argyres--Douglas theories via the 3d/3d correspondence, focussing on $(A_1, A_{2n})$ theories realised as the class-$\mathcal{S}$ theory $T[\mathcal{C}]$ for a curve $\mathcal{C}$ with one irregular puncture. We argue the resulting 3d $\mathcal{N}=4$ rank-0 superconformal field theory (SCFT) arises as the IR fixed point of a Dimofte--Gaiotto--Gukov (DGG) abelian Chern--Simons-matter (ACSM) theory $T[M_3^{(k)}]$ for the lens space $M_3^{(k)}=L(2n+3,2k)$, obtained by fibering $\mathcal{C}$ over the circle with twist $k \in \mathbb{Z}_{2n+3}^\times$. The triangulation of $M_3^{(k)}$, derived from the 4d BPS spectrum, determines the ACSM theory including its superpotential. $T[M_3^{(k)}]$ flows to the expected SCFT when the monopole superpotential is near-maximal in a precise sense, while the maximal superpotential gives $T_A[M_3^{(k)}]$, which flows directly to a non-unitary TQFT, the topological $A$-twist of the SCFT. Geometrically, the SCFT and TQFT points are related by shifting conical singularities between edges of the triangulation, and we propose a correspondence between singular edges and SCFT points predicting when the SCFT is a unitary TQFT.
  The TQFTs from $M_3^{(k)}$ can support 2d vertex operator algebras (VOAs) on their holomorphic boundary, including the Schur-sector VOA of the 4d SCFT for $k=1$. For $n=k=1$, our construction reproduces the minimal 3d $\mathcal{N}=4$ SCFT of Gang and Yamazaki from $L(5,2)$, where $T_A[M_3^{(k)}]$ is the Yang--Lee TQFT supporting $M(2,5)$ on its boundary. We check our proposals in detail, reconstructing the modular structure of the IR TQFTs from partition functions on Seifert manifolds, and matching phases to determine VOA central charges $c_{\text{2d}} \bmod 8$ from the ACSM data, including the gravitational Chern--Simons level.

</details>


### [45] [Higher Superspace Supergravity and its IR-Completions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20312)
*Grigorios Giotopoulos,Hisham Sati,Urs Schreiber*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文采用现代化严谨框架，论证了高维超引力（super-gravity）可通过超时空上的超-比安基恒等式（super-Bianchi identities）与超挠率约束（super-torsion constraints）置于壳上，并指出该视角通过微分非交换上同调理论（differential nonabelian cohomology）中的电磁通量量子化（flux quantization）自然地构造出超引力的红外完备化（infrared completion）。文章综述了 11D 超引力、6D M5-膜世界体积和 10D IIA 超引力中各类超场通量所满足的 L∞-代数比安基恒等式及其降维关系，并指出对应的通量量子化方案分别由 4-余同伦（4-Cohomotopy）、扭曲不稳定 K-理论（twisted unstable K-theory）及扭曲（twistor）相对余同伦（relative Cohomotopy）实现，后者可几何工程化实验相关的拓扑量子序（topological quantum orders）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观念认为高维超引力可通过在受超挠率约束的超时空上对超场强施加比安基恒等式来置于壳上。本文旨在为该观点提供一个现代化的严格论述，并综述相关最新进展，尤其关注如何利用该视角通过微分非交换上同调理论中的电磁通量量子化来构造超引力的红外完备化。

Method: 方法核心在于将超-比安基恒等式提升为系数 L∞-代数（L∞-algebra）结构，并引入微分非交换上同调理论 $\mathcal{A}_{\mathrm{dff}}$ 来刻画通量量子化。具体推导中，通过 $\mathfrak{l}S^4$、$\mathfrak{l}_{S^4}S^7$、$\mathfrak{l}\mathrm{Cyc}(S^4)$ 和 $\mathfrak{l}\mathrm{Tor}(S^4)$ 等不同的 L∞-代数系数，分别建立 11D、6D M5-膜、10D IIA 及 9D 超引力中 C-场、B-场、NS/RR-通量所满足的比安基恒等式及其超空间维数约化（superspace dimensional reduction）关系。

Result: （1）证明了 11D 超引力的解等价于无超挠率 11D 超时空上超 C-场通量的 $\mathfrak{l}S^4$-比安基恒等式；（2）指出 6D M5-膜世界体积上的非线性自对偶规范扇区等价于超 B-场通量的 $\mathfrak{l}_{S^4}S^7$-比安基恒等式；（3）完整讨论了该情形经 $\mathfrak{l}\mathrm{Cyc}(S^4)$-比安基恒等式到 10D IIA 超引力的超空间维数约化，及其经 $\mathfrak{l}\mathrm{Tor}(S^4)$-比安基恒等式进一步到 9D 超引力的推广。由此导出红外完备化方案：11D 超引力由 4-余同伦实现 C-场通量量子化，10D IIA 超引力由扭曲不稳定 K-理论实现 NS/RR-场通量量子化，M5-膜世界体积由扭曲（twistorial）相对余同伦实现 B-场通量量子化。

Conclusion: 上述通量量子化方案为相应超引力提供了自洽的红外完备化。特别地，M5-膜世界体积上的扭曲相对余同伦量子化方案能够几何工程化实验上相关的拓扑量子序，暗示了超引力理论在红外与拓扑物态理论之间的深层联系。

Abstract: It is an old idea that higher-dimensional super-gravity (SuGra) is put on-shell just by imposing Bianchi identities on super-field strengths over super-spacetimes subject to super-torsion constraints. We give a modernized, rigorous account and review recent developments, pointing out how this perspective lends itself to the construction of infrared completions of SuGra by electromagnetic flux quantization in differential nonabelian cohomology theories $\mathcal{A}_{\mathrm{dff}}$ lifting the coefficient $L_\infty$-algebra $\mathfrak{l}\mathcal{A}$ of the super-Bianchi identities. After surveying necessary background, we highlight: (1.) our recent proof that solutions of 11D SuGra are equivalent to the $\mathfrak{l}S^4$-Bianchi identities on super $C$-field flux over super-torsion-free 11D super-spacetimes, (2.) how from this the nonlinearly self-dual gauge sector on 6D M5-brane worldvolumes is equivalent to the $\mathfrak{l}_{S^4}S^7$-Bianchi identity on super $B$-field flux, (3.) and the recent complete discussion of superspace dimensional reduction of this situation to 10D IIA SuGra via $\mathfrak{l}\mathrm{Cyc}(S^4)$-Bianchi identities on super NS/RR-flux, together with its extension to further reduction to 9 SuGra via $\mathfrak{l}\mathrm{Tor}(S^4)$-Bianchis on the corresponding super-fluxes.
  We close by indicating how this implies consistent infrared completions of 11D SuGra by $C$-field flux quantization in 4-Cohomotopy, of 10D IIA SuGra by NS/RR-field flux-quantization in a form of twisted unstable K-theory, and of M5-brane worldvolumes by $B$-field flux-quantization in twisted (twistorial) relative Cohomotopy. The latter admits geometric engineering of experimentally relevant topological quantum orders.

</details>


### [46] [Resolution of Gauss' law in the maximal Abelian gauge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20313)
*D. R. Junior,H. Reinhardt*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文在最大阿贝尔规范（maximal Abelian gauge）中求解高斯定律（Gauss' law），并辅以库仑规范（Coulomb gauge）处理阿贝尔规范场（Abelian gauge field），最终推导出QCD的规范固定哈密顿量（gauge-fixed Hamiltonian）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决QCD中规范固定后的高斯定律约束问题，为从哈密顿量视角研究夸克禁闭（quark confinement）等非微扰现象提供理论工具。

Method: 在最大阿贝尔规范基础上引入库仑规范作为阿贝尔规范场的附加条件，通过双重规范固定消除冗余自由度，并求解高斯定律约束。

Result: 成功推导出在最大阿贝尔规范与库仑规范联合条件下的QCD规范固定哈密顿量的具体形式。

Conclusion: 所构建的规范固定哈密顿量可为后续非微扰QCD分析（如色电动力学（color electrodynamics）中的禁闭机制研究）提供理论框架。

Abstract: We resolve Gauss' law in the maximal Abelian gauge supplemented by the Coulomb gauge for the Abelian gauge field and derive the gauge-fixed Hamiltonian of QCD.

### [47] [Interacting Dark Energy and Dark Matter in O(3) No-Scale Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20320)
*Lincoln da S. Pereira,Muzi Hong,Elisa G. M. Ferreira,Tsutomu T. Yanagida*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出暗能量（Dark Energy, DE）和暗物质（Dark Matter, DM）可能均源于纯引力领域，具体来自无标度引力（No-Scale Gravity）中 Brans-Dicke 玻色子及其 O(3) 对称性伙伴的自由度。通过 O(3) 轻微破缺产生质量和相互作用，该模型可重现背景宇宙学演化与当前丰度，并预言一种有效的类幻影（phantom-like）晚期演化行为，与 DESI 等宇宙学探测数据一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暗能量与暗物质的起源是粒子物理和宇宙学中最大的谜团之一。本文旨在探索两者是否可能共同来源于纯引力扇区，从而为暗成分的起源提供一个基本原理层面的统一解释。

Method: 作者基于无标度引力（一种 Planck 标度具有虚幻性的基础标度不变引力理论）构建模型。将 Brans-Dicke 玻色子与两个标量场组合成 O(3) 对称性下的矢量多重态（vector multiplet），在 Einstein 框架下将角度方向识别为 DM 和 DE。引入 O(3) 的小量显式破缺以生成质量和相互作用，并分析该模型对应的宇宙学演化方程。

Result: 模型成功重现了所需的背景宇宙学演化以及暗物质与暗能量的当前丰度。较轻的场在晚期提供动力学暗能量（dynamical DE）成分。尽管 DE 场本身是经典的（canonical），但相互作用的宇宙学在晚期表现出有效的类幻影演化行为，与 DESI 结合其他宇宙学探测的提示一致，且无需引入基本的幻影自由度。

Conclusion: 该模型从第一性原理（first-principles）实现了相互作用暗能量（interacting DE）的构建，其中暗物质、暗能量及其耦合均由底层引力理论的对称性结构自然产生。

Abstract: Dark Energy (DE) and Dark Matter (DM) are among the greatest mysteries in particle physics and cosmology, since their origins remain unclear. It is intriguing to consider whether both may originate from a purely gravitational sector. We propose that they arise from degrees of freedom associated with the partners of the Brans-Dicke boson in No-Scale Gravity, a fundamental scale-invariant gravitational theory in which the Planck scale is illusional. We consider the Brans-Dicke boson, together with two scalar fields, to form a vector multiplet under an $O(3)$ symmetry, whose angular directions in the Einstein frame are identified with DM and DE. Small explicit breaking of $O(3)$ generates their masses and interaction, and we show that the resulting model reproduces the required background cosmological evolution and present-day abundances, with the lighter field providing a dynamical DE component at late times. Although the DE field remains canonical, the interacting cosmology exhibits an effective phantom-like evolution at late times, of the type suggested by DESI in combination with other cosmological probes, without introducing a fundamental phantom degree of freedom. The model provides a first-principles realization of interacting DE, in which DM, DE, and their coupling emerge from the symmetry structure of the underlying gravitational theory.

</details>


### [48] [Accurate parameter inference for the Light-cone Epoch of Reionization 21-cm signal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19792)
*Suman Pramanick,Anoop Krishna,Rajesh Mondal,Somnath Bharadwaj*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文比较了三种统计量（标准圆柱功率谱、切片功率谱和演化功率谱）在分析光锥效应下21厘米信号时的性能，发现演化功率谱（ePS）能最有效地恢复理论基准并给出最紧的参数约束，将其确立为解读未来数据的优选统计量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光锥（light-cone, LC）效应使21厘米信号沿视线方向（line-of-sight, LoS）呈现统计不均匀性，传统功率谱（power spectrum, PS）无法完整捕捉两点统计信息。因此需要寻找更优的替代统计量。

Method: 对比了三种统计量：标准圆柱功率谱 $P(k_\perp,k_\parallel)$、切片功率谱 $P_s(k, z)$（即小带宽LC切片的3D PS）以及演化功率谱（evolving power spectrum, ePS）$P_e(k, z)$。训练了人工神经网络（artificial neural network, ANN）仿真器，基于500个LC 21厘米信号进行参数推断，并利用50个统计独立实现估计宇宙方差，同时加入SKA-Low系统噪声（积分时间1000小时和104小时）。

Result: 演化功率谱$P_e(k,z)$在大部分$k$和$z$范围内成功恢复了共同时代模拟（coeval simulation）的基准3D功率谱；切片功率谱仅在$k$较大时才能恢复。ePS在参数约束上优于其他两种统计量，比标准圆柱PS和切片PS分别紧约3倍和1.4倍。

Conclusion: 演化功率谱（ePS）被确立为一种最优的汇总统计量（summary statistic），适用于解释即将到来的观测数据。

Abstract: The light-cone (LC) effect introduces line-of-sight (LoS) statistical inhomogeneity into the 21-cm signal. Consequently, the traditional power spectrum (PS) fails to capture the full two-point statistical information. The evolving power spectrum (ePS), $P_e(k, z)$, offers an alternative that accounts for this LoS evolution. We compare the statistical power of three different summary statistics: the standard cylindrical PS $P(k_\perp,k_\parallel)$, slice-wise PS $P_s(k, z)$ (3D PS for small bandwidth LC slices), and ePS $P_e(k, z)$. We first demonstrate that $P_e(k,z)$ successfully recovers the benchmark 3D PS of coeval simulations across most $k$ and $z$, whereas the slice-wise PS recovers only at large $k$. To efficiently perform parameter inference, we train artificial neural network (ANN) emulators on $500$ LC 21-cm signals. Our forecasts incorporate cosmic variance, estimated using $50$ statistically independent realizations of the signal, alongside SKA-Low system noise for integration times of $1000$ and $104$ hrs. We find that ePS outperforms its peers, yielding $3$ and $1.4$ times tighter constraints than $P(k_\perp,k_\parallel)$ and $P_s(k,z)$, respectively. Our results establish the ePS as an optimal summary statistic for interpreting forthcoming data.

</details>


### [49] [Can cosmic voids ease the Hubble tension? Local expansion in $w_0w_a$CDM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20257)
*Tommaso Moretti,Noemi Frusciante,Giovanni Verza*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本研究在平坦 $w_0w_a$CDM 宇宙学中，利用流体动力学模型分析了局部宇宙空洞对低红移哈勃速率测量的影响。结果表明，空洞效应主要由物质密度对比度 $δ_{\rm E}$ 和物质密度参数 $Ω_{\rm m,0}$ 控制，暗能量贡献仅为亚主导水平。要完全匹配 SH0ES 值，需要一个比 KBC 型空洞更深的局部空洞。即使引入动力学暗能量，也仅带来百分之几的变化。整体而言，局部空洞无法在球对称空洞模型下解决哈勃张力问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 哈勃张力（Hubble tension）——即早期宇宙（如 Planck 卫星测量）与晚期宇宙（如 SH0ES 项目测量）所得哈勃常数 $H_0$ 之间的显著不一致——是当前宇宙学的主要未解问题之一。本研究旨在检验局部宇宙空洞作为一种可能的系统误差来源，能否通过影响低红移哈勃速率测量来缓解或解释这一张力。

Method: 采用孤立球状反顶帽欠密度（inverse top-hat underdensities）的流体动力学模型，计算空洞诱导的哈勃偏移（void-induced Hubble shift）作为红移、包裹密度对比度 $δ_{\rm E}$ 和宇宙学参数的函数。在平坦 $w_0w_a$CDM 宇宙学框架下进行分析，并考虑了动力学暗能量（dynamical dark energy）场景。

Result: 空洞效应主要受物质部分控制（$δ_{\rm E}$ 和 $Ω_{\rm m,0}$），动力学暗能量仅产生亚主导的晚期修正。对于 Planck 标定的 $Λ$CDM 背景，匹配 SH0ES 值需 $δ_{\rm E}(z=0)\simeq -0.44$，显著深于 KBC 型局部欠密度。KBC 型空洞可将 SH0ES-Planck 差异降至约 $2σ$ 但无法完全调和。引入动力学暗能量（包括参考 DES 和 DESI 分析的区域）仅改变结果约百分之一。报道的 $H_0$ 值红移依赖可用有效包裹物质剖面加以现象学表征。

Conclusion: 局部宇宙空洞确实能影响低红移哈勃速率推断，但在本文所考虑的球对称空洞设定下，它们无法解决哈勃张力。所重建的有效物质剖面应被视为局部结构效应的一致性检验，而非解释 $H_0$ 背景值演化的证据。

Abstract: We investigate the effect of local cosmic voids on low-redshift measurements of the Hubble rate in flat $w_0w_a$CDM cosmologies. Using a hydrodynamical model for isolated spherical inverse top-hat underdensities, we compute the void-induced Hubble shift as a function of redshift, enclosed density contrast $δ_{\rm E}$ and cosmological parameters. We find that the effect is mainly controlled by the matter sector, through $δ_{\rm E}$ and $Ω_{\rm m,0}$, while dynamical dark energy gives only subdominant late-time corrections. For a Planck-calibrated $Λ$CDM background, matching the SH0ES value requires a present-day void with $δ_{\rm E}(z=0)\simeq -0.44$, substantially deeper than the KBC-like local underdensity. A KBC-like void lowers the SH0ES-Planck discrepancy to about $2σ$, but is not deep enough to fully reconcile the two measurements. Allowing for dynamical dark energy, including regions motivated by recent DES and DESI analyses, changes this result only at the percent level. We also show that the reported redshift dependence of locally inferred $H_0$ values can be represented phenomenologically by an effective enclosed matter profile. This reconstruction should be interpreted as a consistency test of local-structure effects rather than as explanation for an evolving background value of $H_0$. Overall, local underdensities can affect low-redshift Hubble-rate inferences, but they do not resolve the Hubble tension within the spherical void setup considered here.

</details>


### [50] [Beyond $j=1$: Observational Constraints on Almost-$Λ$CDM Cosmologies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20348)
*Jess Worsley,Saikat Chakraborty,Peter Dunsby*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过三种“近乎ΛCDM”宇宙学封闭模型，利用DESI重子声学振荡、Planck宇宙微波背景和多种Ia型超新星数据，对宇宙加加速度（jerk）参数偏离1的程度进行观测约束。研究发现所有模型均被严格限制在ΛCDM不动点附近，且重构的暗能量演化呈现平滑冻结行为，未跨越幻影分界线。模型比较表明，这些几乎ΛCDM模型在统计上与传统暗能量参数化相当，同时更少依赖函数形式假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有宇宙学观测支持平直ΛCDM模型，但其背后的暗能量或修正引力机制仍不确定。本文旨在利用模型无关的宇宙学图（cosmography）方法，直接基于观测重构膨胀历史，检验当前数据是否允许宇宙加加速度（jerk）偏离ΛCDM模型的运动学特征j(z)=1，从而在不预设暗能量状态方程形式的前提下评估ΛCDM模型的稳健性。

Method: 采用三种现象学的“几乎ΛCDM”宇宙学图闭合模型，每个模型通过一个小变形参数ε使宇宙加加速度（jerk）略微偏离1。使用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov Chain Monte Carlo）方法，结合DESI重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillation）测量、压缩的Planck宇宙微波背景（cosmic microwave background）似然函数以及Union3、Pantheon+和DESY5三组Ia型超新星（Type Ia supernova）数据集进行约束。

Result: 三种闭合模型均被严格约束在ΛCDM宇宙学图不动点附近。Planck数据驱动演化趋向j₀≃1和w_DE,0≃-1。重构的暗能量演化始终呈现接近w=-1的平滑冻结（smooth freezing）行为，未跨越幻影分界线（phantom divide）。基于赤池信息准则（Akaike information criterion）和贝叶斯信息准则（Bayesian information criterion）的模型比较显示，几乎ΛCDM模型在统计上与标准暗能量参数化具有竞争力。

Conclusion: 模型无关的宇宙学图方法在约束宇宙膨胀历史方面具有强大能力。几乎ΛCDM模型在需要更少关于w(z)函数形式假设的前提下，仍能与标准参数化方案保持统计竞争力。该框架为未来研究宇宙学扰动和结构形成提供了自然的基础。

Abstract: The cosmographic condition $j(z)=1$ provides the kinematical signature of the spatially flat $Λ$CDM model independently of any specific dark-energy or modified-gravity theory. We investigate the extent to which current observations permit departures from this condition by considering three phenomenological ``almost-$Λ$CDM'' cosmographic closures, in which the cosmic jerk differs slightly from unity through a small deformation parameter $ε$. The models are constrained using Markov Chain Monte Carlo analyses of recent DESI baryon acoustic oscillation measurements together with compressed Planck cosmic microwave background likelihoods and the Union3, Pantheon+, and DESY5 Type Ia supernova compilations.
  Rather than assuming a parameterized dark-energy equation of state, our cosmographic framework reconstructs the expansion history directly from observations, with the effective dark-energy equation of state emerging as a derived quantity. We find that all three closures are tightly constrained to the vicinity of the $Λ$CDM cosmographic fixed point, with Planck data driving the preferred evolution toward $j_0\simeq1$ and $w_{\rm DE,0}\simeq-1$. Despite their distinct kinematical constructions, the reconstructed dark-energy evolution consistently exhibits smooth freezing behaviour close to $w=-1$, without crossing the phantom divide.
  Model comparison using the Akaike and Bayesian information criteria shows that the almost-$Λ$CDM models remain statistically competitive with standard dark-energy parameterizations while requiring fewer assumptions about the functional form of $w(z)$. These results demonstrate the power of model-independent cosmography for constraining the cosmic expansion history and provide a natural framework for future studies of cosmological perturbations and structure formation.

</details>

# gr-qc [[Back]](#toc)

### [51] [The general set of Noetherian energy-momentum tensors in linearized gravity: mathematical framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19445)
*Lydia Beth Taylor,Mark Robert Baker*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用诺特定理（Noether's first theorem）推导了线性引力（linearized gravity）中所有诺特型能量-动量张量（Noetherian energy-momentum tensor）的一般数学框架，证明无需引入超势“改进”（superpotential improvement）方法即可得到满足对称性和无迹性的能量-动量张量，并与现有文献中的多种引力能量-动量表达式进行比较，评估其诺特性归属。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 线性引力中能量-动量张量存在长期的非唯一性问题（non-uniqueness problem），文献中存在多种互不相同的表达式且缺乏共识；近期研究表明超势“改进”方法不足以解决该问题，因此有必要从诺特定理出发建立一般性的数学框架。

Method: 基于诺特定理，推导线性引力中所有可能的诺特型能量-动量张量的一般形式，不引入任何“改进”项；将所得一般结果与文献中多种常见的引力能量-动量表达式进行对比分类，并使用对称性（symmetry）和无迹性（tracelessness）等物理判据进一步筛选。

Result: 给出了线性引力中所有诺特型能量-动量张量的一般数学表达；证明了无需引入“改进”项，即可从诺特流（Noether current）中直接得到同时具有对称性和无迹性的能量-动量张量；识别了哪些现有表达式可归类为诺特型、哪些不能。

Conclusion: 该一般框架在不依赖“改进”方法的前提下，能够导出满足标准物理判据的能量-动量张量，并对解决线性引力中能量-动量张量的非唯一性问题具有重要启示。

Abstract: Energy-momentum tensors are foundational objects which are uniquely defined in standard physical field theories such as electrodynamics and Yang-Mills theory. In general relativity, and in particular linearized gravity where symmetries required for an energy-momentum tensor derived from Noether's first theorem are well defined, there exists a long standing non-uniqueness problem; numerous distinct energy-momentum expressions exist in the literature, and there is not consensus which, if any, is the unique expressions for the theory. Recently, the viability of the superpotential `improvement' method was shown to be insufficient for addressing the non-uniqueness problem of energy-momentum tensors in linearized gravity. In the present article, the mathematical framework for the general set of Noetherian energy-momentum tensors in linearized gravity is derived using Noether's first theorem, which consists of all possible energy-momentum tensors from the Noether current which yield the linearized Einstein field equations in the corresponding Euler-Lagrange equation of the Noether identity without introducing any `improvement' terms. This result has several advantages in addition to not requiring `improvements', such as the ability to impact the Lagrangian proportional piece of the energy-momentum tensor. Numerous common published gravitational energy-momentum expressions are then compared to these general results to assess which can be classified as Noetherian, and which cannot. Standard physical criteria such as symmetry and tracelessness are then used to prove that it is possible to directly obtain an energy-momentum tensor which is simultaneously symmetric and traceless from the Noether current; such an expression is derived from the general results. Consequences of these results and their relation to the aforementioned non-uniqueness problem are discussed.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将天体模型简化为常密度牛顿星（constant-density Newtonian stars），通过有效势（effective potential）分析快子模式，将其映射为解耦的倒谐振子（inverted harmonic oscillators），利用rigged Hilbert space形式体系进行量子化，并采用Unruh-DeWitt探测器计算跃迁概率。

Result: 快子模式在量子层次被描述为共振态（resonant states），其平均寿命由虚频率决定；探测器响应在快子模式存在时额外获得一个有限洛伦兹线形（Lorentzian profile），改变了标准的圆轨道Unruh类背景。

Abstract: A real scalar field nonminimally coupled to the curvature of an astrophysical object can develop an effective potential that supports, alongside stable oscillatory solutions, a set of tachyonic modes with purely imaginary frequencies. Focusing on constant-density Newtonian stars, we show that the tachyonic sector behaves as a collection of decoupled inverted harmonic oscillators, whose quantization is naturally addressed within the rigged Hilbert space formalism. At the quantum level, this sector is described by resonant states, with mean lifetimes determined by the associated imaginary frequencies. To probe the physical implications of this framework, we compute the transition probability of an Unruh-DeWitt detector in a circular orbit. In the presence of tachyonic modes, the detector response acquires an additional finite Lorentzian profile that modifies the standard circular Unruh-like background.

### [53] [Schrödinger perturbation theory for black hole quasinormal modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19492)
*Jacopo Lestingi,Laura Sberna,Stephen R. Green*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于双线性形式的系统化框架，将薛定谔微扰论推广到黑洞准正则模（QNM），从而实现了任意阶频率移的计算，并通过慢旋Kerr和Pöschl-Teller例子展示了该框架的应用及其QNM求和的发散性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真空广义相对论的偏差（如修正引力理论或环境效应）会在黑洞准正则模（QNM）谱中产生微小频移。虽然一阶频移已有较好理解，但缺乏计算高阶修正的系统性框架，主要障碍在于QNM因系统的非自伴性（non-self-adjointness）而不构成完备基。

Method: 利用近期发现的QNM在适当双线性形式（bilinear form）下的正交性，将薛定谔微扰论（Schrödinger perturbation theory）系统性地推广到黑洞背景，得到任意阶准正则频移公式，该公式依赖低阶模的频移；同时给出了一阶模移的谱分解。

Result: 得到了任意阶准正则频移的递推公式，以及一阶模移的谱分解（包含投影到未扰QNM上的部分和连续谱贡献，从而显式体现了非完备性）。在慢旋Kerr和Pöschl-Teller例子中，发现QNM求和本身是发散的。

Conclusion: 该框架填补了黑洞微扰论中高阶QNM频移计算方法的空白，且通过具体例子揭示了QNM谱展开的数学特性（非完备性与发散性），对引力波天文学中环down谱（ringdown spectra）的精确分析具有重要理论意义。

Abstract: Deviations from vacuum general relativity (such as modified theories or the presence of an environment) produce small shifts in black hole quasinormal mode (QNM) spectra. These effects are becoming increasingly relevant for gravitational wave astronomy as observations of ringdown spectra become more precise. The first-order frequency shift (in a small dimensionless coupling parameter) is now well understood, but no systematic framework exists to compute higher order corrections. The major obstacle is that QNMs do not form a complete basis due to the non-self-adjointness of the system. Nevertheless, it was recently shown that QNMs are orthogonal with respect to an appropriate bilinear form. In this work, we use the bilinear form to systematically lift Schrödinger perturbation theory to the black hole setting. We obtain a formula for quasinormal frequency shifts to any order, in terms of lower order mode shifts. We also provide a spectral decomposition of the first-order mode shift, which involves projections onto unperturbed QNMs along with continuous-spectrum contributions -- making incompleteness explicit. We illustrate the framework on slowly-spinning Kerr and Pöschl-Teller examples, where we find that the QNM sum itself diverges.

### [54] [Repetitive Penrose Process in Rastall Rotating Black Holes Immersed in Quintessence Dark Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19541)
*Ali Ahmad Sabir,Muhammad Israr Aslam,Abdul Malik Sultan,Ke Wang,Hamood Ur Rehman,Yakup Yildirim*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先回顾黑洞几何的基本性质，然后推导ergoregion内粒子分裂的守恒方程及对应的迭代演化方程，建立终止能量提取迭代所需的物理条件，并分析衰变粒子的最小自旋阈值（minimum spin threshold）以识别关键停止判据。

Result: 重复彭罗斯过程的终止始终由具有最高最小自旋阈值的衰变产物Particle 0控制。无量子Rastall结构参数\hat{N}_s和Rastall耦合参数α的初始值增加均能提升能量利用效率（energy utilization efficiency）和能量投资回报率（energy return on investment）。较小\hat{N}_s在较低衰变半径下增强效率，使最大提取能量向低半径偏移，并加速可提取能量储库的耗竭；较小\hat{N}_s还产生更大的最大能量投资回报率。α的增加也提升能量利用效率并改变峰值位置，但减少总可提取能量；α的影响远小于\hat{N}_s。

Conclusion: 重复彭罗斯过程在较低衰变半径（lower decay radii）下更受青睐。参数\hat{N}_s对能量提取过程的影响远大于α，前者是调控能量提取效率与投资回报率的关键因素。

Abstract: We investigate the repetitive Penrose process in the spacetime of a Rastall rotating black hole surrounded by a quintessence dark energy field. After reviewing the fundamental properties of the black hole geometry, we formulate the repetitive Penrose process by deriving the conservation equations governing particle splitting within the ergoregion, along with the corresponding iterative evolution equations. The physical conditions required for terminating the energy extraction iterations are established, and the minimum spin thresholds of the decay particles are analyzed to identify the critical stopping criterion. Our analysis reveals that the termination of the repetitive Penrose process is consistently governed by Particle~$0$, which possesses the highest minimum spin threshold among all decay products. Numerical results further demonstrate that the dimensionless Rastall structure parameter $\hat{N}_s$ and the Rastall coupling parameter $α$ significantly influence the evolution of the energy extraction process. At the same decay radii increasing initial values of both parameters boosts the energy utilization efficiency and energy return on investment. Specifically, smaller values of $\hat{N}_s$ enhances the energy utilization efficiency at lower decay radii, shifts the maximum extracted energy toward lower decay radii, and accelerates the depletion of the remaining extractable energy reservoir. This indicates that the repetitive Penrose process is highly favored at lower decay radii. Smaller initial values of $\hat{N}_s$ yield a larger maximum energy return on investment. Similarly, increasing $α$ enhances the energy utilization efficiency, alters the location of the peak extracted energy, and reduces the total extractable energy. But the effects of $α$ on these energetics are very small as compared to $\hat{N}_s$.

### [55] [On the geometrical and dynamical distinction between Unimodular and General Relativistic wormholes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19657)
*Marco Bosquez,Erick Pastén,Mauricio Cataldo,Norman Cruz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文表征了单模引力（Unimodular Gravity, UG）中的可穿越虫洞（traversable wormholes），并研究了它们与广义相对论（General Relativity, GR）中对应解的差异。尽管两种理论在几何和测地线结构上等价，但维持相同虫洞几何所需的源（source）扇区不同，差异体现在有效非均匀真空结构（effective inhomogeneous vacuum structure）中，其渐近行为类似宇宙学常数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究单模引力（UG）中的可穿越虫洞（traversable wormholes）与广义相对论（GR）中对应解的区别，并理解这两种理论在几何等价性之外，其物理差异的起源。

Method: 针对一类静态球对称解（static and spherically symmetric solutions），分析其嵌入（embedding）和类时测地线（timelike geodesics）；通过比较维持相同虫洞几何所需的源扇区（source sectors），研究能量-动量守恒（energy-momentum conservation）条件的约束作用以及有效非均匀真空贡献（inhomogeneous vacuum contribution）的影响。

Result: 测地线结构完全由度规（metric）决定，因此在UG和GR中完全相同。维持固定UG几何并施加能量-动量守恒会限制状态方程（equation of state）；放松该条件则引入有效非均匀真空贡献。奇异程度（degree of exoticity）在能量-动量不守恒时仍然保持，与GR扇区的偏离体现在有效非均匀真空结构中，其渐近行为类似宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）。

Conclusion: UG在几何上与GR等价，其独特特征体现在源扇区的动力学解释中。不同的引力理论可能产生相同的时空几何，但需要不同的源来维持它们。

Abstract: We characterize traversable wormholes in Unimodular Gravity (UG) and investigate what distinguishes them from their General Relativistic (GR) counterparts. For a class of static and spherically symmetric solutions, we analyze their embedding and timelike geodesics, showing that the geodesic structure is entirely determined by the metric and is therefore identical in both theories.
  To identify the physical origin of their differences, we compare the source sectors required to sustain the same wormhole geometry. We find that preserving a fixed UG geometry while imposing energy-momentum conservation requires restricting the equation of state, whereas relaxing this condition introduces an effective inhomogeneous vacuum contribution. We further show that the degree of exoticity is preserved even when energy-momentum is not conserved, while departures from the GR sector are encoded in an effective inhomogeneous vacuum structure whose asymptotic behavior resembles that of a cosmological constant.
  Our results reinforce that UG is geometrically equivalent to GR, while its distinctive features emerge in the dynamical interpretation of the source sector. More generally, our analysis illustrates that different gravitational theories may give rise to identical spacetime geometries while requiring different sources to sustain them.

### [56] [Instability of regular black holes in non-minimally coupled scalar field theories: an analytical approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19755)
*Majid Karimabadi,Davood Mahdavian Yekta,S. A. Alavi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文揭示，在两类非最小耦合标量-张量模型中，当耦合常数取某些临界值时，黑洞稳定性不再保持；通过近视界近似得到临界耦合常数的精确表达式，数值分析表明该临界值与摄动时域轮廓的阈值点一致，且此时Regge-Wheeler方程的有效势在事件视界位置出现极值，准正则模的实部消失，最终在不依赖高度阻尼模近似的情况下恢复了球对称黑洞的一般面积量子化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究非最小耦合标量-张量模型（non-minimally coupled scalar-tensor models）中黑泂稳定性（black hole stability）的鲁棒性（robustness）是否在特定耦合常数临界值下被破坏，尤其针对一类正则黑洞（regular black holes）。

Method: 采用近视界近似（near-horizon approximation）进行解析推导，得到临界耦合常数的精确表达式；结合时域摄动轮廓（time-domain profiles of field perturbations）进行数值分析验证；利用Regge-Wheeler方程的有效势（effective potential）考察视界位置处的极值行为；分析准正则模（quasi-normal frequencies）在近视界区域的实部变化。

Result: 解析获得了两个模型中导致不稳定的临界耦合常数精确表达式。数值分析表明临界值与摄动时域轮廓的阈值点吻合。在临界值处，有效势在事件视界（event horizon）位置达到极值，准正则模实部在近视界区域消失（即纯虚模态，purely imaginary modes）。

Conclusion: 在不依赖高度阻尼模近似（highly-damped mode approximation）的前提下，恢复了临界耦合常数下球对称黑洞的一般面积量子化（general area quantization），且该结果与具体的耦合模型无关。

Abstract: In this paper, we show that the robustness of black hole stability is not preserved when the perturbations are disposed on some critical values of the coupling constant in two non-minimally coupled scalar-tensor models, in particular for a number of regular black holes. Using an analytical demonstration in the near-horizon approximation, we obtain exact expressions for the critical coupling constant in two models for which the instability will occur. The numerical analysis show that these critical values are consistent with the threshold points in time-domain profiles of field perturbations. At that threshold value, the effective potential of the Regge-Wheeler equation exhibits an extremum exactly on the location of event horizon. We also show that the real part of the quasi-normal frequencies vanish in the near-horizon regime at critical coupling constant -- recently addressed as purely imaginary modes. Finally, we recover the general area quantization of the spherical black holes at that critical coupling without invoking to highly-damped mode approximation and the result is independent of a specific coupling model.

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the quantum entanglement properties of analog Hawking radiation produced by a moving mirror. This indicates that the negative energy flux acts as a channel through which information can be returned. ### [58] [Circular-orbit dynamics and QPO constraints in static Einstein--scalar--Gauss--Bonnet black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19805)
*Sardor Murodov,Bekzod Rahmatov,Otabek Umarov,Anvar Kurbaniyazov,Faisal Javed,Javlon Rayimbaev*

TL;DR: 本文在爱因斯坦-标量-高斯-博内（Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet, EsGB）引力框架下，研究了静态黑洞周围的中性粒子圆轨道运动和高频准周期振荡（HF-QPOs），并利用相对论进动模型对四个X射线双星源的孪峰QPO数据进行马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）分析。结果表明，径向epicyclic频率对形变参数p最敏感，但由于仅用两个测量频率拟合三个相关参数，参数p的后验分布主要由先验决定，无法实现独立测量，只能给出模型依赖的相容区间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EsGB引力为检验史瓦西几何的强场偏离提供了物理动机明确的理论框架，但该理论的静态黑洞解参数是否可被现有天文观测约束尚不清楚。本文旨在通过高频准周期振荡数据系统检验EsGB形变参数p的可测量性。

Method: 采用持续分数（continued-fraction）度规描述静态EsGB黑洞，该度规仅包含一个无量纲形变参数p。推导了有效势、圆轨道能量与角动量、特征半径以及轨道和径向epicyclic频率的表达式，并基于相对论进动模型（relativistic precession model）对XTE J1550-564、GRO J1655-40、GRS 1915+105和M82 X-1四个源的孪峰QPO数据进行逐个源的MCMC分析。此外，使用均匀先验和截断高斯先验进行了受控的先验敏感性分析。

Result: 观测频率对在不确定度内均可被重现，径向epicyclic频率对参数p的模型级敏感性最高。但先验敏感性分析显示，在所有四个源中，p的边际后验分布几乎完全跟随所采用的先验分布，这反映出用两个测量频率拟合三个相关参数(M,p,r)存在内在的欠约束（underconstraint）问题。

Conclusion: 推断出的区间本质上是模型依赖的相容区域，而非EsGB形变的独立测量或偏好值。该静态结果为未来考虑旋转效应和多观测量联合检验的研究提供了基准。

Abstract: Einstein--scalar--Gauss--Bonnet (EsGB) gravity provides a physically motivated framework for testing strong-field deviations from the Schwarzschild geometry through scalar hair. We study neutral-particle circular motion and high-frequency quasi-periodic oscillations (HF-QPOs) in static EsGB black holes described by a continued-fraction metric with a single dimensionless deformation parameter \(p\) on the Schwarzschild-connected quadratic-coupling branch. We determine the effective potential, circular-orbit energy and angular momentum, characteristic radii, and orbital and radial epicyclic frequencies, and apply the relativistic precession model to twin-peak QPO data from XTE J1550--564, GRO J1655--40, GRS 1915+105, and M82 X-1. A source-by-source Markov chain Monte Carlo analysis shows that the observed frequency pairs can be reproduced within their uncertainties and that the radial epicyclic frequency carries the main model-level sensitivity to \(p\). However, a controlled prior-sensitivity analysis using uniform and truncated Gaussian priors finds that the marginal posterior of \(p\) closely follows the adopted prior for all four sources. This reflects the intrinsic underconstraint of fitting three correlated parameters \((M,p,r)\) to two measured frequencies. The inferred intervals therefore represent model-dependent compatibility regions rather than an independent measurement or preferred value of the EsGB deformation. The static results provide a baseline for future rotating and multi-observable tests.

### [59] [Characterization of the Scattered Light Noise in KAGRA Interferometer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19814)
*Shih-Hong Hsu,Hirotaka Yuzurihara,Chia-Jui Chou,Yi Yang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为 f-cluster 的新分析方法，用于在引力波望远镜中识别和表征散杂光噪声（scattered light noise）。该方法无需对散射源做先验假设，通过提取时频图中拱形特征的周期性，成功应用于 KAGRA 2025 年 4 月的数据，识别出 0.432 Hz 的散射频率，并发现散杂光噪声的发生率与 0.3–1.0 Hz 频段的地面运动振幅存在强相关（Pearson 相关系数 0.82）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波望远镜中的非平稳噪声（non-stationary noise）会干扰干涉仪稳定运行并限制引力波分析。散杂光噪声在短时间内跨越宽频带波动，可能模仿引力波信号、增加误报率或使参数估计产生偏差。现有方法缺乏对散射源无先验假设的散杂光噪声特征刻画手段。

Method: 提出 f-cluster 算法，利用散杂光噪声在时频图中呈现的拱形（arch-shaped）特征，从频谱图（spectrogram）中提取拱形结构的周期性，检测过功率区域的发生时间和周期，进而估计散射物体的振荡频率。该方法不依赖对散射源的先验假设。

Result: 将 f-cluster 算法应用于 KAGRA 2025 年 4 月 1 日至 30 日的数据，成功识别出散射频率 $f_{sc} = 0.432$ Hz。散杂光噪声的发生率与 0.3–1.0 Hz 频段地面运动振幅的 Pearson 相关系数为 0.82，表明散杂光噪声的发生可通过地震运动进行预测。

Conclusion: 该算法能在不对散射对象做假设的前提下，识别散杂光噪声的频率和发生时间，有助于实际数据中散杂光噪声的特征刻画，并为定位散杂光噪声源的噪声溯源（noise hunting）提供信息。

Abstract: In a gravitational wave (GW) telescope, non-stationary noise can prevent stable interferometer operation and limit the GW analyses. Among the non-stationary noise, we focus on the scattered light noise. It fluctuates across a wide frequency band within a short time. Therefore, the scattered light noise can mimic the GW signal, increase the false alarm rate, or bias the parameter estimation results. In this work, we propose a new analysis method, named f-cluster, to characterize these features without prior assumptions about the scattering source. The scattered light noise shows characteristic arch-shaped features in time-frequency maps. Therefore, the algorithm extracts the periodicity of the arch shapes from the spectrogram. The algorithm detects the occurrence times and periodicity of excess-power regions in the spectrogram to estimate the oscillation frequency of the scattering object. To demonstrate the algorithm, we applied this method to KAGRA data from April 1 to 30, 2025, and successfully identified a scattering frequency of $f_{sc} = 0.432$ Hz. Furthermore, we found a strong correlation between the occurrence rate of the scattered light noise and the amplitude of ground motion in the $0.3-1.0$ Hz band with a Pearson correlation coefficient of 0.82. This correlation showed that the occurrence of scattered light noise can be forecast from the seismic motion. We confirmed that our algorithm identifies the frequency of the scattered light noise and its occurrence time, without making assumptions about the scattering object, thereby contributing to the characterization of the scattered light noise in real data. Our algorithm provides information that leads to further investigation into the noise hunting to specify the source of scattered light noise.

</details>


### [60] [Coordinate Independence of the Schwarzschild Black Hole Accretion Vlasov Gas Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19815)
*Ping Li,Jun Cheng,Jiang-he Yang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究Vlasov气体吸积到Schwarzschild黑洞时的坐标依赖性问题。通过渐近展开和数值计算，发现粒子数密度、能量密度、压力及吸积率等物理量不依赖于坐标选择，而粒子流密度和应力-能量张量则依赖坐标系。吸积粒子的平均能量低于经典Maxwell-Boltzmann系统的平均值，比熵也低于全局平均值，原因是低能粒子更易被吸积。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在广义相对论框架下，Vlasov气体吸积到Schwarzschild黑洞时，不同坐标系下的物理量是否具有坐标不变性尚不明确。本文旨在系统研究吸积理论中关键物理量的坐标依赖性，并澄清其背后的物理机制。

Method: 采用最一般的稳态球对称时空（stationary spherically symmetric spacetime）框架，对三种不同统计分布进行Taylor展开，得到无穷远处和视界（horizon）附近的渐近结果。同时给出有限半径处相关物理量的数值结果。

Result: 粒子数密度、能量密度、径向和切向压力以及吸积率（accretion rate）不依赖于坐标选择；而粒子流密度（particle current density）和应力-能量张量（stress-energy tensor）则显式依赖坐标系。吸积粒子的平均能量为$m_0+k_BT$，低于经典极限下Maxwell-Boltzmann系统的平均能量$m_0+\frac{3}{2}k_BT$；吸积粒子的比熵（specific entropy）比全局平均值低$\frac{3}{2}k_B$。

Conclusion: 吸积理论可以不依赖于任何特定的坐标系进行表述。低能粒子更易被吸积而高能粒子更易被散射，这解释了吸积粒子平均能量和比熵均低于全局平均值这一现象。

Abstract: This paper presents a detailed study of the coordinate dependence of Vlasov gas accretion onto a Schwarzschild black hole. Asymptotic results at infinity and near horizon are obtained via Taylor expansions for three different statistical distributions within the framework of the most general stationary spherically symmetric spacetime. Our findings demonstrate that the particle number density, energy density, radial and tangential pressures, and accretion rates are independent of the coordinate choice, even though individual components such as the particle current density and the stress-energy tensor explicitly depend on the coordinate system. Consequently, the accretion theory can be formulated without reference to any particular coordinate system. We also show that the mean energy of the accreted particles is $m_0+k_BT$, lower than the mean energy $m_0+\frac{3}{2}k_BT$ of the Maxwell-Boltzmann system in the classical limit. And the specific entropy of the accreted particles is lower than the global average by $\frac{3}{2}k_B$. This is because particles of lower energy are more easily accreted, while particles of higher energy are more readily scattered. We also present numerical results at finite radii for the relevant physical quantities.

</details>


### [61] [Quasinormal modes of the Kazakov--Solodukhin quantum-corrected black hole: a spectral analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19860)
*Davide Batic,Denys Dutykh,Mark Sukaiti*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 采用高精度切比雪夫谱方法（Chebyshev spectral method）计算 Kazakov–Solodukhin 量子修正黑洞的拟正则模（quasinormal modes），将径向问题简化为关于无量纲频率 Ω 的二次矩阵铅笔（quadratic matrix pencil），并应用于多种扰动场；结果复现了已有基准方法，并解析了新的过阻尼根与近极端行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确计算量子修正黑洞的拟正则模，以超越传统 WKB、时域等方法的分辨率限制，并探索纯虚过阻尼根（overdamped roots）及其谱结构。

Method: 使用切比雪夫谱方法，在剔除事件视界与空间无穷远处的渐近行为后，将径向摄动方程化为关于无量纲频率 Ω 的二次矩阵铅笔，数值求解特征值问题。分别处理了最小耦合标量扰动、电磁扰动、非最小耦合标量场以及轴向有效 Regge–Wheeler 型引力扇区。

Result: 复现了已有 WKB、时域、Mashhoon 和渐近迭代法（asymptotic-iteration method）的基准结果；发现额外过阻尼根候选，其间距标度接近 Mκ = 1/4；在近极端（near-extremal）亚极端区域，纯虚分支趋近于按表面引力（surface gravity）等间距标度的阶梯结构，而振荡谱仍依赖于扇区；所有保留模式的虚部均小于零，未检测到稳定增长模。

Conclusion: 谱方法能够高效、精确地解析 Kazakov–Solodukhin 黑洞的拟正则谱，揭示其过阻尼根的结构和近极端行为，且在该参数范围内未发现不稳定模。

Abstract: We compute quasinormal modes of the Kazakov--Solodukhin quantum-corrected black hole using a high-precision Chebyshev spectral method. After factoring out the quasinormal mode asymptotics at the event horizon and at spatial infinity, the radial problem is reduced to a quadratic matrix pencil for the dimensionless frequency $Ω=Mω$. We apply this framework to minimally coupled scalar perturbations, electromagnetic perturbations, a non-minimally coupled scalar field, and an axial effective source Regge--Wheeler-type gravitational sector. The latter is treated as an effective axial model, rather than as the full gravitational perturbation problem, because the Kazakov--Solodukhin spacetime is not Ricci flat. Our results reproduce the available WKB, time-domain, Mashhoon, and asymptotic-iteration benchmarks in their common regimes of validity, after accounting for the different normalisations used in the literature. The spectral method also resolves additional overtones and candidate purely imaginary overdamped roots. In several sectors, these roots exhibit a spacing scale close to $Mκ=1/4$, with occasional multiple gaps in the retained numerical sequence. In the near-extremal, but still subextremal, regime, the detected purely imaginary branches approach an approximately equally spaced surface-gravity-scaled ladder, while the oscillatory spectra remain sector dependent. Within the parameter ranges and resolutions considered here, all retained modes have $\ImΩ<0$, and no stable growing mode is detected.

### [62] [Quasinormal modes of scalar and Maxwell field perturbations coupled to the Einstein tensor in generalized Nariai spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19863)
*Xin Qin,Xiongying Qiao,Qiyuan Pan,Xiangyun Fu,Xuan Zhou,Ying Yang*

TL;DR: 本文研究了广义Nariai时空中，标量场和麦克斯韦场（Maxwell field）扰动与爱因斯坦张量（Einstein tensor）耦合时产生的准正则模（quasinormal modes）。结果表明，耦合引入了不同的临界值，导致频谱分支化，并在特定参数区间产生纯虚数模式；耦合对标量场和麦克斯韦场振荡部分的影响方向相反，且磁荷和时空维度对频谱有调节作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究广义Nariai时空中标量场和麦克斯韦场扰动与爱因斯坦张量耦合后的准正则模行为，揭示曲率耦合（curvature coupling）对不同类型场扰动的影响差异。

Method: 在广义Nariai时空背景下，对标量场和麦克斯韦场扰动施加与爱因斯坦张量的耦合，通过解析方法求解准正则模的频域特征，分析临界值、频率平方的符号变化及参数依赖性。

Result: 耦合引入了不同的临界值，将频率谱（frequency spectrum）分隔为不同分支；在临界值附近，$ω_R^2$ 中的平方根项可能变号，导致某一参数区间内模式变为纯虚数。离开该区域后，耦合对标量场和麦克斯韦场的振荡部分产生相反影响：标量场的 $ω_R^2$ 随耦合常数 $η$ 增加而增加，麦克斯韦场的 $ω_R^2$ 随 $η$ 增加而减小。磁荷（magnetic charge）增强振荡响应，而增大时空维度（spacetime dimension）则压缩纯虚数模式区间。

Conclusion: 相同的曲率耦合对标量场和麦克斯韦场扰动产生定性不同的影响，该差异通过准正则模的频谱行为得到解析证明。

Abstract: We investigate the quasinormal modes of scalar and Maxwell field perturbations coupled to the Einstein tensor in generalized Nariai spacetimes. Our results show that, for both types of perturbations, the coupling introduces different critical values, which separate the frequency spectrum into distinct branches. Near these critical values, the square-root term that determines $ω_R^2$ may change sign, giving rise to a parameter interval in which the modes are purely imaginary. Away from this regime, the coupling affects the oscillatory parts of the two fields in opposite ways: $ω_R^2$ generally increases with the coupling constant $η$ for the scalar field, whereas it decreases with $η$ for the Maxwell field. The magnetic charge tends to enhance the oscillatory response, while increasing the spacetime dimension narrows the purely imaginary regime. This comparison shows analytically that the same curvature coupling can affect scalar and Maxwell perturbations in qualitatively different ways.

### [63] [Geometry-Induced Termination of the Repetitive Penrose Process in Rotating Simpson-Visser Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19904)
*Mohammad Ali S. Afshar,Mohammad Reza Alipour,Saeed Noori Gashti,J. Sadeghi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了旋转Simpson-Visser时空中重复彭罗斯过程（Repetitive Penrose Process）的终止机制。结果表明，当正则化参数足够大时，演化系统可能在达到动态自旋极限之前离开双视界黑洞分支，从而引入一个额外的几何诱导终止条件。该条件与正则化参数共同影响过程的效率、迭代次数及自洽性参数范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 文章在旋转Simpson-Visser时空中，通过理论分析假设正则化参数在整个演化过程中保持不变，考察重复彭罗斯过程的迭代演化动力学特征。结合数值计算，系统分析了提取能量、不可约化质量终值、两种效率度量随正则化参数及粒子衰变半径的变化规律。

Result: 研究发现，当正则化参数足够大时，演化解在达到动态自旋极限前会提前离开两视界黑洞分支，形成几何诱导的终止条件。数值结果显示，小正则化参数下的演化行为与Kerr时空定性相似，但随着参数增大，累积提取能量、可允许的彭罗斯迭代次数及过程效率均显著下降。

Conclusion: 在旋转Simpson-Visser时空中，时空几何结构不仅影响重复彭罗斯过程的累积效率，还限定了迭代演化能够保持自洽的参数范围。这突显了规则旋转黑洞时空中，时空几何在塑造彭罗斯型能量提取过程长期演化中的作用。

Abstract: We examine the Repetitive Penrose Process in the rotating Simpson-Visser spacetime, whose parameter space includes regular black holes, black-bounce geometries, and traversable wormholes. Assuming that the regularization parameter remains unchanged throughout the evolution, the analysis shows that the endpoint of the repetitive process is not always determined solely by the conventional minimum spin condition. Instead, for sufficiently large values of the regularization parameter, the evolving solution may leave the parameter domain corresponding to the original two horizon black hole branch before the dynamical spin limit is reached. Within the present framework, this provides an additional geometry-induced condition that limits the continuation of the iterative sequence. The numerical results further show that the relative importance of the dynamical and geometry-induced termination mechanisms depends sensitively on the regularization parameter. For small deformations, the evolution remains qualitatively similar to that of the Kerr spacetime. As the regularization parameter increases, however, the cumulative extracted energy, the number of admissible Penrose iterations, and the efficiency of the process are progressively reduced. We also examine how the extracted energy, the final irreducible mass, and two complementary efficiency measures vary with both the regularization parameter and the particle decay radius. Overall, the present analysis indicates that, within the RSV geometry, the underlying spacetime structure influences not only the cumulative efficiency of the repetitive Penrose process but also the parameter range over which the iterative evolution remains self-consistent. These results highlight the role that spacetime geometry can play in shaping the long-term evolution of idealized Penrose-type energy extraction processes in regular rotating black-hole spacetimes.

### [64] [What may come beyond the Wheeler-DeWitt approach?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19958)
*T. P. Shestakova*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文比较了广义的Wheeler-DeWitt方法与扩展现相空间方法（extended phase space approach）在引力量子化中的差异，指出前者由于依赖渐近态假设而与任意时空拓扑的设想矛盾，而后者完全基于路径积分，避免了该矛盾并导出了薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation），因此超越了Wheeler-DeWitt方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 比较Wheeler-DeWitt方法（广义理解）与扩展现相空间方法这两种引力量子化途径，指出前者在逻辑上存在的内在矛盾，并论证后者的优越性。

Method: 从理论分析层面出发，逐一检视Wheeler-DeWitt方程的推导基础——Dirac形式体系（Dirac formalism）及其应用于引力时的后果；同时分析路径积分（path integral）途径与正则量子化（canonical quantization）之间的矛盾，并引入完全基于路径积分的扩展现相空间形式体系作为替代方案。

Result: Wheeler-DeWitt方法依赖渐近态假设，因此无法与任意时空拓扑（spacetime topology）的设想兼容；若放弃该假设，则路径积分的规范不变性（gauge invariance）无法得到证明，Wheeler-DeWitt方程也失去意义。扩展现相空间方法则导出了薛定谔方程，从而超越了Wheeler-DeWitt量子几何动力学（quantum geometrodynamics）。

Conclusion: 扩展现相空间方法是一种真正超出Wheeler-DeWitt框架的替代方案，能够得出后者无法获得的结论。

Abstract: The goal of this paper is to compare the Wheeler-DeWitt approach, understood in a broad sense, with an alternative one, the so-called extended phase space approach to quantization of gravity. By "the Wheeler-DeWitt approach", I mean not only quantum geometrodynamics formulated by DeWitt in his seminal paper of 1967, but also any approach to quantization of gravity based on the Wheeler-DeWitt equation in some form. Since the Wheeler-DeWitt equation is a direct consequence of the Dirac formalism, its analysis requires examination of the latter and its application to gravity. In particular, I argue that there is a contradiction between canonical quantization and the idea put forward by founders of quantum gravity that, in this theory, all possible spacetime topologies should be taken into account. The path integral approach seems to be more adequate then the canonical approach. However, to derive the Wheeler-DeWitt equation from the path integral, most authors make the assumption about asymptotic states, that again contradicts the supposition of arbitrary spacetime topology. The extended phase space formalism is entirely based on the path integral approach. Note that if one refuses the assumption about asymptotic states, one cannot prove the gauge invariance of the path integral, and the Wheeler-DeWitt equation loses its sense. In the alternative approach, one derives the Schrodinger equation instead. Thus, the extended phase space approach is really beyond the Wheeler-DeWitt approach. The features of this alternative approach are explored with special emphasis on conclusions that cannot be obtained by using the Wheeler-DeWitt quantum geometrodynamics.

*Yuna Gouin,Sugumi Kanno,Jiro Soda*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在旋转波近似下精确求解引力子-声子量子动力学，发现相干态下的转换以间歇性窄爆发形式发生，压缩态下的转换在初期增长后受到强烈抑制，这些非微扰效应可为单引力子探测提供量子特征信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微扰论预测的引力子-声子转换概率在相干或压缩参数较大时会超过单位性（unitarity）边界，违反量子力学的概率守恒。因此需要超越微扰论，精确求解该量子动力学过程。

Method: 在旋转波近似（rotating-wave approximation）下精确求解引力子-声子量子动力学方程，针对初始相干态（coherent state）和初始压缩态（squeezed state）分别进行分析。

Result: 初始相干态下，转换呈间歇性窄爆发（narrow bursts）模式，爆发之间被强烈抑制区间隔开；初始压缩态下，非微扰行为更早出现，转换在初期增长后受到强烈抑制。

Conclusion: 这些非微扰效应可作为量子引力子-声子动力学的特征信号，对单引力子探测（single-graviton detection）具有潜在意义。

Abstract: A graviton can be converted into a phonon in a resonant bar detector. First-order perturbation theory predicts a strong enhancement of this conversion for coherent and squeezed graviton states, but the probability can exceed unity when the coherent or squeezing parameter is large. Since a conversion probability must satisfy the unitarity bound, we solve the graviton-phonon quantum dynamics exactly within the rotating-wave approximation. For an initial coherent state, we find that the conversion occurs intermittently through narrow bursts separated by intervals of strong suppression. For an initial squeezed state, the departure from perturbative behavior occurs earlier, and the conversion is strongly suppressed after its initial growth. These effects may provide signatures of quantum graviton-phonon dynamics relevant to single-graviton detection.

### [66] [Cosmological horizon thermodynamics in Gauss-Bonnet quasi-dilaton Massive Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20112)
*Sobhan Kazempour,Orlando Luongo,Sabahat,Sichun Sun,Chengye Yu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了Gauss-Bonnet准膨胀大质量引力（Gauss-Bonnet quasi-dilaton massive gravity）中宇宙学表观视界（apparent horizon）的热力学性质，推导了修正的弗里德曼方程，分析了平衡态与非平衡态下的热力学定律，并验证了全息熵界（holographic entropy bound）的稳健性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过推导修正的弗里德曼方程并将其改写成标准形式，分别从平衡态和非平衡态两个角度分析表观视界的热力学第一定律与第二定律，并检验全息熵界在不同宇宙学时期（包含尘埃主导时期）的成立条件。

Result: 平衡态描述下，第一定律保持传统形式并沿用Bekenstein-Hawking面积律（area law），广义第二定律在零能量条件（null energy condition）下成立；非平衡态下，Wald熵（Wald entropy）受Gauss-Bonnet耦合修正，第一定律出现额外项。全息熵界在采用真实物理流体温度时在所有宇宙学时期稳健成立，且约束条件$ξ(σ)\ge0$与先前张量扰动稳定性分析兼容。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic properties of the cosmological apparent horizon in Gauss-Bonnet quasi-dilaton massive gravity. We derive the modified Friedmann equations and reformulate them in standard form, thereby allowing us to study the first and second laws of thermodynamics for the apparent horizon. Both equilibrium and non-equilibrium states are considered. In the equilibrium description, the first law retains the conventional form with the Bekenstein-Hawking area law for the horizon entropy, and we show that the generalized second law is satisfied under the null energy condition. In the non-equilibrium description, the Wald entropy receives a correction from the Gauss-Bonnet coupling, and the first law acquires an additional term associated with using the Wald entropy representation of the Gauss-Bonnet sector. We demonstrate that the total entropy change is non-negative provided the null energy condition, the positive horizon temperature condition, and the Gauss-Bonnet positivity constraints $ξ(σ)\ge0$ are simultaneously satisfied. Furthermore, we investigate the holographic entropy bound $S_{\text{inside}} \le S_{\text{horizon}}$. We demonstrate that while the idealized local thermal equilibrium assumption leads to a formal saturation or apparent breakdown during dust-dominated eras, the bound is robustly preserved across all cosmological epochs when utilizing realistic physical fluid temperatures. The condition $ξ(σ)\ge0$ is shown to be compatible with the stability constraints derived from tensor perturbations in our previous work. Our results establish that Gauss-Bonnet quasi-dilaton massive gravity is a consistent modified gravity theory from the perspective of horizon thermodynamics and the holographic principle.

### [67] [Parity-violating spatially covariant gravity at total derivative order $d=5$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20317)
*Jin-Jian Song,Xian Gao*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文将宇称破坏的空间协变引力（SCG）的多项式构造推广到总导数阶 $d=5$，通过约化得到59个基元，并分析了包含时间导数项的扇区，揭示了在宇宙学背景下的张量扰动性质，包括与螺旋度相关的修正和光速相位速度的条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在空间协变引力（spatially covariant gravity, SCG）框架中，系统性构造宇称破坏（parity-violating）的高阶导数项，以研究其在宇宙学扰动和引力波传播中的效应。

Method: 将单项式按 $(d_{\mathrm{t}},d_{\mathrm{s}})$ 分类（$d_{\mathrm{t}}$ 和 $d_{\mathrm{s}}$ 分别为时间和空间导数的数量），利用分部积分（integration by parts）、张量对称性、三维曲率恒等式、Schouten 恒等式（Schouten identity）和 Cayley-Hamilton 关系进行简化，最终在 $(0,5)$、$(2,3)$ 和 $(4,1)$ 扇区分别得到 2、40 和 17 个基元，总计 59 个基元。进一步将基元分为三类：不含 $\mathcal{L}_{\bm{u}}\ln N$ 和 $\mathcal{L}_{\bm{u}}K_{ij}$ 的35个单项式、11个含时间导数（lapse velocity）的单项式，以及13个含空间度量更高阶法向导数的单项式。

Result: 在空间平坦宇宙学背景（spatially flat cosmological background）下，无加速度的显式一阶时间导数扇区包含16个基元，其二次作用量仅依赖于四个系数组合。这些组合在动能和梯度函数中产生与 $k/a$ 和 $(k/a)^3$ 成正比的螺旋度奇（helicity-odd）修正。推导出两个关系式，使得两种圆偏振（circular polarization）的相位速度均为光速，同时仍允许与螺旋度相关的动能归一化和阻尼。

Conclusion: 该构造为宇称破坏的空间协变引力在 $d=5$ 阶提供了完整的基元系统，揭示了张量扰动中与螺旋度相关的修正行为，并给出了保持光速相位速度的理论约束条件，有助于后续研究宇称破坏效应对引力波传播的影响。

Abstract: We extend the polynomial construction of parity-violating spatially covariant gravity (SCG) to total derivative order $d=5$, where $d=d_{\mathrm{t}}+d_{\mathrm{s}}$ counts the total number of temporal and spatial derivatives. After organizing the monomials by $(d_{\mathrm{t}},d_{\mathrm{s}})$ and reducing them using integrations by parts, tensor symmetries, three-dimensional curvature identities, the Schouten identity, and the Cayley-Hamilton relation, we obtain a $59$-element basis: $2$, $40$, and $17$ monomials in the sectors $(0,5)$, $(2,3)$, and $(4,1)$, respectively. A direct inspection separates $35$ monomials containing neither the lapse velocity $\mathcal{L}_{\bm{u}}\ln N$ nor $\mathcal{L}_{\bm{u}}K_{ij}$ from $11$ lapse-velocity monomials and $13$ monomials containing higher normal derivatives of the spatial metric. The latter two sectors require a dedicated degeneracy analysis. For tensor perturbations about a spatially flat cosmological background, the acceleration-free part of the manifestly first-order-in-time sector contains $16$ basis elements, whose quadratic action depends on only four combinations of coefficients. These combinations generate helicity-odd corrections proportional to $k/a$ and $(k/a)^3$ in the kinetic and gradient functions. We derive two relations that enforce luminal phase velocity for both circular polarizations while still allowing helicity-dependent kinetic normalization and damping.

</details>


### [68] [Critical analysis of some weak-field Weyl conformal gravity solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20381)
*Miguel Yulo Asuncion,Reinosuke Kusano*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文指出，由于在弱场极限下使用了二阶泊松方程而非正确的四阶泊松方程，多篇已发表文献中关于共形引力（Conformal Gravity, CG）弱场解的结果存在错误。此外，还指出了这些推导中将已知CG（电）真空解误用于描述物质分布内部等其他不一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 共形引力（Conformal Gravity, CG）的场方程涉及度规的四阶导数，在弱场极限下应导出四阶泊松方程（fourth-order Poisson equation）。然而，Tanhayi等人、Payandeh与Fathi以及Fathi等人的系列工作却使用了二阶泊松方程来推导CG的弱场近似解。本文旨在指出并纠正这些错误推导。

Method: 本文通过理论分析，对比广义相对论（General Relativity, GR）与共形引力在弱场极限下的行为差异：GR的二阶场方程约化为二阶泊松方程，而CG的四阶场方程应约化为四阶泊松方程。基于这一基本事实，对相关文献中使用的错误方程进行逐一比对和指正。

Result: 明确证明相关文献中给出的共形引力弱场解是错误的，根本原因在于使用了不恰当的二阶泊松方程（second-order Poisson equation）替代了正确的四阶泊松方程。此外，还发现了其他推导不一致性，例如将已知的CG（电）真空解（CG (electro)vacuum solutions）错误地用于描述物质分布（matter distributions）的内部。

Conclusion: 相关文献中声称的共形引力弱场解在数学推导上存在根本性错误，不应被接受为正确的CG解。CG的弱场近似必须基于四阶泊松方程进行求解。

Abstract: The field equations of Conformal Gravity (CG) are constructed from fourth-order derivatives of the metric. While the second-order field equations of General Relativity (GR) reduce to a second-order Poisson equation in the weak-field limit, those of CG yield a fourth-order one. Despite this, works by Tanhayi, Fathi, and Takook [Mod. Phys. Lett. A 26, 2403 (2011)], Payandeh and Fathi [Int. J. Th. Phys. 51, 2227 (2012)], and Fathi, Olivares, and Villanueva [Galaxies 9, 43 (2021)] use second-order Poisson equations to generate purported solutions to CG in a weak-field limit. We demonstrate that these solutions are erroneous due to the use of second-order Poisson equations instead of appropriate fourth-order ones. We also point out other inconsistencies in the derivations of these metrics, such as the assertion that known CG (electro)vacuum solutions describe the interiors of matter distributions.

</details>

### [69] [Vanishing spin stiffness in weakly disordered two-dimensional Heisenberg ferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20036)
*Jacopo Niedda,Aldo Coraggio,Giacomo Bracci-Testasecca,Antonello Scardicchio*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索少量反铁磁键（antiferromagnetic bonds）对二维海森堡铁磁体（Heisenberg ferromagnet）长波长动力学的定性影响，分析弱键阻挫（bond frustration）如何在短程微观无序下改变系统的集体行为。

Method: 采用复本场论（replica field theory）计算来刻画有效无序强度的粗粒化演化与自旋刚度的重正化行为；同时通过半经典自旋波哈密顿量（semiclassical spin-wave Hamiltonian）的数值对角化来验证低能标度的异常行为。

Result: 少量的反铁磁键导致局域自旋刚度出现对数相关的空间涨落；有效无序强度随粗粒化过程增长，自旋刚度下降；产生尺度依赖的动态临界指数（dynamical exponent）z > 2，即异常软的磁振子；数值结果确认了低能标度的异常行为。

Conclusion: 系统在重正化群（renormalization group）流中趋于无限无序、零刚度的极端无序相，表明弱键阻挫足以从根本上改变二维铁磁体的长波长动力学。

Abstract: We show that a small fraction of antiferromagnetic bonds qualitatively alters the long-wavelength dynamics of two-dimensional Heisenberg ferromagnets. Although the classical ground state remains magnetized, weak bond frustration generates logarithmically correlated spatial fluctuations of the local spin stiffness, despite the microscopic disorder being short ranged. A replica field theory calculation shows that the effective disorder strength grows under coarse graining, while the spin stiffness decreases, yielding anomalously soft magnons with a scale-dependent dynamical exponent $z > 2$. Numerical diagonalization of the semiclassical spin-wave Hamiltonian confirms the anomalous low-energy scaling. The flow is toward an infinite-disorder, zero stiffness regime.

Abstract: We critically assess the performance of an autoregressive generative neural network model by applying it to an antiferromagnetic Ising model on a random regular graph. We train the network on equilibrium configurations in the low-temperature spin-glass phase of the model and perform Monte Carlo simulations using spin configurations generated by the network. The relaxation time of the Monte Carlo simulations drastically decreases with increasing the size of the training dataset and converges to an optimal value. The dynamical exponent characterizing the growth of the optimal relaxation time as a function of the system size is slightly reduced compared to the local Monte Carlo dynamics. However, we find that the size of the training dataset to achieve the optimal performance grows much faster with the system size than the relaxation time, implying that the total training cost eventually hinders a practical use of the method at large system sizes.

### [71] [Core and valence photoemission spectra of atoms and molecules from a multichannel Dyson equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20070)
*Stefano Paggi,J. Arjan Berger,Pina Romaniello*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文发展了多通道戴森方程（multichannel Dyson equation）的高效数值方法，用于原子与分子光电子能谱（photoemission spectra）的从头算（ab initio）模拟。通过与完全组态相互作用（full configuration interaction）及GW方法对比，证明该方法对shake-up过程产生的卫星峰（satellite features）描述显著优于GW。此外，讨论了卫星能量随基组大小的缓慢收敛问题，并提出一种简单的完备基组极限外推方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用多通道戴森方程（multichannel Dyson equation）进行光电子能谱的从头算模拟；引入一种数值高效（numerically efficient）的方法计算谱函数（spectral function）。通过与完全组态相互作用及GW方法的结果进行对比验证；针对基组收敛问题，提出一种简单的完备基组极限外推方法（extrapolation method）。

Result: 多通道戴森方程对因shake-up过程产生的卫星特征（satellite features）的描述显著优于GW方法。此外，卫星能量（satellite energies）随基组增大的收敛速度较慢，但所提出的外推方法可有效逼近完备基组极限。

Conclusion: 多通道戴森方程是一种比GW更精确的光电子能谱模拟工具，尤其在处理多电子关联效应的卫星结构方面。同时，基组收敛问题可通过外推方法缓解，为实际计算提供了可行方案。

Abstract: We recently presented multichannel Dyson equations for the \textit{ab initio} simulation of various spectroscopies. In particular, we introduced a multichannel Dyson equation for the description of photoemission spectra. In this work, we apply our approach to the simulation of photoemission spectra of atoms and molecules. We introduce a numerically efficient approach to calculate their spectral functions. We compare the spectra obtained within the multichannel Dyson equation to those obtained with full configuration interaction and the $GW$ method. We are thus able to show that the satellite features due to shake-up processes are significantly better described by the multichannel Dyson equation than by $GW$. Finally, we also discuss the slow convergence of the satellite energies with the size of the basis set and we propose a simple extrapolation method to reach the complete basis-set limit.
