### [72] [Quantum geometry and critical temperature enhancement in MgB$_2$ superconductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19458)
*Yi Jiang,Haoyu Hu,Dumitru Călugăru,Kaja H. Hiorth,Junze Deng,Hanqi Pi,Handong Chen,Maia G. Vergniory,Ion Errea,Emilia Morosan,Leslie M. Schoop,Claudia Felser,Miguel A. L. Marques,Päivi Törmä,Daniel Agterberg,B. Andrei Bernevig*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文以最小化第一性原理输入，对MgB₂的电子结构、声子及电声耦合（EPC）建立了紧凑解析模型；揭示了键中心Kagome晶格导致的受阻带结构、量子几何效应，并证明掺杂下EPC增强主要源于量子几何贡献，为理解MgB₂的超导性及量子几何在声子介导超导体中的作用提供了对称性清晰的理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对记录高温临界温度T_c ≈ 39 K的声子介导超导体MgB₂，建立一个兼顾电子、声子及其耦合的全面理论，且仅依赖最少的从头算（ab initio）输入，从而以透明、基于对称性的方式解释其超导机制。

Method: 构建MgB₂电子结构、声子及电声耦合（electron-phonon coupling, EPC）的紧凑解析模型；结合第一性原理（ab initio）计算验证掺杂效应；采用高斯近似处理EPC张量，以分离几何贡献。

Result: 发现面内B sp²强键合形成受阻带结构（obstructed band structure），其自然描述为键中心Kagome晶格（bond-centered kagome lattice），产生准二维σ带费米面圆柱及显著量子几何效应（quantum-geometric effects）。仅Γ点键伸缩模式可通过对称性耦合至σ费米面，主导EPC。轻电子掺杂下，EPC矩阵元增强超过态密度减少，导致T_c提升；该增强主要源于量子几何贡献。

Conclusion: 研究提供了基于对称性的MgB₂超导性清晰解释，并指出量子几何效应（quantum-geometric effects）对声子介导超导体掺杂趋势具有关键塑造作用。

Abstract: MgB$_2$, a phonon-mediated superconductor with record-high critical temperature $T_c\simeq 39$ K, is revisited to obtain a comprehensive theory of electrons, phonons, and their coupling with minimal ab initio input. We construct compact analytic models for the electronic structure, phonons, and electron-phonon coupling (EPC) of MgB$_2$. We show that strong in-plane B $sp^2$ bonding realizes an obstructed band structure whose natural description is a bond-centered kagome lattice, yielding small quasi-2D $σ$-band Fermi-surface cylinders and pronounced quantum-geometric effects. The phonon spectrum is found to closely track that of a graphene-like boron layer, but the heavy intercalated Mg atoms dominate the three acoustic branches and rigidly lift the boron modes into the optical sector, while the in-plane B-B bond-stretching mode exhibits a pronounced softening along $Γ$-A. By symmetry, this $Γ$-point bond-stretching mode is the only $Γ$ phonon that can couple to the $σ$ Fermi surface, explaining its dominant contribution to the EPC. Upon electron doping toward the doubly degenerate band edge of the $σ$ sheets, we find that a reduced density of states competes with enhanced EPC matrix elements. At light electron doping, ab initio calculations show that the EPC enhancement dominates, leading to an increase in $T_c$ (within the clean doping limit without disorder effects). Using the Gaussian approximation for the EPC tensor, we further show that this enhancement is overwhelmingly quantum geometric in origin, arising from a geometric EPC contribution of the small $σ$ Fermi surface peaked at $Γ$. Overall, our results provide a transparent, symmetry-based account of superconductivity in MgB$_2$ and suggest that quantum-geometric effects can be essential for shaping doping trends in phonon-mediated superconductors.

</details>


### [73] [Power-Law Suppression of Superfluid Stiffness in High-Kinetic-Inductance NbN Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20096)
*Meenakshi Sharma,Hrishikesh Borah,Sandeep Singh,Berit H. Goodge,Edouard Lesne,Sandra Nestler,Surinder P. Singh,Haolin Jin,Yejin Lee,Bernd Büchner,Uri Vool*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过超薄NbN微波谐振器（厚度低至2.8 nm，面动能电感高达300 pH/sq）研究了无序对超导薄膜电动力学的影响，发现超流刚度（superfluid stiffness）在低温下呈现幂律压制，偏离Mattis-Bardeen理论，并识别出超流刚度与配对能之比Θ(0)/Tc是区分相位涨落主导与能隙主导超导电动力学的关键参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无序超薄超导膜虽能实现高动能电感（kinetic inductance）以构建紧凑高阻抗量子电路，但会削弱相位刚性（phase rigidity）并引发反常电动力学。本文旨在系统探究这一权衡如何改变超导响应，并揭示其背后的物理机制。

Method: 采用NbN微波谐振器，厚度低至2.8 nm、面动能电感高达300 pH/sq，结合输运测量、微波响应测量及截面透射电子显微镜（cross-sectional transmission electron microscopy）表征微结构。

Result: 在超薄薄膜中，输运显示Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless转变特征；微波响应呈现低温超流刚度幂律压制，与Mattis-Bardeen理论不符。随厚度增加，该反常行为被逐步压制，向常规能隙主导电动力学连续交叉。截面透射电子显微镜显示纳米晶孪晶畴结构（nanocrystalline twin-domain structure）。

Conclusion: 无序超薄膜中超导电动力学的相涨落主导与能隙主导之间的交叉由超流刚度与配对能之比Θ(0)/Tc控制，该比值可作为区分两类电动力学行为的特征参数。

Abstract: Disorder is a powerful route to high kinetic inductance in superconducting ultrathin films, enabling compact high-impedance quantum circuits. This functionality, however, comes at the cost of reduced phase rigidity and potentially anomalous electrodynamics. Here, we use NbN microwave resonators with thicknesses down to 2.8 nm and sheet kinetic inductance up to 300 pH per square to probe how this trade-off reshapes the superconducting response. In the thinnest films, transport shows signatures of a Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless transition, while the microwave response reveals a pronounced low-temperature power-law suppression of the superfluid stiffness, inconsistent with Mattis-Bardeen theory. With increasing thickness, this anomalous regime is progressively suppressed, marking a continuous crossover toward conventional, gap-dominated electrodynamics. Cross-sectional transmission electron microscopy reveals a nanocrystalline twin-domain structure, pointing to oriented microstructural disorder as a crucial factor in the observed response. Overall, the crossover is governed by the ratio of superfluid stiffness to pairing energy, Theta(0)/Tc, identifying this ratio as a parameter governing the boundary between phase-fluctuation-dominated and gap-dominated superconducting electrodynamics in disordered nanofilms.

</details>


### [74] [Stacking-tuned superconductivity and competing charge-density-wave states in NbSe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20335)
*Sandra Sajan,Xinze Yang,Haojie Guo,Tarushi Agarwal,Samuel Mañas-Valero,Carla Boix-Constant,Eugenio Coronado,Fernando de Juan,Eduardo H. da Silva Neto,Ravi P. Singh,Maria N. Gastiasoro,Miguel M. Ugeda*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过高分辨扫描隧道显微镜和能谱学发现，仅通过改变堆叠顺序（stacking sequence）即可在NbSe₂中定性改变电荷密度波（charge density wave, CDW）和超导序（superconducting order），而不改变面内原子结构。4Ha-NbSe₂中存在两种相互竞争的CDW态（单向公度的1Q^C相和三角非公度的3Q^I相），CDW相边界处存在涡旋（vortices）以容纳动量失配，且超导性也受堆叠方式重塑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 堆叠方式（layer stacking）作为调控范德华（van der Waals）材料中集体量子序的一种有效但尚未充分探索的手段，本文旨在探究仅改变堆叠顺序是否能定性改变电荷序和超导序，而不改变面内原子结构。

Method: 采用高分辨扫描隧道显微镜和扫描隧道能谱学（high-resolution scanning tunneling microscopy and spectroscopy），对NbSe₂的4Ha和2H两种多型体（polytypes）进行对比研究，并引入相位分辨分析（phase-resolved analysis）直接映射CDW相位的梯度。

Result: 4Ha-NbSe₂中不存在2H-NbSe₂中常见的三角非公度3Q^I序，而是存在两种竞争的CDW态：单向公度1Q^C相和三角非公度3Q^I相，两者之间动量失配δ=Q^I−Q^C。相位边界处存在与局部应变无显著关联的涡旋，通过2π相位突变容纳动量失配δ。两种多型体均表现出多带配对（multiband pairing）的超导性，但堆叠重塑了超导序。

Conclusion: 堆叠顺序可作为独立于面内原子结构的自由度，定性调控范德华材料中的电荷序和超导序；CDW涡旋为不同电荷序的共存提供了机制。

Abstract: Layer stacking provides a powerful yet underexplored route for reshaping collective quantum order in van der Waals materials. Here we use high-resolution scanning tunneling microscopy and spectroscopy to show that the stacking sequence alone can qualitatively transform the charge density and superconducting orders in NbSe$_2$, while preserving the same in-plane atomic structure. Comparing the 4Ha and 2H polytypes, we find that, unlike the ubiquitous triangular incommensurate $3Q^\mathrm{I}$ order of 2H-NbSe$_2$, 4Ha-NbSe$_2$ hosts two competing CDW states with no measurable correlation with local strain: a unidirectional commensurate $1Q^\mathrm{C}$ phase and a triangular incommensurate $3Q^\mathrm{I}$ phase, with $Q^\mathrm{I}=Q^\mathrm{C}+δ$. We introduce a phase-resolved analysis that directly maps the gradient of the CDW phases and reveals vortices bound to the $1Q^\mathrm{C}$ - $3Q^\mathrm{I}$ phase boundaries. These vortices accommodate the momentum mismatch $δ$ through abrupt $2π$ phase slips, providing a mechanism by which distinct charge orders coexist. Superconductivity is also reshaped by stacking, while both polytypes exhibit multiband pairing.

</details>


### [75] [Exact static exchange benchmark for the uniform electron gas: Dynamic-kernel tests and exchange-correlation cancellation near 2kF](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20403)
*Carl A. Kukkonen*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过精确的交换-局域场因子解析形式（universal exchange-only local field factor）解释了均匀电子气（uniform electron gas）中两个长期未解的静态局域场特征：G_+ 在高达约 2k_F 范围内几乎严格按 q^2 增长，以及费米面（Fermi surface）的剧烈 2k_F 物理仅留下微弱痕迹。解析基准揭示这些特征源于交换-关联强抵消效应（exchange-correlation cancellation），并对现有数值结果（BDL 1980、Nazarov & Silkin 2024）进行了精度评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 均匀电子气的静态局域场因子（static local field factor）虽可通过量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo, QMC）计算精确获得，但其两个最显著特征——G_+ 在接近 2k_F 范围内近乎严格地按 q^2 增长，以及费米面处剧烈的 2k_F 物理仅在其中留下微弱痕迹——一直缺乏机理性解释。

Method: 将教科书的一阶局域场关系（first-order local-field relation）与精确的静态交换极化率（static exchange polarizability）结合，推导出通用交换-局域场因子 G_x(q,0) 的紧凑精确解析形式：G_x(q,0) = -I(Q)Q^2/L(Q)^2，其中 Q = q/2k_F。在此基础上对 QMC 局域场因子进行自旋分辨分解（spin-resolved decomposition），以精确基线为参考分析交换-关联抵消效应。

Result: G_x 在小 q 极限下为 (1/4)(q/k_F)^2，在 2k_F 处为 π²/6，在大 q 极限下为 1/3，并给出非极化气体的交换-自旋平均接触值 g(0)=1/2。G_x 在 1.9685k_F 处达到有限最大值 1.9924，且在 2k_F 处以 diverging ln³|q-2k_F| 斜率通过 π²/6。BDL 1980 表格在 1.5k_F 以下精度约 1%，而 Nazarov & Silkin 2024 的 McLachlan 变分核（McLachlan-variational kernel）仅在 0.5k_F 以下达到 2% 精度，在 2k_F 处偏低 1.74 倍。在 QMC 最接近 2k_F 的点（q=2.01k_F, r_s=2）处，关联抵消了精确交换值 1.33 中的 0.43(7)。

Conclusion: 两个长期未解的特征均可归结于强交换-关联抵消效应。由封闭解析形式导出的静态交换核阈值（static exchange-kernel thresholds）以 0.2% 的精度重现了 1980 年数值计算和 2014 年恢复的有限波矢电荷阈值（charge threshold）r_s ≈ 10.6（近 q=1.94k_F 处）。

Abstract: The static local field factors of the uniform electron gas are known accurately from quantum Monte Carlo (QMC) calculations, but two of their most striking features have lacked a mechanism: $G_+$ grows almost exactly as $q^2$ up to nearly $2k_F$, and the violent $2k_F$ physics of the Fermi surface leaves only a faint trace in it. Combining the textbook first-order local-field relation with the exact static exchange polarizability gives a compact exact benchmark: the universal exchange-only local field factor $G_x(q,0) = -I(Q)Q^2/L(Q)^2$, $Q = q/2k_F$, with exact values $(1/4)(q/k_F)^2$ at small $q$, $π^2/6$ at $2k_F$ -- apparently never before stated as a local-field value -- and $1/3$ at large $q$, giving the exchange-only spin-averaged contact value $g(0) = 1/2$ of the unpolarized gas (BDL 1977). $G_x$ rises to a finite maximum of 1.9924 at $1.9685k_F$ and passes through $π^2/6$ at exactly $2k_F$ with a slope diverging as $\ln^3|q-2k_F|$. Against this benchmark, the 1980 BDL tabulation is accurate to about one percent below $1.5k_F$, while the 2024 McLachlan-variational kernel of Nazarov and Silkin is two-percent accurate only below $0.5k_F$, is a factor of 1.74 low at $2k_F$, and its large-q limit is inconsistent with the contact constraint. A spin-resolved decomposition of QMC local field factors about the exact baseline shows that, within the resolution and smoothness assumptions of the QMC-based representations, both features follow from a strong exchange-correlation cancellation: at the QMC point closest to $2k_F$ ($q = 2.01k_F$, $r_s = 2$), correlation cancels 0.43(7) of the exact exchange value 1.33. Computed consistently at each wavevector, the static exchange-kernel thresholds derived from the closed form reproduce, to 0.2%, the finite-wavevector charge threshold $r_s \approx 10.6$ near $q = 1.94k_F$ obtained numerically in 1980, and recovered again in 2014.

</details>

### [76] [Four, One, and None: Quantifying the Ultra-High-Energy Neutrino Anomaly Across ANITA-IV, KM3NeT, and IceCube](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19487)
*Dibya S. Chattopadhyay,Carlos A. Argüelles,Vedran Brdar*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 对ANITA-IV四个近水平中微子事件和KM3NeT的KM3-230213A超高能径迹事件进行联合分析，发现其在弥漫全天空通量模型下与IceCube零结果存在约7.5σ的张力；即使引入稀有时变瞬变源假说，张力仍无法在标准模型框架内被消除（最低5.9σ）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ANITA-IV探测到的四个近水平中微子事件（near-horizon neutrino-like events）以及KM3NeT观测到的超高能径迹事件（ultra-high-energy track-like event）KM3-230213A所隐含的中微子事件率，与IceCube未观测到对应事件这一事实存在明显冲突，需要进行定量一致性检验。

Method: 构建了三个探测器（ANITA-IV、KM3NeT和IceCube）的半解析（semi-analytic）、依赖于能量和方向的等效面积（effective area），并考虑了ANITA-IV和KM3NeT的时间依赖曝光（time-dependent exposure）。在弥漫全天空功率律谱（diffuse all-sky power-law flux）假设下同时调节归一化（normalization）和谱指数（spectral index）进行联合分析；随后引入短时标瞬变源（short-duration transients）和稀有时变源（rare transients）假说进行大规模蒙特卡罗（Monte Carlo）模拟。

Result: 弥漫全天空通量模型的最佳拟合（best-fit configuration）与观测数据存在约7.5σ的张力，该方案预测约5个IceCube事件，但严重低估ANITA-IV和KM3NeT的计数。若事件来源于恰好沿观测方向且在探测窗口内发生的短时标瞬变源，张力可大幅缓解，但该方案高度精细调节（fine-tuned）。对稀有时变源随机分布的全天空蒙特卡罗模拟，在产生4个ANITA-IV有利瞬变源概率约10⁻⁴的基准群体（benchmark population）中，最佳拟合仍保持5.9σ张力。

Conclusion: 在标准模型（Standard Model）框架下，无论是弥漫全天空通量假设还是稀有时变源假说，仅靠方向和时间上的变化均无法调和ANITA-IV和KM3NeT的观测与IceCube零结果之间的冲突。

Abstract: The four near-horizon neutrino-like events reported by ANITA-IV and the ultra-high-energy track-like event KM3-230213A observed by KM3NeT imply neutrino event rates that are in tension with the absence of corresponding events at IceCube. In this work, we perform a joint analysis of these events, taking into account the absence of any corresponding ones at IceCube. We construct semi-analytic, energy- and direction-dependent effective areas for the three detectors and account for the time-dependent ANITA-IV and KM3NeT exposures. For a diffuse all-sky power-law flux varying both the normalization and the spectral index, the measured event rates across the three detectors are not reproduced. The best-fit configuration, corresponding to a tension of $\sim7.5σ$, predicts approximately five IceCube events while strongly underpredicting the ANITA-IV and KM3NeT counts. In contrast to the diffuse scenario, the tension can be substantially alleviated if the events arise from short-duration transients that occur exactly along the observed directions during the ANITA-IV and KM3NeT detection windows. Such a realization, however, is highly fine-tuned. If rare transients are instead distributed randomly across the full sky over the $\sim15$-year IceCube observation period, additional sources inevitably contribute to the IceCube exposure. For benchmark populations with a probability of approximately $10^{-4}$ to produce four favorable transients at ANITA-IV, the best-fit configuration of sources, out of $10^5$ Monte Carlo realizations, remains in $5.9σ$ tension. We conclude that, within the Standard Model, directional and temporal variations alone can not reconcile the ANITA-IV and KM3NeT observations with the IceCube null result, under both a diffuse all-sky flux and a rare-transient source hypothesis.

### [77] [Resolving Galactic and Cluster Dynamics Without Dark Matter: Tsallis Entropy as the Unique Foundation of Emergent Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19435)
*S. Shamari,A. Sheykhi*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文论证在熵引力（entropic gravity）框架下，为同时解释星系、星系团和球状星团等不同尺度的观测数据，必须唯一选择Tsallis熵作为广义熵公式；研究还发现非广延参数（nonextensive parameter）与引力系统的宏观量无相关性，并预言存在无需暗物质的星系团。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Barrow、Tsallis、Kaniadakis等修正熵模型已在宇宙学领域被广泛探索，但它们在星系尺度上的影响尚未得到充分检验；本文旨在系统测试不同广义熵公式在星系旋转曲线和星系团重子质量上的表现，并填补从星系到星系团再到球状星团的结构层级验证空白。

Method: 将熵力（entropic force）框架应用于星系旋转曲线和星系团的重子质量（baryonic mass），以此筛选出唯一合适的广义熵公式——Tsallis熵；随后将Tsallis修正引力推广至球状星团，完成从星系到星系团再到球状星团的结构层级检验，并分析非广延参数与系统宏观量的相关性。

Result: Tsallis熵是被熵力框架唯一选择的广义熵公式；非广延参数δ与引力系统的质量、半径、温度或密度等宏观量均无相关性；预言存在δ=1的星系团——即其动力学不需要暗物质，类似于已在星系和球状星团尺度上观测到的δ=1系统。

Conclusion: 为在从球状星团到星系再到星系团的所有尺度上与观测数据保持一致，熵引力范式必然建立在Tsallis熵之上；δ=1星系团的预言为区分Tsallis引力与ΛCDM模型及MOND提供了独特的观测检验。

Abstract: While modified entropy models-such as Barrow, Tsallis, Kaniadakis,Power-law, Logarithmic, and Rényi entropies-have been widely explored in cosmological contexts, their implications on galactic scales remain largely untested. These generalizations of the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy encode quantum gravitational, nonextensive, or fractal spacetime effects and can alter the gravitational entropy-area relation. In this paper, we demonstrate that the entropic force framework, when applied to galactic rotation curves and the baryonic mass of galaxy clusters, uniquely selects Tsallis entropy as the specific generalized entropy formulation. We then extend this Tsallis modified gravity to globular clusters to complete the structural hierarchy from galaxies to galaxy clusters to globular clusters and to investigate its behavior as a function of system scale. We will show that the nonextensive parameter exhibits no correlation with any of the macroscopic quantities characterizing gravitational systems, such as mass, radius, temperature, or density. Furthermore, it has previously been shown that entropy is not well-defined within the standard thermodynamic approach to gravity. The adoption of nonextensive statistics provides a foundation for entanglement, thereby enabling a consistent definition of entanglement entropy. We predict the existence of galaxy clusters with $δ= 1$ (i.e., clusters whose dynamics require no dark matter) analogous to $δ= 1$ systems already observed at galactic and globular cluster scales. This prediction provides a unique observational test to discriminate Tsallis gravity from $Λ$CDM and MOND. Therefore, for the entropic gravity paradigm to be consistent with observational data across all scales-from globular clusters to galaxies to galaxy clusters-it is inevitably required to be built upon \textit{Tsallis} entropy.

### [78] [Local morphology and asymmetry of galactic rotation curves in a kinetic gas transport framework: NGC 3198](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19505)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 分别使用NGC 3198星系靠近侧（north-eastern side, 东北侧）和远离侧（south-western side, 西南侧）的观测HI密度分布剖面（density profiles），基于Lipovka (2022) 推导的方程重构对应的旋转曲线（rotation curves）。

Result: 重构曲线不仅复现了观测旋转曲线近似平坦的大尺度行为（approximately flat large-scale behaviour），还分别再现了银河盘东北侧和西南侧详细的局部形态（local morphology）和非对称性（asymmetry）。

Conclusion: 星系旋转曲线的局部结构（local structure）与局域HI分布（local HI distribution）紧密相关，是银河盘中气体动理学输运过程（kinetic gas transport processes）的自然结果。

Abstract: We investigate whether the observed fine structure and asymmetry of non-averaged galactic rotation curves can be reconstructed directly from the observed HI distribution within the framework of a kinetic gas transport description. Using the observed HI density profiles separately for the approaching (north-eastern) side and the receding (south-western) side of the galaxy NGC~3198, we reconstruct the corresponding rotation curves based on the equation previously derived in \citet{Lipovka2022}. It is shown that the reconstructed curves reproduce not only the approximately flat large-scale behaviour of the observed rotation curves, but also their detailed local morphology and asymmetry separately for the north-eastern and south-western sides of the galactic disk. The obtained results indicate that the local structure of galactic rotation curves is closely connected with the local HI distribution and arises naturally as a consequence of kinetic gas transport processes in galactic disks.

### [79] [Nucleon unpolarized second Mellin moments using lattice QCD ensembles with physical quark masses and in the continuum limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20337)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在连续极限下提取了Q²=0处的引力形状因子，给出了夸克与胶子对质子动量和角动量的贡献值；并结合相同系综计算的内禀夸克自旋，确定了各夸克味的轨道角动量（orbital angular momentum）。

Abstract: We compute the matrix elements of the energy-momentum tensor of the nucleon using four ensembles of twisted mass clover-improved fermions with the up, down, strange and charm quark masses tuned to approximately their physical values. The four ensembles have similar physical volume and lattice spacings $a=0.080$~fm, $0.068$~fm, $0.057$~fm, and $0.049$ fm, allowing us to take the continuum limit directly at the physical pion mass point. We compute both connected and disconnected quark contributions as well as gluon contributions. All renormalization functions, including the mixing of the quark singlet with the gluon, are determined non-perturbatively. We extract the gravitational form factors in the continuum limit at $Q^2=0$ and evaluate the contribution of quarks and gluons to the momentum and angular momentum of the proton. Using the values of the intrinsic quark spin computed using the same gauge ensembles we also determine the orbital angular momentum for each quark flavor.

### [80] [Cavitation Acoustic Perturbation Equations: A Computational Framework for Source-Resolved Multiphase Hydroacoustics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19567)
*Zhi Cheng,Rajeev K. Jaiman*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种空化声学扰动方程（CAPE）框架，将空化物理直接嵌入声学方程中，用于预测空化流动中的声生成与传播。数值验证基于一维波动问题，应用至圆柱绕流和NACA水翼的空化流后，发现非空化时表现为偶极子辐射，空化时表现为单极子或几何调制辐射，相变项对单极子声源有直接体积贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统声学扰动方程仅适用于单相或弱可压缩流动，无法处理空化（cavitation）引起的多相流噪声问题。本文旨在开发一种能够直接嵌入空化物理的声学框架，弥补现有方法在空化流声预测中的不足。

Method: 推导了空化声学扰动方程（cavitation acoustic perturbation equations, CAPE），将蒸汽质量传递（vapor mass transfer）、混合物可压缩性（mixture compressibility）和压力率效应（pressure-rate effects）统一纳入声学方程。采用完美匹配层（perfectly matched layer）抑制边界反射，并通过一维波动问题验证数值框架的收敛性与衰减特性。

Result: 一维验证表明，解对网格和时间步长细化不敏感，边界反射被有效抑制，衰减符合斯托克斯声衰减定律（Stokes' sound attenuation law）。圆柱和水翼算例显示，非空化时呈偶极子（dipole）辐射，空化时呈单极子（monopole）或几何调制辐射。相变项对单极子声源有直接体积贡献，局部溃灭事件通过压力率源项放大体现。

Conclusion: 所提CAPE框架将声学扰动方法扩展至空化多相流，为海洋和水力应用中的水声预测、声源定位及机理分析提供了一种高效工具。

Abstract: This work develops a cavitation-consistent acoustic perturbation framework for predicting sound generation and propagation in cavitating flows. Unlike conventional acoustic perturbation equations for single-phase or weakly compressible flows, the proposed formulation embeds cavitation physics directly into the acoustic equations. The cavitation acoustic perturbation equations (CAPE) incorporate vapor mass transfer, mixture compressibility, and pressure-rate effects within a unified formulation, allowing cavitation-induced noise sources to be resolved in the computational domain. The numerical framework is verified using one-dimensional wave-propagation problems. The solutions become insensitive to further mesh and time-step refinement, the perfectly matched layer suppresses boundary reflections, and the predicted attenuation over a range of source frequencies follows Stokes' sound attenuation law. The framework is then applied to cavitating flow past a circular cylinder and a NACA hydrofoil. The non-cavitating benchmark shows dipole-like radiation associated with unsteady loading, whereas cavitating cases exhibit monopole-like or geometry-modulated radiation caused by volumetric phase change. Source-term analyses identify tonal frequencies associated with vortex shedding, cavity shedding, and collapse-induced excitation. The phase-change terms provide a direct volumetric contribution to the monopole-like source, while localized collapse events appear through amplification of the pressure-rate source. The proposed framework extends acoustic perturbation methods to cavitating multiphase flows and provides an efficient tool for hydroacoustic prediction, source localization, and mechanism analysis in marine and hydraulic applications.

</details>


### [81] [The spectral picture of self-similar collapse in the Constantin-Lax-Majda equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19762)
*Jie Xu*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文对 Constantin-Lax-Majda (CLM) 方程（广义族中 $a=0$ 的锚点）的自相似坍缩廓线给出了一个谱描述。作者将线性化算子 $L_0$ 视为原点 $H^2$ 空间上的闭算子，证明了其本质谱、点谱、半群衰减率以及离散化谱的实现依赖性，并针对 $a>0$ 情况给出了条件性的两条谱线包含关系和形式标度相关指数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解 Constantin-Lax-Majda (CLM) 方程（$a=0$）自相似坍缩廓线的谱结构，澄清此前未知的本质谱边界、点谱构成以及线性半群的衰减率，并揭示谱实现依赖性对离散化行为的影响。

Method: 对精确自相似廓线 $\Omega(y) = -y/(y^2+1/4)$ 进行线性化，将算子 $L_0$ 作为原点 $H^2$ 空间上的闭算子处理；利用对数展宽 Weyl 序列（log-widening Weyl sequence）放置本质谱的垂直线，通过显式 Hardy-Mellin 预解式界（Hardy-Mellin resolvent bound）排除半平面中除 0 和 1 以外的区域；通过标准调制（standard modulation）移除对称模式以在 $X$ 上获得谱间隙；在有界传递映射（bounded transfer map）到达的共轭变量加权空间上闭式计算线性半群及其精确衰减率 $e^{-\tau/2}$；通过实现二分法（realization dichotomy）识别离散化抹平谱与极大 $L^2$ 实现谱的关系；对 $a>0$ 情况建立条件性两条谱线包含，并重新计算分支 $c_l(a)$ 以交叉检验。

Result: 在 $a=0$ 时，本质谱与闭半平面 $\{\mathrm{Re}\,\lambda \ge -1/2\}$ 仅在单条垂直线 $\{\mathrm{Re}\,\lambda = -1/2\}$ 上相交；全复平面上的点谱（奇数实现）精确为 $\{0,1\}$（标度和时间平移对称模式），无嵌入本征值，去除后谱间隙为 $1/2$；线性半群的精确衰减率为 $e^{-\tau/2}$，但仅在共轭变量加权空间上达成，$X$ 范数下谱间隙不能直接给出衰减率；实现二分法表明离散化的带内抹平谱对应于极大 $L^2$ 实现的谱，而原点 $H^2$ 实现消除了这一谱；对 $a>0$ 建立了条件性的两条谱线包含，并验证了分支 $c_l(a)$，得到形式标度相关指数 $s^*(a) = 1/c_l(a)$。

Conclusion: 自相似坍缩廓线的谱结构高度依赖于算子的实现选择；$L_0$ 的非正规性（non-normality）使得谱间隙本身不足以在 $X$ 范数下直接决定衰减率；对角化离散化必须谨慎处理实现依赖的谱行为；$a>0$ 时的结果给出了分数耗散（fractional dissipation）在自相似变量中渐近次主导的条件。

Abstract: We give a spectral description of the self-similar collapse profile of the Constantin-Lax-Majda (CLM) equation, the $a=0$ anchor of the generalized family $w_t + a\,u\,w_x = u_x\,w$, $u_x = Hw$. Linearizing about the exact profile $Ω(y) = -y/(y^2+1/4)$ and realizing $L_0$ as a closed operator on the origin-$H^2$ space, we prove three things at $a=0$. Its essential spectrum meets the closed half-plane $\{\mathrm{Re}\,λ\ge -1/2\}$ in the single vertical line $\{\mathrm{Re}\,λ= -1/2\}$: the line is placed by a log-widening Weyl sequence, and an explicit Hardy-Mellin resolvent bound constructively empties the rest of the half-plane apart from $0$ and $1$. Its full point spectrum over $\mathbb{C}$, on the odd realization, is exactly $\{0,1\}$, the scaling and time-shift symmetry modes, with no embedded eigenvalues; removing these by the standard modulation leaves a spectral gap of $1/2$ on $X$. The linear semigroup and its exact decay rate $e^{-τ/2}$ are computed in closed form, but on a weighted space of the conjugated variable reached from $X$ by a bounded transfer map; we keep the two separate, since $L_0$ is non-normal and a spectral gap does not by itself give a decay rate in the $X$ norm. A realization dichotomy identifies the in-strip smear of generic discretizations as the faithful spectrum of the maximal $L^2$ realization, which origin-$H^2$ removes. For $a>0$ we prove a conditional two-line inclusion for each admissible smooth focusing profile, recompute the branch $c_l(a)$ of Lushnikov, Silantyev, and Siegel as a cross-check, and record the formal scaling-relevance exponent $s^*(a) = 1/c_l(a)$, below which fractional dissipation is asymptotically subdominant in self-similar variables for fixed sufficiently regular data. The contribution is the realization-dependent spectral picture of the collapse profile itself.

</details>


### [82] [Elastohydrodynamic instability of a spinning elastic disk](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19561)
*Sifan Yin,Paul R. Kaneelil,L. Mahadevan*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个在粘性流体中旋转的软薄弹性圆盘，通过线性化Föppl-von Kármán方程与经典von Kármán涡流的剪切应力耦合，建立了弹性流体动力学稳定性问题。线性稳定性分析揭示了由离心刚化和流体诱导剪切两个无量纲控制参数决定的屈曲阈值，超越阈值后圆盘屈曲成方位向周期性的鞍形模态，并支持逆行的行进波。结果表明流体的剪切作用能使旋转弹性结构失稳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旋转弹性圆盘在流体中的稳定性是工程和物理中的重要问题，而现有研究尚未充分考虑流体剪切诱导失稳的机制。作者旨在通过解析模型揭示离心张力与粘性剪切应力之间的竞争如何导致屈曲失稳。

Method: 将旋转弹性圆盘的线性化Föppl-von Kármán方程与经典的von Kármán涡流（von Kármán swirling flow）产生的剪切应力耦合，构建了一个弹性流体动力学稳定性问题（elastohydrodynamic stability problem），并进行了线性稳定性分析（linear stability analysis）。

Result: 提出了两个无量纲控制参数：离心刚化（centrifugal stiffening）和流体诱导剪切（fluid-induced shear），用于描述失稳阈值。超过阈值后，圆盘屈曲成方位向周期性的鞍形模态（azimuthally periodic saddle-like modes），其波数随旋转张力增大而增加。屈曲构型还支持比材料框架旋转更慢的逆行行进波（retrograde traveling waves）。

Conclusion: 识别了一种简单的机制——流体剪切使旋转弹性结构失稳。这一发现有助于理解弹性结构与流体相互作用中的失稳行为，并可能对旋转机械或生物流体系统中的相关现象提供理论依据。

Abstract: A soft thin elastic disk spinning in a viscous fluid experiences centrifugal tension generated by rotation together with viscous shear generated by the surrounding flow. While the former stabilizes the flat state, the latter can destabilize it. We combine the linearized Föppl-von Kármán equations for a rotating elastic disk with the shear stresses arising from the classical von Kármán swirling flow to derive an elastohydrodynamic stability problem. Linear stability analysis identifies the onset of buckling in terms of two dimensionless control parameters measuring centrifugal stiffening and fluid-induced shear. Above threshold the disk buckles into azimuthally periodic saddle-like modes whose wavenumber increases with increasing rotational tension. The buckled configuration also supports retrograde traveling waves that rotate more slowly than the material frame. These results identify a simple mechanism whereby fluid shear destabilizes rotating elastic structures.

</details>

# hep-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [83] [Machine Can Automatically Discover Parametric Functions to Model HEP Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19750)
*Ho Fung Tsoi,Dylan Rankin,Cecile Caillol,Miles Cranmer,Sridhara Dasu,Javier Duarte,Philip Harris,Elliot Lipeles*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出利用符号回归（symbolic regression）自动搜索函数空间来替代高能物理（HEP）数据分析中手动选择函数拟合分箱数据的迭代过程，并开发了SymbolFit软件包。在CMS与ATLAS Run 2双喷注（dijet）能谱上，该包在560次独立运行中生成了超过1000个满足χ²/NDF≈1的拟合函数，其中111次运行成功重现了已发表双喷注搜索中的dijet与UA2函数形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高能物理（high-energy physics, HEP）数据分析中，寻找合适的函数对分箱数据（binned data）进行建模高度依赖手动过程：凭直觉猜测函数形式、拟合、检查并反复迭代，效率低且易受人为偏误影响。本文旨在自动化这一过程，以提升函数搜索的效率与客观性。

Method: 采用符号回归（symbolic regression）进行数据驱动的函数空间搜索，无需预设函数形式的先验知识。将符号回归与不确定性建模（uncertainty modeling）相结合，开发了SymbolFit软件包，并针对HEP分析用例进行优化。

Result: 在CMS和ATLAS Run 2的双喷注（dijet）能谱上进行测试：560次独立有种子（seeded）运行，覆盖七种简单拟合配置，生成了超过1000个拟合函数，其χ²/NDF均接近1。其中111次运行成功重新发现了已发表双喷注搜索中使用的dijet函数与UA2函数。

Conclusion: 符号回归可以有效地自动化HEP数据拟合中的函数选择迭代过程，且能够在不依赖先验知识的情况下发现甚至重现人工选定的已知函数形式，表明该方法具有通用性与实用价值。

Abstract: In HEP data analyses, finding an adequate function to model binned data has largely relied on a manual process: guess a functional form by intuition, fit, examine, then repeat until successful. We show that this iterative process can be automated by a machine using symbolic regression, which performs a data-driven search over function space without requiring prior knowledge of what an adequate function should look like. We present the SymbolFit package, which pairs symbolic regression with uncertainty modeling to target HEP analysis use cases, and demonstrate it on the CMS and ATLAS Run 2 dijet spectra: 560 independent seeded runs across seven simple fit configurations generated over 1000 functions fitting the spectra with $χ^2/\text{NDF}\approx 1$, and 111 of the runs rediscovered the very dijet and UA2 functions used in published dijet searches.

</details>

Zhou,Y. X. Zhou,Y. Z. Zhou,A. N. Zhu,J. Zhu,K. Zhu,K. J. Zhu,K. S. Zhu,L. X. Zhu,Lin Zhu,S. H. Zhu,T. J. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,M. Zhuge,J. H. Zou*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 在BESIII实验中使用约101亿J/ψ事例验证了一种在通用谱仪上测量末态核子自旋极化的新技术，通过测量探测器支撑材料上极化质子散射的不对称性并确认与预期值一致，证明通用谱仪可作为大接收度极化计（polarimeter），在提供常规四动量（four-momentum）信息之外额外提供自旋极化（spin polarization）信息，从而增强现有及未来粒子与核物理设施的物理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有通用谱仪通常只能测量末态粒子的四动量信息，无法提供自旋极化这一重要自由度；研究者希望验证一种能够在通用谱仪上测量末态核子自旋极化的新技术，以扩展其物理探测能力。

Method: 利用BESIII实验采集的10.09×10⁹个J/ψ事例，通过测量极化质子在探测器支撑材料上散射所产生的左右不对称性（asymmetry），将该不对称性与预期理论值进行比较，从而验证技术可行性。

Result: 测量得到的极化质子散射不对称性与预期值在误差范围内一致，证实该技术有效。研究证明通用谱仪可以作为大接收度极化计使用。

Conclusion: 该技术使得通用谱仪在输出常规四动量信息的同时能够提供末态粒子的自旋极化信息，进而增强了现有及未来粒子物理与核物理设施的物理分析能力。

Abstract: A novel technique for measuring the spin polarization of final-state nucleons in a general-purpose spectrometer is validated. Using $10.09\times10^{9}$ $J/ψ$ events at BESIII, the asymmetry of polarized proton scattering on detector support material is measured, and is consistent with the expected value. This proves that a general-purpose spectrometer can be utilized as a large-acceptance polarimeter, providing the spin polarization in addition to the conventional four-momentum information of the final-state particles. With this technique, physics capabilities are enhanced for existing and future facilities in particle and nuclear physics.

</details>

X. Zhao,Z. G. Zhao,A. Zhemchugov,B. Zheng,B. M. Zheng,J. P. Zheng,W. J. Zheng,W. Q. Zheng,X. R. Zheng,Y. H. Zheng,B. Zhong,C. Zhong,H. Zhou,J. Q. Zhou,S. Zhou,X. Zhou,X. K. Zhou,X. R. Zhou,X. Y. Zhou,Y. X. Zhou,Y. Z. Zhou,A. N. Zhu,J. Zhu,K. Zhu,K. J. Zhu,K. S. Zhu,L. X. Zhu,Lin Zhu,S. H. Zhu,T. J. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,M. Zhuge,J. H. Zou*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本研究利用BESIII收集的约10^9个J/ψ衰变事件，通过测量次级散射极化这一新技术，首次测定了质子在类时区域（time-like region）的电弱形状因子（electromagnetic form factors）之间的相对相位正弦值，结果为sinΔΦ = -0.20 ± 0.34(stat) ± 0.11(syst)，为理解质子内部结构的复杂动力学提供了直接实验约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 质子的时间型（time-like）形状因子之间的相对相位（relative phase）是完整理解其内部结构的关键可观测量，但由于测定末态极化或使用极化束的实验难度极大，该量至今未被测量。

Method: 采用一种新技术，通过次级散射（secondary scattering）在谱仪材料上测量极化；利用BESIII实验收集的10.09×10^9个J/ψ事件，分析了e⁺e⁻ → J/ψ → p反p反应过程。

Result: 首次测定了质子psionic形状因子之间相对相位的正弦值，结果为sinΔΦ = -0.20 ± 0.34(统计不确定度) ± 0.11(系统不确定度)。

Conclusion: 该结果为质子形成的复杂动力学提供了首次直接实验洞察，并为约束核子结构（nucleon structure）的理论模型提供了有价值的新信息。

Abstract: The relative phase between the time-like form factors of the proton is a crucial observable for a complete understanding of its internal structure, yet it has remained unmeasured due to the formidable experimental challenge of determining the final-state polarization or having available polarized beams. With a novel technique that measures polarization via secondary scattering on spectrometer material, we use $10.09\times10^{9}$ $J/ψ$ events collected at BESIII to analyze the reaction $e^+e^-\rightarrow J/ψ\rightarrow p\bar{p}$. This allows the first determination of the sine of the relative phase between the proton psionic form factors, $\sinΔΦ=-0.20\pm0.34_{\textrm{stat}}\pm0.11_{\textrm{syst}}$. This result provides the first direct insight into the complex dynamics of proton formation, and offers valuable new information to constrain theoretical models of nucleon structure.

</details>


### [86] [Evidence for longitudinally polarised $Z$ bosons in electroweak $W^{\pm}Z$ production in association with two jets from $pp$ collisions at $\sqrt{s} = $ 13 TeV and 13.6 TeV with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20246)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于ATLAS探测器在13 TeV和13.6 TeV质子-质子对撞数据（积分亮度140 fb⁻¹和164 fb⁻¹），测量了电弱过程W±Z与双喷注伴随产生（WZjj-EW）中W和Z规范玻色子的极化态。观测到包含纵向极化Z玻色子的WZjj-EW事件显著性为4.0倍标准差，纵向极化Z玻色子的事件比例fX0=0.32±0.09，与标准模型（Standard Model）次领头阶电弱修正预言一致。同时给出了W和双玻色子纵向极化比例的上限，并测量了13.6 TeV下的积分赝快度截面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电弱过程WZjj-EW中的规范玻色子极化态测量是检验标准模型电弱相互作用和电弱对称性破缺（electroweak symmetry breaking）机制的关键观测量。纵向极化（longitudinal polarisation）的W/Z玻色子与希格斯机制（Higgs mechanism）直接相关，其精确测量有助于验证标准模型预言并探寻新物理信号。

Method: 使用ATLAS探测器记录的13 TeV（140 fb⁻¹）和13.6 TeV（164 fb⁻¹）质子-质子对撞数据，通过轻子衰变道（电子和缪子）重建W±Z候选事件。基于运动学变量和事件拓扑筛选WZjj-EW过程，通过数据-蒙特卡洛比较提取极化态信息。

Result: 观测到包含纵向极化Z玻色子的WZjj-EW事件显著性4.0倍标准差；赝快度区内纵向极化Z玻色子事件比例fX0=0.32±0.09；95%置信水平（confidence level）下W玻色子纵向极化比例上限0.19，双玻色子纵向极化比例上限0.12；13.6 TeV下每轻子味道的积分赝快度截面为0.374±0.077(统计)±0.053(系统)±0.009(亮度) fb。

Conclusion: 所有测量结果均与标准模型次领头阶电弱修正预言在误差范围内一致。该工作首次在WZjj-EW过程中实现Z玻色子纵向极化的显著观测，并对W玻色子及双玻色子纵向极化比例给出了实验上限，为电弱对称性破缺的检验提供了新约束。

Abstract: Measurements of polarisation states of $W$ and $Z$ gauge bosons in electroweak $W^{\pm}Z$ production in association with two jets ($WZjj\mathrm{-EW}$) in proton-proton collisions are presented. The data set used corresponds to integrated luminosities of 140 fb$^{-1}$ and 164 fb$^{-1}$ of proton-proton collisions at centre-of-mass energies of 13 TeV and 13.6 TeV, respectively, recorded by the ATLAS detector at the CERN Large Hadron Collider. The $W^{\pm}Z$ candidate events are reconstructed using leptonic decay modes of the gauge bosons into electrons and muons. The observed significance for the presence in data of $WZjj\mathrm{-EW}$ events containing a longitudinally polarised $Z$ boson is of 4.0 standard deviations. The measured fraction of such events, integrated over the fiducial region, is $f_{\mathrm{X0}} = 0.32 \pm 0.09$, in agreement with the Standard Model prediction at next-to-leading-order in electroweak corrections. Upper limits at 95% confidence level of 0.19 and 0.12 are set on the fraction of events with a $W$ boson longitudinally polarised and on the fraction of events with the two bosons longitudinally polarised, respectively. The integrated fiducial cross-section per lepton flavour of $WZjj\mathrm{-EW}$ production at $\sqrt{s} = 13.6$ TeV is also measured to be $σ_{WZjj\mathrm{-EW} \rightarrow \ell^{'} ν\ell \ell jj} = 0.374 \; \pm 0.077 (\mathrm{stat.}) \; \pm 0.053 (\mathrm{syst.}) \; \pm 0.009 (\mathrm{lumi.}) \; \mathrm{fb}$, where $\ell$ and $\ell^{'}$ are either an electron or a muon. This measurement is in agreement with the Standard Model expectation.

</details>

*LHCb collaboration,R. Aaij,M. Abdelfatah,A. S. W. Abdelmotteleb,C. Abellan Beteta,F. Abudinén,T. Ackernley,A. A. Adefisoye,B. Adeva,M. Adinolfi,P. Adlarson,C. Agapopoulou,C. A. Aidala,S. Akar,K. Wu,Y. Wu,Z. Wu,K. Wyllie,S. Xian,Z. Xiang,Y. Xie,T. X. Xing,A. Xu,L. Xu,M. Xu,R. Xu,Z. Xu,Z. Xu,Z. Xu,Z. Xu,S. Yadav,K. Yang,X. Yang,Y. Yang,Y. Yang,Z. Yang,Z. Yang,H. Yeung,H. Yin,X. Yin,C. Y. Yu,J. Yu,X. Yuan,Y Yuan,J. A. Zamora Saa,M. Zavertyaev,M. Zdybal,F. Zenesini,C. Zeng,M. Zeng,S. H Zeng,C. Zhang,D. Zhang,J. Zhang,L. Zhang,R. Zhang,S. Zhang,S. L. Zhang,Y. Zhang,Z. Zhang,J. Zhao,Y. Zhao,A. Zhelezov,S. Z. Zheng,X. Z. Zheng,Y. Zheng,T. Zhou,X. Zhou,V. Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,Y. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文基于LHCb探测器在Run 2期间收集的质心能量为13 TeV、总积分亮度为6 fb⁻¹的质子-质子对撞数据，对卡比玻压低衰变过程D⁺→φπ⁺中的电荷-宇称（CP）破坏进行了搜寻，测得直接CP不对称性为(0.1±4.9(stat)±2.4(syst))×10⁻⁴；此外，首次在强子对撞机上研究了D⁺→K⁰π⁺与D⁺→K⁻⁰π⁺衰变振幅的模比和相对强相位，并报告了二维置信区间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在卡比玻压低（Cabibbo-suppressed）的D⁺→φπ⁺衰变中搜寻电荷-宇称（CP）破坏，以检验标准模型对粲介子系统中CP破坏的预言，并探索可能的新物理信号。

Method: 利用LHCb探测器在质子-质子对撞中采集的6 fb⁻¹数据进行分析；采用丰富的D⁺→K⁰_Sπ⁺衰变样本，校正由粲介子产生和伴随φ介子的带电π子探测效应引起的不对称性；通过减法扣除中性K介子混合、中性K介子再生以及卡比玻允许过程D⁺→K⁻⁰π⁺与双卡比玻压低过程D⁺→K⁰π⁺之间干涉等多项过程引起的背景不对称性。

Result: 测得D⁺→φπ⁺衰变的直接CP不对称性为a_CP=(0.1±4.9(stat)±2.4(syst))×10⁻⁴；首次在强子对撞机（hadron collider）上获得了D⁺→K⁰π⁺与D⁺→K⁻⁰π⁺衰变振幅的模比和相对强相位的二维置信区间。

Conclusion: 测量结果显示D⁺→φπ⁺衰变中未观测到显著的直接CP破坏，结果与标准模型预期一致；D⁺→K⁰π⁺与D⁺→K⁻⁰π⁺衰变振幅相关参数的首次强子对撞机测量为相关理论模型提供了新的实验约束。

Abstract: A search for charge-parity ($C\!P$) violation in the Cabibbo-suppressed $D^+ \to φπ^+$ decay is presented, using proton-proton collision data corresponding to an integrated luminosity of $6\text{ fb}^{-1}$, collected at a centre-of-mass energy of $13\text{ TeV}$ with the LHCb detector during Run 2. An abundant sample of $D^+ \to K_{\rm S}^0 π^+$ decays is employed to correct for asymmetries arising from the production of the charmed meson and from detection effects associated with the charged pion accompanying the $φ$ meson. Asymmetries induced by interference of multiple processes, such as neutral kaon mixing, regeneration of neutral kaons, and interference between the Cabibbo-favoured $D^+ \to \overline{K}^0 π^+$ and the doubly Cabibbo-suppressed $D^+ \to {K}^0 π^+$ decay, are subtracted. The direct $C\!P$ asymmetry in the $D^+ \to φπ^+$ decay is measured to be \begin{equation*} a_{C\!P}(D^+ \to φπ^+) = \left(0.1 \pm 4.9\text{ (stat)} \pm 2.4\text{ (syst)} \right)\times 10^{-4}. \end{equation*} For the first time at a hadron collider, the modulus of the ratio and the relative strong phase of the $D^+ \to {K}^0 π^+$ to $D^+ \to \overline{ K}^0 π^+$ decay amplitudes are also investigated. Two-dimensional confidence intervals are reported for these parameters.

</details>


### [88] [Lightest $0^{-+}$ Glueball as Dominant Constituent of $X(2370)$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20366)
*BESIII Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于BESIII收集的100亿J/ψ事件，论文搜寻了X(2370)到K*(892)⁰K̅⁰+c.c.的衰变模式，未发现显著信号，并给出了90%置信水平的上限。研究表明X(2370)具有味单态（flavor-singlet）性质，系统总结了所有BESIII对该粒子的测量结果，论证了最轻0⁻⁺胶球（glueball）是其主导成分的结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验X(2370)是否衰变至K*(892)K̅模式，以确定其味单态性质；进而探讨X(2370)是否以最轻0⁻⁺胶球（glueball）为主要成分，这是理解强相互作用非微扰区奇特强子态的核心问题之一。

Method: 利用BESIII采集的100亿J/ψ事例，通过J/ψ→γK_S⁰K_S⁰π⁰过程搜寻X(2370)→K*(892)⁰K̅⁰+c.c.衰变道；基于未观测到显著信号，设定90%置信水平（confidence level）下的分支比上限。

Result: 未发现X(2370)→K*(892)⁰K̅⁰+c.c.衰变模式的证据，分支比乘积上限为2.7×10⁻⁶（90%置信水平）。K*(892)K̅模式的压低表明X(2370)为味单态（flavor-singlet）粒子，这是首个在1GeV/c²以上观测到的味单态轻强子。

Conclusion: 最轻0⁻⁺胶球（glueball）作为X(2370)的主导成分，能够自然且完整地解释其全部性质——质量、自旋宇称、在J/ψ辐射衰变中的高产生率、与η_c相似的衰变模式、味单态性质、窄部分衰变宽度（partial decay width）以及向ω和φ辐射衰变的压低——而其他解释目前均不被支持。

Abstract: With 10 billion $J/ψ$ events collected at \mbox{BESIII}, the decay of $X(2370)\rightarrow K^{*}(892)^{0}\bar{K}^{0}+\mathrm{c.c.}$ is searched for via the $J/ψ\rightarrowγK_{S}^{0}K_{S}^{0}π^{0}$ process. No evidence of this decay mode is found, with $\mathcal{B}[J/ψ\rightarrowγX(2370)] \times \mathcal{B}[ X(2370) \rightarrow K^{*}(892)^{0}\bar{K}^{0}+\mathrm{c.c.} \rightarrow K^{0}_{S}K^{0}_{S}π^{0}] < 2.7\times 10^{-6}$ at the $90\%$ confidence level. The suppression of the $K^{*}(892)\bar{K}$ mode indicates the $X(2370)$ as a flavor-singlet state. It is the first flavor-singlet light hadron observed above $1~\textrm{GeV}/c^{2}$. All \mbox{BESIII} measurements on the $X(2370)$ are summarized. A dominant component of the lightest $0^{-+}$ glueball is essential for a natural and complete explanation of the properties of the $X(2370)$~\textemdash~the mass, spin-parity, high production rate in $J/ψ$ radiative decays, decay pattern similarities to that of $η_{c}$, flavor-singlet property, narrow partial decay width, and suppression of radiative decays to $ω$ and $φ$, since these properties are all consistent with the features of the lightest $0^{-+}$ glueball while other interpretations at present are disfavored. This supports that the lightest $0^{-+}$ glueball is the dominant constituent of the $X(2370)$.

</details>


### [89] [Interaction-model dependence in calorimetric energy reconstruction methods due to non-linear material effects in modern neutrino detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20419)
*Katharina Lachner,Steven Boyd,Stephen Dolan,Laura Munteanu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文系统评估了中微子振荡实验中，由于探测器材料效应（如Birks猝灭和复合效应）导致的能量重建偏差在不同相互作用模型（GENIE、NEUT、NuWro、GiBUU）之间的差异。结果表明，纯量热法重建下，闪烁体探测器平均偏差约为7–9 MeV，氩探测器约为11–18 MeV；采用理想化的混合重建（径迹+量热法）可将其降低至约3.5 MeV。材料效应带来的重建偏差可能对中微子振荡和截面测量引入不可忽视的系统性不确定度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中微子振荡实验依赖高精度的中微子能量重建，但探测器响应中的非线性效应（如闪烁体中的Birks猝灭和TPC中的复合效应）导致可见强子能量重建存在歧义。解决这些歧义需要依赖相互作用模型的假设，从而引入重建偏差。现有研究主要集中在末态中子等造成的缺失能量偏差，而材料效应造成的相互作用模型依赖性偏差尚未被充分量化。

Method: 本文针对多个中微子相互作用事件生成器（GENIE、NEUT、NuWro、GiBUU）的不同调谐版本，评估了材料效应（Birks猝灭、复合效应）导致的能量重建偏差对模型的依赖性。研究中选择了代表T2K (ND280)、NOνA、MINERνA、μBooNE和DUNE实验的探测器场景，分别使用纯量热法（calorimetric）重建和理想化混合重建（hybrid reconstruction，基于径迹追踪和量热法）进行分析。

Result: 纯量热法重建下，中微子能量重建平均偏差在不同模型间存在显著差异：闪烁体探测器约为7–9 MeV，氩基探测器约为11–18 MeV。氩探测器的偏差在使用理想化混合重建后可降至约3.5 MeV。

Conclusion: 材料效应导致的中微子能量重建偏差在模型间差异显著，可能对中微子振荡和截面测量引入不可忽视的系统性不确定度。作者建议采用替代分析策略以缓解该问题。

Abstract: Neutrino oscillation experiments rely on high precision neutrino energy reconstruction. A common reconstruction technique in LAr-TPCs and scintillators is via the calorimetric sum of visible particles created in the interaction. However, non-linearities in the detector response, such as Birks quenching for scintillators and recombination effects for TPCs, lead to ambiguities in the reconstruction of visible hadronic energies. Interaction-model-dependent assumptions are required to resolve these ambiguities, which introduces a bias in reconstruction of neutrino energy. This introduces a systematic uncertainty separate from the well-studied bias due to interaction-model dependent modelling of missing energy caused by, for example, the production of final state neutrons. In this work, we evaluate the interaction-model dependence of the bias caused by these material effects across multiple tunes of the GENIE, NEUT, NuWro, and GiBUU neutrino interaction event generators for cases representative of calorimetric energy reconstruction at the T2K (ND280), NO$ν$A, MINER$ν$A, $μ$BooNE, and DUNE experiments. Using pure calorimetric reconstruction, our results show significant differences in the mean neutrino-energy reconstruction bias between models, at the level of $\sim$7-9\,MeV for scintillator detectors and $\sim$11-18\,MeV for argon-based detectors in the relevant energy range. The latter is shown to be reduced (down to $\sim$3.5\,MeV) when using an idealised hybrid energy reconstruction based on tracking and calorimetry. Overall, we conclude that neutrino-energy reconstruction bias due to material effects may imply non-negligible systematic uncertainties for neutrino oscillation and cross-section measurements, and discuss alternative analysis strategies to mitigate the issue.

</details>

### [90] [Noise reduction in suspension control with photon-pressure actuator for CHRONOS gravitational wave detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19983)
*Daiki Tanabe,Yuki Inoue,Mario Juvenal S. Onglao*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种光压致动器（photon-pressure actuator），用于降低引力波探测器在亚赫兹频段的致动噪声，并通过CHRONOS实验验证了其扭矩、效率及噪声水平满足设计要求，同时可作为光子校准器使用，系统误差为1.14%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提升引力波（gravitational wave, GW）探测器在亚赫兹（sub-Hz）频段的灵敏度，对于探测更重的双黑洞合并现象及研究强引力场物理至关重要。然而，低频段中力源振动与环境磁场涨落引起的致动噪声（actuation noise）成为主要限制因素之一。

Method: 提出光压致动器作为解决方案，通过光压（photon-pressure）效应将致动器与地震噪声和磁噪声隔离；设计了包含四束独立控制光束的光学布局，并将其应用于CHRONOS实验的扭摆（torsion bar）系统。

Result: 基于实际功率控制系统，估算出绕偏航旋转轴（yaw rotation axis）的最大扭矩幅度为$1.0\times 10^{-8}$ N·m，致动效率为$6.6\times 10^{-13}$ rad/V，满足CHRONOS扭摆控制需求；致动噪声在1 Hz处估计为$5.3\times 10^{-19}$ rad Hz^{-1/2}，低于CHRONOS目标灵敏度；作为光子校准器使用时，系统误差为1.14%。

Conclusion: 光压致动器可有效抑制低频致动噪声，适用于基于扭摆的引力波探测器（torsion-bar-based GW detectors），并具备光子校准功能，系统误差较小。

Abstract: Improving sub-Hz sensitivity of gravitational wave (GW) detectors is important to detect heavier binary black hole mergers and study phenomena in stronger gravity fields. Torsion-bar-based GW detectors have been projected to focus on low-frequency GW. Among noise sources of GW detector, actuation noise induced by vibration of force sources and fluctuation of environmental magnetic fields is one that increases in low frequency. In this study, we propose photon-pressure actuator as a solution to isolate an actuator from seismic and magnetic noise. It can also be used as a photon calibrator. We designed an optical layout of the photon-pressure actuator having four beams independently controlled and applied it to CHRONOS experiment. Based on a realistic power control system, we estimated its maximum torque amplitude around yaw rotation axis as $1.0\times 10^{-8}$ N$\cdot$m and actuation efficiency as $6.6\times 10^{-13}$ rad/V, which are sufficiently large for controlling the CHRONOS torsion bar. The actuation noise was estimated as $5.3\times 10^{-19}$ rad ${\rm Hz}^{-1/2}$ at 1 Hz, lower than the target sensitivity of CHRONOS. Assuming its usage as a photon calibrator, the estimated systematic error was 1.14%.

### [91] [Measurement of the $γγ\to ττ$ cross section and constraints on the anomalous magnetic moment of the $τ$ lepton in ultraperipheral PbPb collisions at $\sqrt{s_\mathrm{NN}}$ = 5.02 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20148)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于CMS实验2018年收集的1.70 nb$^{-1}$铅铅超外周碰撞数据，通过光子-光子聚变产生$τ$轻子对（$γγ\to ττ$）的过程，首次利用该过程在LHC上对$τ$轻子反常磁矩（$a_τ$）进行了约束，给出了$-$0.039 $\lt$ $a_τ$ $\lt$ 0.032的95%置信区间，并测量了该过程的赝快度截面，为目前LHC上最精确的测量结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用铅铅超外周碰撞（ultraperipheral lead-lead collisions）中的光子-光子聚变过程（photon-photon fusion, $γγ\to ττ$），约束$τ$轻子的反常磁矩（anomalous magnetic moment, $a_τ$），并精确测量该过程的截面（cross section），以检验量子电动力学（quantum electrodynamics, QED）的次领头阶预言。

Method: 基于CMS实验2018年采集的质心系能量5.02 TeV、积分亮度1.70 nb$^{-1}$的铅铅碰撞数据；分析$τ^+τ^-$四种不同衰变末态（final states）；对测量得到的轻子横动量（transverse momentum, $p_\mathrm{T}$）分布进行同时似然拟合（simultaneous likelihood fit），同时利用能谱形状（spectral shape）和归一化（normalization）信息来约束$a_τ$并提取截面。

Result: $a_τ$的95%置信区间（CL interval）为$-$0.039 $\lt$ $a_τ$ $\lt$ 0.032；赝快度截面（fiducial cross section）$σ_{γγ\to ττ}^\text{fid}$ = 555$^{+60}_{-14}$ $μ$b（条件：$p_\mathrm{T}^τ$ $\gt$ 1 GeV，赝快度$\lvertη^τ\rvert$ $\lt$ 3），为LHC上该过程目前最精确的测量结果，与次领头阶量子电动力学（next-to-leading-order QED）预言一致。

Conclusion: 本文展示了通过超外周重离子碰撞中的光子-光子过程约束轻子反常磁矩的可行性，所得$a_τ$区间和截面测量结果均与次领头阶QED理论预言吻合，为未来更高精度检验标准模型（Standard Model）电弱部分提供了重要参考。

Abstract: The production of $τ$ lepton pairs via photon-photon fusion, $γγ\to ττ$, is studied in ultraperipheral lead-lead collisions at a nucleon-nucleon center-of-mass energy of 5.02 TeV. The dataset, collected by the CMS experiment in 2018, corresponds to an integrated luminosity of 1.70 nb$^{-1}$. Four different $τ^+τ^-$ decay final states are analyzed. A simultaneous likelihood fit to the measured lepton transverse momentum ($p_\mathrm{T}$) distributions, which incorporates information from both spectral shape and normalization, is used to constrain the anomalous magnetic moment of the $τ$ lepton, $a_τ$, and to extract the cross section of the process. The measured 95% CL interval for $a_τ$ is $-$0.039 $\lt$ $a_τ$ $\lt$ 0.032. The fiducial cross section, $σ_{γγ\to ττ}^\text{fid}$ = 555$^{+60}_{-14}$ $μ$b for tau leptons with $p_\mathrm{T}^τ$ $\gt$ 1 GeV and pseudorapidity $\lvertη^τ\rvert$ $\lt$ 3, is the most precise measurement for this process at the LHC to date and is in agreement with next-to-leading-order quantum electrodynamics predictions.

### [92] [Quantum Mott semimetal in a one-dimensional Hubbard mode](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19465)
*Boran Zhou,Taige Wang,Ya-Hui Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文在一维自旋1/2 Hubbard模型中证明了量子莫特半金属（quantum Mott semimetal）基态的存在，该相受反演对称性和粒子-空穴对称性保护，并可通过引入反铁磁自旋耦合（antiferromagnetic spin coupling）来稳定。该模型捕捉了扭曲双层石墨烯（TBG）中莫特物理（Mott physics）的一些关键特征，提供了莫特半金属基态的首个无偏证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑能带中的莫特物理（Mott physics in topological bands）近年来引起广泛关注，尤其在扭曲双层石墨烯（twisted bilayer graphene, TBG）背景下。然而，稳定该物理的关键要素尚不清楚。本文旨在澄清这些要素，并寻找莫特半金属相的无偏证据。

Method: 从具有A子晶格局域化f轨道和B子晶格离域化c轨道的双轨道模型出发，将f轨道的Hubbard U投影到活性平带（flat band）上，得到Wannier轨道中心位于B子晶格的晶格模型。采用精确对角化（exact diagonalization, ED）和密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）方法进行数值计算。

Result: 仅含Hubbard U时基态为铁磁态；引入交错位点反铁磁自旋耦合（inter-site antiferromagnetic spin coupling）J后，可稳定一个中心荷（central charge）c=3的莫特半金属相。该相包含一个自旋1/2狄拉克费米子（spinful Dirac fermion）与一个中性自旋模式（neutral spin mode）共存，类似于高维中的分数化费米液体（fractionalized Fermi liquid, FL*）相。通过色散打破粒子-空穴对称性后，莫特半金属转变为莫特绝缘体（Mott insulator），该绝缘体与另一不同的莫特绝缘体相之间发生连续相变，伴随1/2的极化跳变（polarization jump）。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了莫特半金属基态的首个无偏证据，并表明该一维模型虽缺乏Wannier阻塞（Wannier obstruction），但仍能捕捉TBG物理的部分关键特征。

Abstract: Mott physics in topological bands has recently attracted considerable attention, particularly in the context of twisted bilayer graphene (TBG). However, the essential ingredients for stabilizing this physics remain unclear. Here, we demonstrate a quantum Mott semimetal phase as the ground state within a one-dimensional spinful Hubbard model featuring only one orbital per unit cell, protected by inversion and particle-hole symmetries. We start from a two-orbital model where a localized $f$ orbital on the A sublattice hybridizes with a delocalized $c$ orbital on the B sublattice. Projecting the $f$-orbital Hubbard $U$ onto the active flat band yields a lattice model with Wannier orbitals centered on the B sublattice. Similar to TBG, a momentum-space scale $k_*$ emerges, setting the interaction range in the projected model to $1/k_*$. While the ground state is ferromagnetic with only the Hubbard $U$, introducing an inter-site antiferromagnetic spin coupling $J$ stabilizes a Mott semimetal$^*$ phase with a central charge $c=3$. Using exact diagonalization (ED) and density matrix renormalization group (DMRG) methods, we show that this phase hosts a spinful Dirac fermion coexisting with a neutral spin mode -- analogous to the fractionalized Fermi liquid (FL$^*$) phase in higher dimensions. Furthermore, breaking particle-hole (PH) symmetry via dispersion transforms the Mott semimetal into a Mott insulator, which is separated from a distinct Mott insulating phase by a continuous transition with a polarization jump of $1/2$. Our work provides the first unbiased evidence of a Mott semimetal ground state and demonstrates that this 1D model captures some essential aspects of TBG physics, despite lacking a Wannier obstruction.

</details>


### [93] [Anyon Crystals and Hall Crystals in a Periodic Potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19466)
*Sayak Bhattacharjee,Julian May-Mann,Srinivas Raghu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过平均场（mean-field）分析一个有效晶格模型，证明了在强垂直磁场和周期势作用下，二维电子系统可以形成整数和分数量子霍尔晶体（integer and fractional quantum Hall crystals）。对于某些分数态，霍尔晶体可以构成任意子晶体（anyon crystal），其中任意子（anyons）呈现周期性有序排列。这些相态在玻色子坐标下表现为超固体（supersolid），即具有电荷序的超流体；在强相互作用下，超固体中自发产生涡旋-反涡旋对，从而实现任意子的晶格态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索二维电子系统在强磁场和周期势共同作用下可能形成的新的量子基态，特别是分数量子霍尔晶体和任意子晶体的存在性及其稳定性条件。

Method: 对附着奇数个磁通量子（flux quanta）的玻色子有效晶格模型进行平均场分析，利用统计变换将玻色子统计转化为电子统计，从而在玻色子坐标下研究霍尔晶体的性质。

Result: 发现了整数和分数量子霍尔晶体作为系统的基态；证明分数态霍尔晶体可构成任意子晶体；确定了此类态在朗道能级混合（Landau level mixing）足够弱且填充接近底层晶格半填充时的稳定条件。

Conclusion: 霍尔晶体在玻色子坐标下本质上是超固体；强相互作用可在超固体中诱导出涡旋-反涡旋对的自发成核，从而形成任意子的晶体态。

Abstract: We obtain integer and fractional quantum Hall crystals as ground states of a two-dimensional electron system subject to a strong perpendicular magnetic field and a periodic potential. For certain fractional states, we show that the Hall crystal can constitute an anyon crystal, with a periodic ordering of well-defined anyons. We find that the latter states can be stabilized at odd denominator Landau level filling fractions when Landau level mixing is sufficiently weak, and near half-filling of the underlying lattice. These phases are obtained from a mean-field analysis of an effective lattice model of bosons attached to an odd number of flux quanta, which transmutes their statistics to that of electrons. In boson coordinates, the Hall crystal is a supersolid: a superfluid with charge order. Under strong interactions, vortex-anti-vortex pairs spontaneously nucleate in the supersolid, realizing a crystalline state of anyons.

</details>


### [94] [Twisting-operator approach to identifying gaplessness in SU($N$) fermionic systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19694)
*Hao Cheng,Hang Su,Yuan Yao*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出并证明了自旋为1/2的费米子链在具有SU(2)自旋旋转对称性时存在能隙的一个必要判据：适当定义的费米子扭曲算符（fermionic twisting operator）的期望值在热力学极限下趋近于1，反之若不为1则表明体系无能隙。该判据通过BCS哈密顿量和DQMC模拟验证，并推广至SU(N)对称费米子系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为具有SU(2)自旋旋转对称性的自旋费米子链建立是否存在能隙（gapped）的一般性必要判据，从而提供一种可计算的诊断工具来区分有能隙相和无能隙（gapless）相。

Method: 定义了一个费米子扭曲算符（fermionic twisting operator），证明在有能隙且基态简并度有限的相中，该算符的期望值在热力学极限下趋近于1，且有限尺寸修正被$\mathscr{O}(1/L)$所界。利用s波BCS哈密顿量和相互作用Hubbard模型的确定性量子蒙特卡洛（DQMC）模拟验证该判据，并将方法推广至SU(N)对称系统。

Result: 证明了对于SU(2)对称自旋费米子链，有能隙相中费米子扭曲算符期望值渐近趋于1；非1的值可作为无能隙相的充分判据。在SU(N)对称情形下，有能隙基态扇区须为SU(N)单态（singlet），且对适当整数M有$\langle \hat{\mathcal{U}}^M\rangle=1+\mathscr{O}(1/L)$。

Conclusion: 费米子扭曲算符期望值是否为1提供了一个简洁有效的判据，用以区分SU(2)或SU(N)对称费米子链的有能隙与无能隙相，并得到数值验证。

Abstract: We propose a general necessary condition for a spinful fermion chain with SU(2) spin-rotation symmetry to be gapped. Specifically, we prove that the expectation value of a properly defined fermionic twisting operator asymptotically approaches unity in any gapped phase with finite ground-state degeneracy, with finite-size corrections bounded by $\mathscr{O}(1/L)$. Consequently, a non-unity value in the thermodynamic limit provides a sufficient criterion for identifying gapless fermion chains. We confirm this criterion using the $s$-wave Bardeen-Cooper-Schrieffer (BCS) Hamiltonian and determinant quantum Monte Carlo (DQMC) simulations of interacting Hubbard models. We further extend the twisting-operator approach to SU($N$)-symmetric fermionic systems, where the gapped ground-state sector must be SU($N$)-singlet and $\langle \hat{\mathcal{U}}^M\rangle=1+\mathscr{O}(1/L)$ by a fermionic twisting operator $\hat{\mathcal{U}}$ with a suitably chosen integer $M$.

</details>


### [95] [Coloring in anyon superconductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19470)
*Umang Mehta,Yuto Nakajima,Hart Goldman*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过在扭曲MoTe₂双层体系中构建电荷为e/3的“夸克”费米面与SU(3)₋₁陈-西蒙斯规范场耦合的框架，统一描述了掺杂ν=2/3分数量子反常霍尔（FQAH）态时涌现的多种任意子驱动相，包括超导相（如与拓扑序共存的SC★相、手征中心荷半整数的拓扑超导体）、非费米液体相以及任意子束缚态相，并将它们归结为超导性与巡游色铁磁性之间的竞争。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期在扭曲MoTe₂双层中观测到邻近分数量子反常霍尔（FQAH）态的超导迹象，重新激发了由任意子动力学诱导的量子物相的研究兴趣，亟需一个统一的理论框架来描述掺杂FQAH态时涌现的多种任意子驱动相。

Method: 作者构建了一个电荷为e/3的“夸克”费米面与SU(3)₋₁陈-西蒙斯规范场（Chern-Simons gauge field）耦合的框架，该框架对偶于更传统的准空穴U(1)₃陈-西蒙斯-金兹堡-朗道理论（Chern-Simons-Ginzburg-Landau theory），通过分析费米面的配对不稳定性与巡游铁磁极化来研究各种任意子相的涌现。

Result: 发现了一系列从色超导（color superconductivity）中涌现的电子超导体，包括与拓扑序共存的SC★相以及夸克弱配对时手征中心荷（chiral central charge）为半整数的拓扑超导体，例如通过p+ip“色-谷锁定”配对机制得到的c₋=-1/2拓扑超导体；当夸克形成巡游铁磁体时，涌现超导与非费米液体相；该框架还自然容纳了电荷2e/3的任意子束缚态相。

Conclusion: 该工作将许多先前提出的任意子相统一为单一母体夸克金属相的不稳定性，将它们归结为超导性与巡游色铁磁性之间的竞争，为理解掺杂分数量子反常霍尔态中的任意子驱动量子物相提供了统一的理论视角。

Abstract: The recently observed signatures of superconductivity proximate to a fractional quantum anomalous Hall (FQAH) state in a twisted MoTe$_2$ bilayer has revitalized interest in quantum phases of matter induced by anyon dynamics. Here we show how a panoply of anyon-driven phases associated with doping the lattice ${ν=2/3}$ FQAH state can be realized as competing instabilities of a Fermi surface of charge-$e/3$ "quarks" coupled to a $\mathrm{SU}(3)_{-1}$ Chern-Simons gauge field, which is dual to the more conventional $\mathrm{U}(1)_3$ Chern-Simons-Ginzburg-Landau theory of quasiholes. For example, a range of electronic superconductors emerge from color superconductivity, under which the Fermi surface experiences a pairing instability mediated by gauge fluctuations. These include SC$\star$ phases -- where superconductivity coexists with topological order -- as well as topological superconductors displaying half-integer chiral central charges when the quarks are weakly paired. One example is a topological superconductor arising from a $p+ip$ "color-valley-locked" pairing mechanism with chiral central charge $c_-=-1/2$. On the other hand, both superconducting and non-Fermi liquid phases can emerge when the quarks form an itinerant ferromagnet, polarizing the Fermi surface to a particular combination of colors. Finally, our framework naturally accommodates the possibility of anyonic bound state formation, allowing access to phases induced by doping anyons of charge $2e/3$ as opposed to $e/3$ within the same model. Our work unifies many earlier proposed anyonic phases as instabilities of a single parent quark metal phase, distilling their emergence into a competition between superconductivity and itinerant color ferromagnetism.

### [96] [Optical Magnetic Switching in Odd-Parity Magnets with Spin-Orbit Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19483)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于 Floquet 工程（Floquet engineering）框架，分析椭圆偏振光与具有自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的 p 波和 f 波磁体的相互作用，推导光诱导的有效哈密顿量，并计算体系的能带陈数（Chern number）和自旋极化。

Conclusion: 光是一种高效控制磁性态的手段，可用于奇宇称磁体的动态磁化和拓扑调控，在自旋电子学（spintronics）和量子信息（quantum information）领域具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: $p$-wave magnets exhibit odd-parity spin polarization in momentum space, with spin splitting that reverses under $\vec{k}\rightarrow -\vec{k}$, while preserving zero net magnetization. Here we show that, in odd-parity magnets with spin-orbit coupling, elliptically polarized light generates a momentum-independent spin-dependent term that dynamically switches a zero-net-magnetization $p$-wave state into a finite spin-polarized state. The Floquet-engineered bands also acquire a nonzero Chern number whose sign is controlled by the light polarization. For $f$-wave magnets, circularly polarized light induces a net out-of-plane magnetization, offering a direct experimental signature. Our results establish light as an efficient means of controlling magnetic states, with potential applications in spintronics and quantum information.

### [97] [Multi-Criticality and RG Topology in the Charge-Kondo-Breakdown Scenario in the Cuprates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19807)
*Stefan Kirchner,Petr Jizba*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文从重整化群拓扑角度分析铜氧化物超导体的电荷-Kondo击穿动力学，发现相互作用固定点存在边缘相关不稳定性，导致指数级大但有限的交叉标度，从而将表观量子临界行为解释为近临界固定点控制的扩展交叉区，而非真正的量子临界态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铜氧化物超导体中提出的动力学电荷-Kondo击穿（charge-Kondo breakdown）机制是否真正对应一个稳定的量子临界点（quantum critical point），尚存争议。本文旨在通过重整化群（renormalization group, RG）拓扑分析，区分真正的临界行为与赝临界行为（pseudo-critical behavior）。

Method: 采用重整化群拓扑方法，分析耦合的RG流方程（coupled RG flow equations）的固定点结构、稳定性及全局组织。综合运用流方程的解析解、数值相图（numerical phase portraits）和庞加莱紧致化（Poincaré compactification）技术。

Result: 发现假定的有限耦合相互作用固定点（finite-coupling interacting fixed point）在垂直于不变临界流形（invariant critical manifold）的方向上不稳定，导致通用RG轨迹出现失控行为（runaway behavior）。该固定点存在边缘相关不稳定性（marginally relevant instability），产生指数级大但有限的交叉标度（crossover scale）。流拓扑与各向异性驱动的失控流（anisotropy-driven runaway flows）高度相似。

Conclusion: 表观的量子临界区实际上是由近临界固定点（near-critical fixed point）控制的扩展交叉区，而非渐近标度不变性（asymptotic scale invariance）所导致。拓展标度行为的存在本身并不意味着存在稳定的相互作用量子临界态。RG拓扑分析是区分强关联量子物质中真正临界性与赝临界行为的有效诊断工具。

Abstract: In this paper, we examine the dynamical charge-Kondo-breakdown scenario proposed for cuprate superconductors within the perspective of renormalization group (RG) topology. By analyzing the coupled RG flow equations governing the effective low-energy theory, we determine the fixed-point structure, stability properties, and global organization of the flow. We find that the putative finite-coupling interacting fixed point is unstable against perturbations transverse to an invariant critical manifold. As a result, generic RG trajectories exhibit runaway behavior. To elucidate the global structure of the theory, we combine analytical solutions of the flow equations with numerical phase portraits and Poincaré compactification. This analysis reveals that the interacting fixed point exhibits a marginally relevant instability, generating an exponentially large but finite crossover scale. The resulting flow topology closely resembles anisotropy-driven runaway flows encountered in fluctuation-induced weakly first-order transitions. Within this framework, the apparent quantum-critical regime can be understood as an extended crossover controlled by a near-critical fixed point, rather than by asymptotic scale invariance. The results obtained indicate that the existence of extended scaling behavior does not, by itself, imply the presence of a stable interacting quantum critical state. More generally, our analysis demonstrates how RG topology can provide a powerful diagnostic for distinguishing genuine criticality from pseudo-critical behavior in theories of strongly correlated quantum matter.

</details>


### [98] [Spatially Dispersive Second-Harmonic Generation in Ferroaxial Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19821)
*Takumi Shiro,Satoru Hayami*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文建立了一种规范一致的（gauge-consistent）空间色散二次谐波产生（spatially dispersive SHG）微观理论，将电四极（EQ）和磁偶极（MD）过程平等处理。通过对具有铁轴向序（ferroaxial order）的最小三角团簇模型进行分析，发现非线性光学响应直接反映铁轴向序参量，且EQ和MD通道在相同共振能量下具有不同的谱权重，MD通道在某些共振处可主导EQ通道，表明两者对定量描述空间色散SHG均不可或缺。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 空间色散二次谐波产生（spatially dispersive SHG）能够超越电偶极近似（electric-dipole approximation），探测中心对称多极态（centrosymmetric multipolar states），但目前缺乏一个规范一致的微观理论框架来统一处理电四极（electric-quadrupole, EQ）和磁偶极（magnetic-dipole, MD）过程的贡献。

Method: 发展了一种规范一致的微观理论形式，对EQ和MD过程进行平等处理；将该理论应用于一个与电环形偶极矩（electric toroidal dipole）密切相关的具有铁轴向序（ferroaxial order）的最小三角团簇模型，并分别采用长度规范（length gauge）和速度规范（velocity gauge）进行计算以验证规范一致性。

Result: 非线性光学响应直接反映了铁轴向序参量；长度规范与速度规范的计算结果一致，证实了理论形式的规范一致性；EQ和MD通道在相同共振能量下表现出不同的谱权重；MD通道在特定共振处可主导EQ通道，而非仅仅是一个微扰修正。

Conclusion: 在铁轴向序材料中，EQ和MD过程对于定量描述空间色散SHG都是必不可少的；该工作为解释中心对称多极序的非线性光学特征提供了微观基础。

Abstract: Spatially dispersive second-harmonic generation (SHG) provides a powerful probe of centrosymmetric multipolar states beyond the electric-dipole approximation. We develop a gauge-consistent microscopic theory of spatially dispersive SHG that treats electric-quadrupole (EQ) and magnetic-dipole (MD) processes on equal footing. Applying the formulation to a minimal triangular cluster model with ferroaxial order, which is closely related to an electric toroidal dipole, we show that the nonlinear optical response directly reflects the ferroaxial order parameter. The agreement between length- and velocity-gauge calculations confirms the gauge consistency of the formulation. We further demonstrate that the EQ and MD contributions exhibit different spectral weights despite sharing the same resonance energies. In particular, the MD channel can dominate over the EQ channel at selected resonances, indicating that it is not merely a perturbative correction. Our results establish that both EQ and MD processes are essential for a quantitative description of spatially dispersive SHG in ferroaxial materials and provide a microscopic basis for interpreting nonlinear optical signatures of centrosymmetric multipolar order.

### [99] [How to measure loop currents in scanning tunneling microscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20030)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 环电流相已在多种量子材料（如铜氧化物高温超导体欠掺杂侧的赝隙相、Kagome材料及Sr₂RuO₄表面层）中被提出，但实验证据尚不明确——部分检测到时间反演对称性破缺（time reversal symmetry breaking）或弱磁矩有序信号，另一些则未发现显著证据。低温STM/STS本应能探测局域环电流有序信号，但缺乏明确的理论预测。

Method: 利用铜氧化物高温超导体及Sr₂RuO₄表面层的理论模型，对正方晶格中的环电流有序在谱学成像（spectroscopic maps）中可观测的信号进行具体预测。

Result: 在环电流有序的特定波矢处，简并（degeneracies）会被解除；当存在自旋-轨道耦合时，系统会产生有限的自旋极化，该特征可在自旋极化STM中检测到。

Conclusion: 提供了利用STM/STS实验检测正方晶格中环电流有序的具体理论指导，特别是自旋极化STM可作为识别该类有序的有效手段。

Abstract: The emergence of loop current phases, where spontaneous loops of orbital currents give rise to a weak local magnetic moments, has been proposed to exist in a number of quantum materials based on measurements that pick up weak signatures of time reversal symmetry breaking or small magnetic moment order. The most prominent example is as an explanation of the pseudogap phase on the underdoped side of the phase diagram of the high-temperature cuprate superconductors, but more recently, it has been proposed to occur in Kagome materials and at the surface layer of Sr$_2$RuO$_4$. Experimental results have, however, been inconclusive so far, some detecting signatures that can be understood as emerging due to loop current phases, whilst others have not detected any significant proof. One of the techniques that should be able to pick up local signatures of loop current orders is low temperature scanning tunneling microscopy and spectroscopy (STM/STS), however firm predictions of how to detect them are missing. Here, we provide specific predictions for how loop current orders in a square lattice can be seen in spectroscopic maps, using models of the cuprate high-temperature superconductors and of the surface layer of Sr$_2$RuO$_4$. We find that, besides lifting degeneracies at the specific ordering vector of the loop current order, a finite spin polarisation emerges when spin-orbit coupling is present, signatures of which can be detected in spin-polarised STM.

### [100] [Coherence-driven origin of metamagnetism in anisotropic heavy-fermion systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20261)
*Ewan Scott,Zheyu Wu,Theodore I. Weinberger,Alexander G. Eaton,Michal P. Kwasigroch*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个重费米子（heavy-fermion）超导体UTe₂中磁各向异性的解析c–f理论，揭示了混合磁化率χ_cf(T,h,p)是统一温度、磁场和压力下各向异性响应的单一热力学观测量，并通过实验数据验证了该理论，表明Kondo相干（Kondo coherence）是奇异硬轴磁化率极大值和超磁相变（metamagnetism）的共同微观起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重费米子材料在外加磁场沿磁硬轴（magnetic hard axis）时表现出的超磁相变（metamagnetism）现象，其显著的磁各向异性（magnetic anisotropy）的微观起源以及硬轴磁化率随温度异常极大值的问题，虽经数十年唯象建模仍未解决，特别是在5f化合物中，相关电子的局域-巡游双重特性使问题更加复杂。

Method: 本文发展了一个解析的c–f理论，引入混合磁化率χ_cf(T,h,p)作为统一描述温度、磁场和压力下各向异性响应的热力学观测量，并通过重费米子超导体UTe₂的原位与文献实验数据对该理论进行定量检验。

Result: 该理论在UTe₂的温度、磁场和压力依赖的磁各向异性演化中与实验数据达到了极佳的定量一致，证实了硬轴磁化率异常极大值源于Kondo相干（Kondo coherence），且该极大值与超磁相变本身直接关联。

Conclusion: 研究建立了一个通用的、基于相干效应的微观各向异性超磁框架，适用于所有呈现该现象的重费米子材料。

Abstract: A number of heavy-fermion materials exhibit magnetic field-induced metamagnetism: on applying a field along the magnetic hard axis, the magnetization first rises gradually, then jumps abruptly once a critical field is reached. Despite decades of phenomenological modeling, the microscopic origin of the pronounced magnetic anisotropy underlying this behavior has remained unresolved. The same is true of a related, long-standing puzzle: an anomalous maximum in the hard-axis susceptibility versus temperature. Both are complicated in $5f$ compounds by the dual localized-itinerant character of the relevant electrons. Here we develop an analytic $c$--$f$ theory of magnetic anisotropy in heavy-fermion metamagnets, identifying the mixed susceptibility $χ_{\rm cf}(T,h,p)$ as a single thermodynamic observable that unifies the anisotropic response across temperature, field, and pressure. We test this theory against primary and literature data for the heavy-fermion superconductor UTe$_2$, finding excellent quantitative agreement in the temperature, field, and pressure evolution of its magnetic anisotropy -- including a Kondo-coherence origin for the anomalous hard-axis susceptibility maximum, which we show is directly connected to the metamagnetic transition itself. Our results establish a general, microscopic, coherence-driven framework for anisotropic metamagnetism, applicable across the broad class of heavy-fermion compounds that display this phenomenology.

Method: 通过对Eu₅In₂As₆材料施加磁场并测量其电阻率随温度、磁场强度以及时间的变化，系统地表征其磁阻记忆效应。

Abstract: Magnetoresistive materials that respond sensitively to applied fields are central to modern data storage technologies. Here we unveil a novel Magnetoresistive Memory (MRM) in Eu$_5$In$_2$As$_6$, where the electrical resistivity depends not only on the magnitude but also on the history of the applied magnetic field. Such an effect has been reported in only two classes of strongly correlated electron systems: perovskite manganites and pyrochlore iridates. In both cases, the effect has been observed in the magnetically ordered phase. It has been attributed to metastable magnetic states in manganites and conducting domain walls in iridates. Remarkably, the MRM in Eu$_5$In$_2$As$_6$ onsets at twice the antiferromagnetic transition temperature, well within the paramagnetic phase. The temperature, field, and time dependence of resistivity suggest that either a hidden order or a fluctuating phase with short-range correlations underlies this effect. Our results offer MRM as a new platform for quantum sensing and memory technologies, and encourage searching for MRM in related materials.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 石墨烯/CrSBr异质结表现出强界面电子与磁耦合所导致的奇异宏观响应（如单轴表面等离激元传播和非传统量子霍尔效应），但其微观电子能带结构机制尚不清楚，亟需从微观层面阐明这些现象的物理起源。

Method: 联合使用角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）、低能电子显微镜（LEEM）和密度泛函理论（DFT）进行综合光谱学表征，并结合拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）提供理论建模支持。

Result: 发现了界面处巨大的电荷重新分布，同时使石墨烯发生空穴掺杂并填充了CrSBr的准一维自旋极化导带，导致界面CrSBr层发生绝缘体-金属相变；CrSBr的电子结构表现出与常规电荷掺杂不同的强动量依赖重整化（momentum-dependent renormalization）；ARPES观测到石墨烯狄拉克锥的分裂特征，与自旋简并解除（spin degeneracy lifting）一致，提供了磁邻近耦合的可能证据。

Conclusion: 这些发现为理解该系统的光学与输运响应提供了关键的微观见解，确立了石墨烯/CrSBr异质结作为电荷转移控制、应变驱动能带工程、磁邻近耦合和方向性受限激发（directionally confined excitations）的多功能平台，应用于下一代自旋电子学（spintronics）和纳米光子学（nanophotonics）器件。

Abstract: Stacking van der Waals materials provides a powerful route to engineer emergent electronic and magnetic behaviors through proximity-driven interactions. The graphene/CrSBr heterostructure has emerged as a compelling platform in this frontier, exhibiting exotic macroscopic responses-- including uniaxial surface-plasmon-polariton propagation and an unconventional quantum Hall effect-- indicative of strong interfacial electronic and magnetic coupling. However, a microscopic electronic landscape governing these phenomena has remained elusive. Here, we provide a comprehensive spectroscopic characterization of the graphene/CrSBr interface using a combination of angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES), low-energy electron microscopy (LEEM), and density functional theory. We resolve a massive redistribution of interfacial charge that concurrently hole dopes graphene and populates the quasi-one-dimensional spin-polarized conduction band of CrSBr, resulting insulator-to-metal transition in the interfacial CrSBr layer. Furthermore, electronic structure of CrSBr exhibits strong momentum-dependent renormalization distinct from conventional charge doping, and theoretical modeling supported by Raman spectroscopy points to additional interfacial compressive strain. In addition, ARPES reveals a splitting-like feature in the graphene Dirac cone consistent with spin degeneracy lifting, providing possible evidence of magnetic proximity coupling. These findings provide crucial microscopic insight into the system's optical and transport responses and establish graphene/CrSBr as a versatile platform for charge-transfer control, strain-driven band engineering, magnetic-proximity coupling, and directionally confined excitations for next-generation spintronic and nanophotonic devices.

</details>


### [103] [Quantum Fisher Information in semiclassical magnon systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20424)
*Wolfgang Simeth,Pontus Laurell,Allen Scheie*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究通过简单理论自旋系统阐明量子Fisher信息（QFI）在凝聚态物质中的物理含义，证明QFI是动量分辨的纠缠深度探针，并在线性自旋波理论（LSWT）框架下揭示其与基态磁振子压缩的关联。研究进一步表明，在阻挫自旋系统的量子临界点附近，QFI会在多个波矢处发散，为量子临界现象提供新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子Fisher信息（QFI）虽已被证明是检测固态材料中多体量子纠缠的有效光谱工具，但其与凝聚态系统其他特征（如磁有序、量子临界性）之间的具体联系尚不明确。本研究旨在通过简单理论自旋系统，阐明QFI在凝聚态物理中的物理意义和解释方式。

Method: 采用有限尺寸自旋系统说明QFI如何量化波函数中动量依赖的量子纠缠深度（entanglement depth）。随后利用半经典阻挫自旋模型，在线性自旋波理论（linear spin wave theory, LSWT）框架下分析QFI与基态磁振子压缩（magnon squeezing）之间的定量关系。

Result: 在反铁磁体（antiferromagnet）中，零能Goldstone模导致LSWT失效，QFI（及纠缠深度）在磁有序波矢处发散。在阻挫自旋系统中，存在经典相图中不出现的涌现量子相（emergent quantum phases）；当趋近这些涌现相时，QFI在动量空间中多个波矢处同时发散。

Conclusion: QFI不仅是纠缠深度的下限（lower bound），更是一种动量分辨的纠缠探针（momentum-resolved probe），为研究量子临界现象（quantum critical phenomena）提供了全新视角。

Abstract: Quantum Fisher Information (QFI) is a powerful spectroscopic tool to witness many-body quantum entanglement in solid state materials, but it is not always obvious how to relate it to other characteristics of condensed matter systems. In this study we elaborate on the meaning and interpretation of QFI in condensed matter by examining simple theoretical spin systems. We use finite sized spin systems to illustrate that QFI quantifies the momentum- dependent degree of quantum entanglement (that is the entanglement depth at a given wave vector) within a wave function. We subsequently use semiclassical frustrated spin models to show that, in the context of linear spin wave theory (LSWT), QFI quantifies the momentum-dependent degree of magnon squeezing in the ground state. In antiferromagnets with a zero-energy Goldstone mode, LSWT breaks down and QFI (and entanglement depth) diverges at the magnetic ordering wave vector. We also show examples of emergent quantum phases in frustrated spin systems that do not appear in classical phase diagrams. When these emergent phases are approached, QFI diverges across multiple wave vectors in momentum space. Taken together, QFI is not only helpful as a lower bound for entanglement depth, but serves as a momentum-resolved probe of entanglement that offers a novel perspective on quantum critical phenomena.

### [104] [On the global well-posedness for the nonlocal Fokas-Lenells equation with the weighted Sobolev initial data on the line](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19649)
*Zhenya Yan,Guoqiang Zhang,Guancheng Zhu*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文通过发展基于黎曼-希尔伯特问题（Riemann-Hilbert problem）的反散射变换（inverse scattering transform），证明了带有加权Sobolev初值的反时空非局域Fokas-Lenells方程（reverse space-time nonlocal Fokas-Lenells equation）柯西问题（Cauchy problem）的整体适定性（global well-posedness），并建立了解映射的Lipschitz连续性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反时空非局域Fokas-Lenells方程在可积系统（integrable system）中具有重要地位，但其整体适定性尚未建立。该问题的主要难点在于：KN型负流谱问题（KN-type negative flow spectral problem）固有的奇异性，以及反时空约化（reverse space-time reduction）导致反射系数（reflection coefficients）失去厄米共轭对称性（Hermitian conjugation symmetry），从而跳跃矩阵（jump matrix）的强制性与预解估计无法先验获得。

Method: 引入谱均匀化变换（spectral uniformization transform）以解决KN型负流谱问题的奇异性。利用初值数据的定量小条件（quantitative smallness condition）获得反射系数的一致有界性，并确保跳跃矩阵厄米部分的一致正定性（uniform positive definiteness）。通过Fredholm与消逝引理（vanishing-lemma）论证，建立相关奇异积分算子（singular integral operator）的有界可逆性。

Result: 在初值 $q_0(x)\in H^{3}(\mathbb{R}) \cap H^{2,1}(\mathbb{R})$ 满足定量小条件时，证明了势与散射数据（scattering data）之间的 $L^{2}$-Sobolev 双射对应，排除了连续谱上的谱奇点（spectral singularities），获得了解的全局存在性与唯一性。此外，解映射在容许初值类上是Lipschitz连续的。

Conclusion: 本文通过系统发展适应于反时空非局域约化的散射与反散射理论，成功克服了跳跃矩阵缺乏先验强制性的困难，完整建立了反时空非局域Fokas-Lenells方程的整体适定性理论。

Abstract: We establish the global well-posedness of the Cauchy problem for the reverse space-time nonlocal Fokas-Lenells equation with the weighted Sobolev initial data $q_0(x)\in H^{3}(\mathbb{R}) \cap H^{2,1}(\mathbb{R})$ on the line. We develop the inverse scattering transform formulated via the associated Riemann-Hilbert problems to study this issue. A spectral uniformization transform is introduced to resolve the singular behavior inherent in the KN-type negative flow spectral problem. Owing to the reverse space-time reduction, reflection coefficients no longer satisfy the usual Hermitian conjugation symmetry, and the coercivity of the jump matrix is therefore not available a priori. The quantitative smallness condition on the initial data yields uniform bounds on the reflection coefficients and ensures the uniform positive definiteness of the Hermitian part of the associated jump matrix. The resulting coercivity allows us to establish the bounded invertibility of the associated singular integral operator through a Fredholm and vanishing-lemma argument. Under this condition, we prove an $L^{2}$-Sobolev bijective correspondence between the potential and scattering data, exclude spectral singularities on continuous spectra, and obtain the global existence and uniqueness of solutions. Moreover, the associated solution map is Lipschitz continuous on the admissible initial-data class.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文证明Kodama与Williams将完全正Grassmannian（totally positive Grassmannian）组合学与KP方程孤立子解相联系的方法，可推广至二维Toda格子（2D Toda lattice）和Davey–Stewartson方程，并基于完全非负Grassmannian（totally nonnegative Grassmannian）为这两种系统推导出了轮廓图生成算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kodama和Williams曾发现KP方程孤立子解的组合结构与Postnikov开创的完全正Grassmannian组合学密切相关，并引入了受热带几何（tropical geometry）多面体结构启发的新型算法。Kodama推测此类方法可推广至二维Toda格子和Davey–Stewartson方程——两个同样由Sato Grassmannian分类孤立子解的可积系统。本文旨在验证该推广是否成立。

Method: 本文从完全非负Grassmannian（totally nonnegative Grassmannian）中的元素出发，针对二维Toda格子和Davey–Stewartson方程分别推导出生成轮廓图（contour plots）的算法。

Result: 成功将Kodama–Williams方法推广至两个目标可积系统，得到了相应的轮廓图生成算法。在渐近（asymptotic）设定下，恢复并细化了Biondini与Wang、以及Biondini、Kireyev与Maruno的前期工作。

Conclusion: Kodama与Williams基于完全正Grassmannian的KP孤立子组合学方法，确实可以推广到二维Toda格子和Davey–Stewartson方程。这进一步揭示了可积系统孤立子解与Grassmannian组合结构之间的深层联系。

Abstract: The KP equation is a prototypical $(2+1)$-dimensional integrable PDE. Its soliton solutions are famously parametrized by the Sato Grassmannian. In seminal work, Kodama and Williams made the surprising discovery that the combinatorics of soliton solutions are intimately related to the combinatorics of the totally positive Grassmannian as pioneered by Postnikov. They introduced novel algorithmic methods inspired by polyhedral structures arising from tropical geometry. Soliton solutions to the 2D Toda lattice and the Davey--Stewartson equation, two closely related integrable systems with soliton solutions, are also classified by the Sato Grassmannian. Kodama suggested that the methods of his work with Williams could generalize to these two integrable equations. In this work, we show that this is indeed the case. We derive algorithms to produce contour plots from elements in the totally nonnegative Grassmannian in both cases. In the asymptotic setting, we recover and refine previous work of Biondini and Wang; as well as Biondini, Kireyev and Maruno.
