### [106] [Electron-Induced Formation of C$_{2}$ on Si(100) from Acetylene and Ethylene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19488)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在+3.2 V及以上偏压激发乙炔可诱导构型转换，包括一种新的亚层键合几何构型（此前被预测为吸附前驱体），以及迁移和脱附；激发还可诱导脱氢生成C₂。在+4.2 V及以上偏压下可诱导三种观测到的C₂构型之间的切换。密度泛函理论（DFT）模拟成功复现了实验图像。此外，场发射电子可在单分子至大于10 nm半径的尺度上诱导脱氢。

Conclusion: 这些观察结果凸显了碳脱氢作为原子级精确制造（APF）的一项附加工具的潜力，为表面图案化与功能化提供了新的技术途径。

Abstract: Hydrogen Desorption Lithography on Si(100) demonstrates the ability of the Scanning Tunneling Microscope (STM) to create functional atomic-scale structures and devices. The dehydrogenation of adsorbed molecules represents a potential complementary technique that has received little attention. For example, formation of C$_{2}$ could introduce local strain or act as centers for subsequent reactions and would inform positionally controlled mechanosynthesis, an approach with vast potential in surface patterning and functionalization. Here, we studied the electron-induced dehydrogenation of acetylene and ethylene on Si(100) at 4 K using STM. Excitation of acetylene at +3.2 V and above induces configurational switching, including to a new sublayer-bonded geometry previously predicted to be an adsorption precursor, as well as migration and desorption. Excitation also induces dehydrogenation to C$_{2}$. Switching between three observed C$_{2}$ configurations can be induced by excitation at +4.2 V and above. Simulations using density functional theory reproduced the experimental images based on choice of functional, dimer-buckling averaging, and inclusion of diffuse basis functions. In addition, dehydrogenation could be induced using field-emitted electrons on a scale ranging from a single molecule to a radius of >10 nm. These observations highlight the potential of carbon dehydrogenation as an additional tool in Atomically Precise Fabrication (APF).

### [107] [Photoemission from Semi-Infinite Crystals: An \emph{Ab Initio} Scattering-State Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19551)
*Tyler Wu,Truman Idso,Siddharth Karkare,Tomás Arias*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无参数的第一性原理（ab initio）框架，通过构建半无限晶体-真空界面的开放散射态，消除光电子发射计算中的人为周期边界，从而实现对Ag(111)表面绝对量子效率、矢量光电子发射和平均横向能量的定量预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光电子发射本质上是逃逸问题，但传统第一性原理计算通常将电子束缚在周期盒子（periodic box）中，引入了人为边界条件（artificial boundary）。现有方法无法自然描述电子从晶体向真空的散射过程，限制了光电子发射关键物理量的定量预测。

Method: 从Wannier哈密顿量（Wannier Hamiltonians）和格林函数嵌入（Green-function embedding）出发，构造半无限晶体-真空界面的开放散射态（open scattering states），得到连续归一化的时间反演低能电子衍射（time-reversed LEED）终态，并包含微观准粒子衰减（microscopic quasiparticle attenuation）。

Result: 对于Ag(111)表面，该方法在实验尺度上预测了绝对量子效率（absolute quantum efficiency）、矢量光电子发射（vectorial photoemission）和平均横向能量（mean transverse energy）。

Conclusion: 该无参数第一性原理框架有效消除了周期边界的人为限制，能够定量描述光电子发射的逃逸过程，为表面光电子发射性质的第一性原理预测提供了可行途径。

Abstract: Photoemission is an escape problem, yet first-principles calculations usually trap the electron in a periodic box. We present a parameter-free \emph{ab initio} framework that removes this artificial boundary by constructing open scattering states for semi-infinite crystal-vacuum interfaces from Wannier Hamiltonians and Green-function embedding. The method gives continuum-normalized time-reversed LEED final states with microscopic quasiparticle attenuation. For Ag(111), it predicts absolute quantum efficiency, vectorial photoemission, and mean transverse energy on the experimental scale.

</details>


### [108] [Assessing the Influence of d-Orbital Radius on the Formation of Localized Photogenerated States in Corundum Metal Oxides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19569)
*Erica P. Craddock,Kathryn E. Knowles*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过对比刚玉族三种金属氧化物（α-Al₂O₃、α-Fe₂O₃、α-Rh₂O₃）的电子、光学和振动性质，揭示了d轨道半径对载流子-声子耦合（carrier-phonon coupling）以及光生极化子（photogenerated polaron）形成机制的影响，发现4d轨道径向扩展导致的晶格共价性增强会改变介导极化子形成的声子模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光生极化子是过渡金属氧化物半导体光物理的基础，理解其形成机制对于实现这类材料在光应用中的潜力至关重要。赤铁矿（α-Fe₂O₃）虽已知会形成光生小极化子（small polaron），但限制了其作为光电催化剂的性能，因此需要更深入地阐明极化子形成的机理。

Method: 采用共振拉曼光谱（resonance Raman spectroscopy）、热差光学光谱（thermal difference optical spectroscopy）以及电子态和振动态的计算建模相结合的方法，系统分析了刚玉族三种金属氧化物：α-Al₂O₃（无d电子）、α-Fe₂O₃（3d）和α-Rh₂O₃（4d）。

Result: α-Al₂O₃因无光吸收，其拉曼光谱随可见区激发波长变化不变；而α-Fe₂O₃和α-Rh₂O₃在吸收起始处均表现出声子与光学跃迁的强耦合，这是激发进入极化子态（polaronic state）的证据。进一步比较发现，α-Rh₂O₃中4d轨道径向扩展增大导致的晶格共价性增强，影响了介导光生极化子形成的声子模式。

Conclusion: d轨道半径的增大（从3d到4d）通过增强晶格共价性，改变了极化子形成过程中耦合的声子模式，揭示了d电子轨道扩展程度对极化子形成机制的关键调控作用。

Abstract: Photogenerated polarons are fundamental to the photophysics of transition metal oxide semiconductors. It is therefore imperative to understand the mechanisms by which polarons form upon photoexcitation of transition metal oxides to realize their potential in photoapplications. Hematite (α-Fe2O3) is known to form photoexcited small polarons, which limit its performance as a photoelectrocatalyst for water oxidation. Here, we report a systematic comparison of the electronic, optical and vibrational properties of hematite to those other metal oxides in the corundum crystal family that elucidates the impact of d-orbital radius on carrier-phonon coupling. Three corundum metal oxides are analyzed: α-Al2O3 (no d-electrons), α-Fe2O3 (3d), and α-Rh2O3 (4d) with a combined approach of resonance Raman spectroscopy, thermal difference optical spectroscopy, and computational modeling of electronic and vibrational states. We find that the Raman spectrum of α-Al2O3 does not change as the Raman excitation is varied across the visible region, as there is no optical absorption. In contrast, both α-Fe2O3 and α-Rh2O3 exhibit strong coupling of phonons to optical transitions at the onset of absorption, which is evidence of excitation into a polaronic state. Closely comparing the optical polaronic properties of α-Fe2O3 and α-Rh2O3, we establish that increased lattice covalency in α-Rh2O3 arising from the increased radial extension of the 4d orbitals influences which phonon modes mediate photogenerated polaron formation.

</details>


### [109] [Macroscopic Polarization and Magnetization from Cavity Vacuum Fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19612)
*Jingkai Quan,Chongxiao Fan,Benshu Fan,I-Te Lu,Dante M. Kennes,Angel Rubio*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文证明腔量子真空涨落（vacuum fluctuations）可以在无外加驱动场的条件下，在原本不具备自发极化或净磁化强度的材料中诱导出宏观极化（polarization）与磁化（magnetization），并通过对称性分析（symmetry analysis）和量子电动力学密度泛函理论（QEDFT）计算给出了相应的响应张量形式及具体材料示例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 腔光-物质相互作用（cavity light-matter interaction）为无需驱动场即可调控材料性质提供了新途径，但腔真空涨落能否在原本不具备自发极化或净磁化的材料中诱导出宏观极化和磁化，尚缺乏系统性的对称性指导原则。

Method: 从有效无光子量子电动力学哈密顿量（effective photon-free QED Hamiltonian）出发，识别出所有允许腔诱导响应的晶体学（磁性）点群（crystallographic (magnetic) point groups）；基于对称性分析推导对应响应张量（response tensors）的形式，并通过量子电动力学密度泛函理论（QEDFT）计算获取张量元。

Result: 在α-石英（α-quartz）中，腔诱导极化可通过旋转腔体实现连续调控；在反铁磁Mn₃Sn中，腔诱导对称性破缺（cavity-induced symmetry breaking）产生了面外磁化（out-of-plane magnetization），并伴随一个在腔外被禁阻的反常霍尔电导（anomalous Hall conductivity）分量。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了对称性作为腔材料工程（cavity materials engineering）的指导原则，提供了一条通过量子真空涨落控制极化和磁化的新路径。

Abstract: Cavity light-matter interaction has recently emerged as a new avenue for manipulating material properties without driving fields. Here, we demonstrate that cavity vacuum fluctuations can induce macroscopic polarization (magnetization), even in materials that lack spontaneous polarization (net magnetization) in free space. Starting from the effective photon-free quantum-electrodynamics Hamiltonian, we identify all crystallographic (magnetic) point groups that allow such cavity-induced responses. We derive the form of the corresponding response tensors based on symmetry analysis, whose elements can be obtained by quantum electrodynamical density functional theory (QEDFT) calculations. As representative examples, we show that the cavity-induced polarization in $α$-quartz can be continuously controlled by rotating the cavity. For antiferromagnetic Mn$_3$Sn, we demonstrate that cavity-induced symmetry breaking generates an out-of-plane magnetization, accompanied by an anomalous Hall conductivity component that is forbidden outside the cavity. Our work establishes symmetry as a guiding principle for cavity materials engineering and provides a route for controlling polarization and magnetization through quantum vacuum fluctuations, i.e., cavity materials engineering.

</details>

In addition, artificial intelligence computing has been demonstrated using spintronic devices. Further progress of these devices can be anticipated through the development of unique and functional materials beyond the existing heavy metals and topological systems with strong spin-orbit coupling. The nitride materials exhibit unique chemical, magnetic, and structural versatility, including antiferromagnetism, high thermal stability, and compatibility with diverse device architectures. Here, we propose Nitrospinics as a conceptual and functional framework that exploits nitride materials for applications ranging from orbital-torque-based spintronic devices to artificial intelligence hardware. Using Cr2N, a two-dimensional nitride MXene with an atomic layered structure, as a prototype system, we discuss how nitrogen contributes to the structural stability, the orbital torque generation, and the interfacial orbital and spin conversion. We further outline key challenges and opportunities toward establishing nitride-based materials for next-generation computing technologies.

### [111] [Raman spectroscopy of van der Waals topological magnet GdGaI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19663)
*Nan Jiang,Yijin Zhang,Yujie Xia,Tomo Higashihara,Ryutaro Okuma,Jun-ichi Yamaura,Yoshinori Okada,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Tiantian Zhang,Tomoki Machida,Yasuhiro Niimi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过偏振分辨拉曼光谱（polarization-resolved Raman spectroscopy）研究了候选激子绝缘体（excitonic insulator）范德华化合物 GdGaI，识别出六个拉曼活性声子（Raman-active phonons），未发现任何晶格畸变或软模信号，支持电子驱动（electronically driven）的能带重构机制；同时观察到 A₁g 模式在面外磁场下的显著圆二色性（circular dichroism），将其归因于时间反演对称破缺态下自旋-声子耦合（spin-phonon coupling）产生的手性声子（chiral phonons），并证明圆偏振拉曼光谱可灵敏探测激子系统中的自旋-声子耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激子绝缘体（excitonic insulator）是凝聚态物理中尚未被充分证实的量子相，其起源是电子-空穴配对还是电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）驱动存在争议。GdGaI 作为候选材料，需要明确区分其能带重构成的驱动机制，并探索其中可能存在的自旋-声子耦合与圆偏振声子行为。

Method: 采用偏振分辨拉曼光谱（polarization-resolved Raman spectroscopy）对范德华化合物 GdGaI 进行测量，结合对称性分析（symmetry analysis）与密度泛函理论计算（density functional theory, DFT）识别拉曼活性声子。在面外磁场（out-of-plane magnetic field）下测量圆偏振拉曼信号，并分析其温度演化。

Result: 识别出六个拉曼活性声子。光谱在 4 K 下仅呈现预期的非简谐硬化（anharmonic hardening），未出现额外峰、软模（soft modes）或能带折叠（zone folding）信号。在面外磁场下观察到 A₁g 模式的显著圆二色性（circular dichroism）。圆偏振度的温度演化显示短程反铁磁关联（short-range antiferromagnetic correlations）的出现。

Conclusion: GdGaI 中的能带重构源于电子驱动机制而非电子-声子驱动机制。圆偏振拉曼光谱可灵敏探测时间反演对称破缺态下自旋-声子耦合产生的手性声子（chiral phonons）。GdGaI 是一个可交织激子序（excitonic order）、磁性与圆偏振声子的理想平台。

Abstract: We report polarization-resolved Raman spectroscopy of a van der Waals compound GdGaI that is a candidate for excitonic insulators. By combining the symmetry analysis with density functional theory calculations, we identify six Raman-active phonons. The spectra exhibit only the expected anharmonic hardening down to 4 K: no additional peaks, no soft modes, and no signatures of zone folding are observed. This result indicates that any lattice distortion is below our experimental sensitivity, supporting an electronically driven origin for the band reconstruction reported by angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy rather than an electron-phonon-driven mechanism. Moreover, we observe a pronounced circular dichroism of the $A_{1g}$ modes under an out-of-plane magnetic field. Based on symmetry considerations, we attribute this dichroic response to chiral $A_{1g}$ phonons with opposite angular momenta generated by spin-phonon coupling in the time-reversal-broken state. The temperature evolution of the degree of circular polarization further suggests that circularly polarized Raman spectroscopy detects the emergence of short-range antiferromagnetic correlations. Our results highlight GdGaI as a promising platform in which excitonic order, magnetism, and circularly polarized phonons can be intertwined, and demonstrate that circular-polarization Raman provides a sensitive probe of spin-phonon coupling in excitonic systems.

Conclusion: 定制化的电解质组成和复合正极结构显著提升了循环稳定性和界面保护能力。硅掺杂锑型碘化物硫银锗矿（Si-doped antimony-type iodide argyrodites）在全固态电池领域具有重要应用潜力，能够在多种热条件下实现持久运行。

Abstract: Solid-state lithium-ion batteries (LIBs) are increasingly recognized for their exceptional energy density and safety. However, their widespread adoption is challenged by persistent issues such as thermal and electrochemical instability, dendrite formation, and limited compatibility with high-voltage cathodes. Sulfide-based solid electrolytes (SEs), particularly iodide argyrodites, offer outstanding ionic conductivity and stability; however, their practical application is constrained by the formation of space-charge layers, slow ion transport, and susceptibility to dendrite penetration. To address these challenges, we synthesized a novel Li6.6Si0.6Sb0.4S5I argyrodite electrolyte via ball milling and heat treatment, achieving a remarkable room-temperature ionic conductivity of 9.9 mS cm^-1. Our study shows that tailored electrolyte composition and a composite cathode configuration significantly enhance cycling stability and improve interfacial protection. These findings highlight the potential of Si-doped antimony-type iodide argyrodites for next-generation high-performance all-solid-state batteries, offering durable operation under diverse thermal conditions.

### [113] [Analytical Retrieval of Material Parameters in Monolayer Transition-Metal Dichalcogenides Based on a Solvable Exciton Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19698)
*Duy-Nhat Ly,Thanh-Son Nguyen,Ngoc-Tram D. Hoang,Van-Hoang Le*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于可解修正Kratzer模型的分析方法，用于从光学和磁光激子光谱中反演单层过渡金属二硫族化物的基本材料参数。该方法分为两个互补阶段：第一阶段通过显式反演公式从三个最低激子态能量直接确定准粒子带隙、有效屏蔽参数和能量标度因子；第二阶段利用激子能量随磁场的解析表达式独立获得约化激子质量和周围介电常数。该方法无需额外拟合参数或矩阵对角化，即可解析预测抗磁系数、激子半径和完整磁激子谱，并在WSe₂、WS₂、MoS₂、MoSe₂和MoTe₂等多种单层材料中验证了与实验和Rytova-Keldysh计算结果的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从光学和磁光激子谱中准确反演单层过渡金属二硫族化物（transition-metal dichalcogenides）的基本材料参数，是二维半导体研究中的重要问题。现有数值拟合方法缺乏物理透明性和分析便捷性，因此需要一种高效且物理清晰的解析方法。

Method: 基于可解的修正Kratzer模型（modified Kratzer model），构建了两阶段分析流程。第一阶段利用三个最低激子态的实验测量能量，通过显式反演公式（explicit inversion formulas）确定准粒子带隙（quasiparticle bandgap）、有效屏蔽参数（effective screening parameter）和能量标度因子（energy scaling factor），进而得到屏蔽长度（screening length）。第二阶段基于激子能量随磁场变化的解析表达式，独立获得约化激子质量（reduced exciton mass），并由此计算周围介电常数（surrounding dielectric constant）。

Result: 该方法成功应用于WSe₂、WS₂、MoS₂、MoSe₂和MoTe₂等多种单层材料的实验数据，涵盖不同介电环境下的样品。反演得到的材料参数与独立实验测量结果及基于Rytova-Keldysh（RK）势的数值计算吻合良好；预测的激子性质准确再现了可用的磁光实验观测结果。

Conclusion: 所提出的解析理论为传统数值拟合流程提供了一种高效、物理透明的替代方案，可作为通过激子光谱学（excitonic spectroscopy）快速表征二维半导体的有效工具。

Abstract: We develop an analytical procedure to retrieve fundamental material parameters of monolayer transition-metal dichalcogenides from optical and magneto-optical exciton spectra, based on the solvable modified Kratzer model. The proposed retrieval procedure naturally consists of two complementary stages. In the first stage, explicit inversion formulas determine the quasiparticle bandgap, effective screening parameter, and energy scaling factor directly from the experimentally measured energies of the three lowest excitonic states, from which the screening length is subsequently obtained. In the second stage, an analytical expression for the magnetic-field dependence of the exciton energies independently yields the reduced exciton mass, from which the surrounding dielectric constant is then calculated. Once the complete set of material parameters has been retrieved, the framework analytically predicts the diamagnetic coefficients, exciton radii, and complete magnetoexciton spectra without introducing additional fitting parameters or matrix diagonalization. The method is applied to a broad range of experimental samples for WSe$_2$, WS$_2$, MoS$_2$, MoSe$_2$, and MoTe$_2$ monolayers embedded in different dielectric environments. The retrieved material parameters are in good agreement with independent experimental measurements and previous Rytova--Keldysh (RK) calculations, while the predicted excitonic properties accurately reproduce available magneto-optical observations. The proposed analytical theory provides an efficient, physically transparent alternative to conventional numerical fitting procedures and offers an effective tool for the rapid characterization of two-dimensional semiconductors via excitonic spectroscopy.

### [114] [A Thermodynamic Pinning Criterion for Two-Dimensional Structural Superlubricity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19732)
*Li Wang,Yunjie Ye*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过严格定义零温完全滑动相（fully sliding phase）和钉扎相（pinned phase），证明了干净的无限莫尔连续体（moiré continuum）可以在不产生体滑动势垒（bulk sliding barrier）的情况下重建。通过对石墨烯/六方氮化硼二维离散模型的数值测试，发现所考察的零温面内模型均与弹性弛豫滑动状态一致，并指出参数Λ=1是重建标度（reconstruction scale）而非静态相判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非公度性（incommensurability）和弹性重建（elastic reconstruction）本身并不足以定义结构超润滑相（structurally superlubric phase），需要建立更严格的相定义和判据来区分滑动和钉扎状态。

Method: 利用上极限和下极限定义零温完全滑动相与钉扎相的严格判据；通过平移协变性（translational covariance）证明连续莫尔模型的重建不产生滑动势垒；在石墨烯/六方氮化硼二维离散模型中采用扩散量子蒙特卡罗（diffusion quantum Monte Carlo, DMC）第一星势和15次谐波Leven势，在三种有理近似（rational approximant）和五个方向上测试平衡态和亚稳态势垒。

Result: 所有物理耦合测试均未解析出平衡态或亚稳态势垒；Leven势的最高Λ值从0.142提升至0.212；人为将Λ标度调至1时，在尺寸无关阈值出现前应变已不可控。Λ=1是重建标度，并非静态相判据。

Conclusion: 所测试的零温面内模型与弹性弛豫滑动状态（elastically relaxed sliding regime）一致；Λ这一参数量化的是重建敏感性（reconstruction susceptibility），而非直接定义滑动或钉扎相。

Abstract: Incommensurability and elastic reconstruction do not by themselves define a structurally superlubric phase. We define fully sliding and pinned zero-temperature phases by $\limsup_{A\to\infty}τ_{\rm dep}^{\max}(A)=0$ and $\liminf_{A\to\infty}τ_{\rm dep}^{\min}(A)>0$, respectively; $Λ_n=|V_n|G_{n,i}[D_{\rm rel}^{-1}(\mathbf q_n)]_{ij}G_{n,j}$ measures only reconstruction susceptibility. Translational covariance then proves that a clean, smooth, infinite moiré continuum can reconstruct without acquiring a bulk sliding barrier. We restore atomic sampling in a two-dimensional discrete model of graphene/hBN and test both a diffusion quantum Monte Carlo first-star potential and a 15-harmonic Leven potential across three rational approximants and five directions. No physical-coupling equilibrium or metastable barrier is resolved. The Leven spectrum raises the largest tested $Λ$ from $0.142$ to $0.212$, while artificial scaling through $Λ=1$ reaches uncontrolled strain before a size-independent threshold appears. The tested zero-temperature in-plane models are therefore consistent with an elastically relaxed sliding regime; $Λ=1$ is a reconstruction scale, not a static phase criterion.

</details>


### [115] [Numerical exploration on unveiling the photovoltaic potential of MgXS3(X = Ti, Zr, Hf) chalcogenide perovskites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19789)
*Md. Mizanur Rahman,Md. Nahid Hasan,Tanvir Ahmed,Jaker Hossain*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过三维有限元全耦合光-电-热模拟，系统研究了基于MgXS₃(X = Ti, Zr, Hf)硫族钙钛矿(chalcogenide perovskite)吸收层的无铅ZnSe/MgXS₃/Sb₂S₃太阳能电池，优化后MgZrS₃、MgTiS₃和MgHfS₃基器件分别实现了28.18%、26.72%和28.16%的功率转换效率(PCE)，并揭示了由非辐射复合和焦耳耗散主导的微小稳态温升特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用COMSOL Multiphysics中的三维有限元模拟，在AM 1.5G 1-sun光照下执行光学生成、漂移-扩散载流子输运和热传递的全耦合光-电-热(self-consistent opto-electro-thermal)自洽模拟，并系统研究吸收层厚度、掺杂浓度和缺陷密度的影响，同时量化Sb₂S₃背表面场(BSF)层对载流子收集和光谱响应的贡献。

Result: 优化条件下，MgZrS₃、MgTiS₃和MgHfS₃基器件的模拟PCE分别达28.18%、26.72%和28.16%；对应开路电压(VOC)为0.94 V、0.74 V和1.07 V，短路电流密度(JSC)为34.46 mA/cm²、42.69 mA/cm²和29.89 mA/cm²，填充因子(FF)为86.99%、84.58%和88.02%。电-热耦合模拟显示超薄电池堆叠中存在微小的空间非均匀稳态温升，主要由活性层内的非辐射复合和焦耳耗散(Joule dissipation)主导。

Conclusion: MgXS₃(X = Ti, Zr, Hf)硫族钙钛矿被证实是有前景的无铅吸收层材料，该研究为实现高效、热稳定的三维器件架构提供了实用设计指导。

Abstract: Lead-free chalcogenide perovskites offer a nontoxic and thermally robust path beyond Pb-based perovskite solar cells (PSCs), but their device-level behavior in realistic three-dimensional geometries remains insufficiently characterized. In this work, we investigate ZnSe/MgXS3(X = Ti, Zr, Hf)/Sb2S3 solar cell architecture where MgXS3 absorbers from the II-IV-VI chalcogenide perovskite family is employed as the absorber layer. The device is analyzed using 3D finite-element simulations in COMSOL Multiphysics that self-consistently couple optical generation, drift-diffusion carrier transport, and heat transfer under AM 1.5G 1-sun illumination, following a fully coupled opto-electro-thermal framework. For each absorber composition, the impacts of absorber thickness, doping, and defect density are systematically investigated, and the contribution of an Sb2S3 back-surface-field (BSF) layer to carrier collection and spectral response is quantified. Under optimized conditions, MgZrS3, MgTiS3, MgHfS3-based devices achieves a simulated power conversion efficiency (PCE) of 28.18%, 26.72%, and 28.16%, respectively. The corresponding open-circuit voltage (VOC) values are 0.94 V, 0.74 V, and, 1.07 V while the short-circuit current density (JSC) values are 34.46 mA/cm2, 42.69 mA/cm2, and 29.89 mA/cm2, with fill factor (FF) values of 86.99%, 84.58%, and 88.02%, respectively. Coupled electro-thermal simulations further reveal a small spatially non-uniform steady-state temperature rise across the ultrathin cell stack, mainly governed by non-radiative recombination and Joule dissipation within the active layers. Overall, these results confirm MgXS3(X = Ti, Zr, Hf) chalcogenide perovskites as promising lead-free absorber materials and offer practical design guidance for achieving high-efficiency, thermally stable three-dimensional device architectures.

</details>


### [116] [The origin of ferroelectricity, polarization and high resistivity in Aurivillius CaBi2B2O9 (B = Ta, Nb)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19885)
*Fengzhang Tang,Shi Wei,Qi Hu,Jie Xing,Jianguo Zhu,Zhi Tan,Qiang Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究结合群论分析（group theoretic analysis）与第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），系统揭示了双层Aurivillius铁电体CaBi₂B₂O₉（B = Ta, Nb）中铁电相变、极化、压电响应及电绝缘性的微观起源，并识别出层间滑移（interlayer sliding）作为Aurivillius氧化物中一种与层数无关的通用铁电机理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Aurivillius层状氧化物是高温铁电和压电应用的重要候选材料，但其铁电相变、极化、压电响应及绝缘性的微观起源尚未得到系统理解，缺乏统一的微观图像。

Method: 采用群论分析（group theoretic analysis）与第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）相结合的方法，对双层Aurivillius铁电体CaBi₂B₂O₉（B = Ta, Nb）的结构畸变与铁电性质进行系统性研究。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了CaBi₂B₂O₉（B = Ta, Nb）中结构畸变、铁电极化、压电响应和电绝缘性的统一微观图像，为设计具有高居里温度（Curie temperature）和良好绝缘性的层状铁电氧化物提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Aurivillius layered oxides are important candidates for high-temperature ferroelectric and piezoelectric application. In this work, we combine group theoretic analysis with first-principles calculations to systematically investigate the origin of ferroelectric phase transition, polarization, piezoelectric response, and intrinsic electrical insulation of the two-layer Aurivillius ferroelectrics CaBi$_{2}$B$_{2}$O$_{9}$ (B = Ta, Nb). The results show that the \textit{A2$_1$am} ferroelectric phase arises from the cooperative condensation of a polar mode and nonpolar oxygen octahedral rotation/tilting modes, whose the $Γ_5^-$X$_2^+$X$_3^-$ trilinear coupling substantially lowers the total energy and deepens the ferroelectric potential well. The spontaneous polarization and anisotropic piezoelectric response are governed primarily by the cooperative displacements of the Bi$_{2}$O$_{2}$ layers and Ta/NbO$_{6}$ octahedra, with Bi ions providing an indispensable contribution to both responses. More importantly, the polar distortion can be traced to the relative in-plane displacement between adjacent the Bi$_{2}$O$_{2}$ layer and the perovskite-like block. Because this displacement is intrinsic to the alternating Bi$_{2}$O$_{2}$/perovskite-block stacking topology and is independent of the number of perovskite layers, we identify interlayer sliding as a general, layer-number-independent structural mechanism for ferroelectricity in Aurivillius oxides. Our findings establish a unified microscopic picture linking structural distortions, ferroelectric polarization, piezoelectric response, and electronic insulation in CaBi$_{2}$B$_{2}$O$_{9}$ (B = Ta, Nb), and provide theoretical guidance for designing layered ferroelectric oxides with high Curie temperatures and robust insulating behavior.

### [117] [Symmetry-Based Design Rules for Second-Harmonic Generation in Stacked and Twisted MoS2 Bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19937)
*Sumanti Patra,Caterina Cocchi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个基于对称性的理论框架，将MoS₂双层结构的四种点群（D3h、D3d、C3v、C3）与二阶磁化率张量χ^(2)映射，揭示了通过对称性破缺调控非线性光学响应的机制，并发现扭转构型（C3群）中面内分量χ_xxx的激活导致二次谐波极瓣的刚体方位旋转，旋转角度锁定为扭转角的一半且与频率无关，为扭转角测定和非线性光学响应工程提供了直接路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于群论（group theory）的对称性分析方法，建立MoS₂双层结构在四种点群（point groups）配置下的结构-二阶磁化率张量（second-order susceptibility tensor χ^(2)）映射关系，并以第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）作为基准验证。

Result: 对称性破缺（symmetry breaking）控制着单个张量元素的激活与抑制；在扭转构型（C3群）中，面内分量χ_xxx被激活，导致二次谐波产生（second-harmonic generation, SHG）的极瓣发生刚体方位旋转，该旋转角度锁定为结构扭转角（twist angle）的一半，且在整个光谱范围内与频率无关。

Conclusion: 本工作确立了一种直接的、与波长无关的光学路径用于扭转角测定，并为二维材料中非线性光学响应的工程化设计提供了清晰的路线图。

Abstract: Understanding how stacking controls the nonlinear optical response of two-dimensional materials is key to designing van der Waals heterostructures with tailored functionalities. Here, we establish a comprehensive symmetry-based framework mapping the structural configuration of MoS2 bilayers across four point groups (D3h, D3d, C3v, C3) to their second-order susceptibility tensor chi^(2). Using group-theory arguments benchmarked against first-principles calculations, we demonstrate how symmetry breaking controls the activation and suppression of individual tensor elements in these systems. We show that the emergence of the in-plane component chi_xxx in twisted configurations (C3 group) induces a rigid azimuthal rotation of the second-harmonic generation polar lobes, which remains frequency-independent across the entire optical spectrum, locking to half of the structural twist angle. Our findings establish a direct, wavelength-independent optical route for twist-angle determination and provide a clear roadmap for engineering nonlinear optical responses in two-dimensional materials.

Conclusion: 惰性气体氟化物为TMD异质结构中的载流子密度非接触调控（noncontact engineering）提供了高效途径，为在二维材料中调控关联电子相（correlated electronic phases）提供了新策略。

Recently, the concept of a chemical capacitor has been proposed as a route to achieving exceptionally high carrier densities through CT across insulating separator layers. Here, we extend this concept to van der Waals heterostructures by investigating TMD hBN OX, oxidizer, systems using density functional theory, DFT. The resulting charge redistribution demonstrates that noble gas fluorides provide an efficient route for noncontact engineering of carrier density in TMD heterostructures, offering a new strategy for tuning correlated electronic phases in two dimensional materials.

The co-integration of these phenomena into a single multifunctional device is an important step toward harnessing the re-programmability of memristive systems with the high yield and varied functionality of MTJs. This study demonstrates the co-existence of magnetoresistance and memristive properties on MgO-based MTJs. Abstract: Freestanding ferroelectric oxide membranes offer a promising route toward silicon-integrated low-power electronic and memory devices, but reproducible membrane quality remains challenging, particularly in ultrathin BaTiO3 (BTO), where cracking and wrinkling hinder integration. Here, we show that crack and wrinkle formation in released BaTiO3 membranes can be tuned by jointly controlling oxide thickness and polymer support thickness. ### [122] [Kinetically-Arrested Phase Separation leads to Tunable Domain Structures in Vapor-Deposited Glasses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20066)
*A T M Mahbub Alahe,Thomas J. Ferron,Camille E. Bishop*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过改变共沉积有机薄膜（TPD与DO37混合物）的沉积速率，系统地揭示了动力学效应对相分离形态的影响。利用功率谱密度（PSD）分析原子力显微镜（AFM）图像和共振软X射线散射（RSoXS）测量，发现沉积速率直接调控表面和体相中多个长度尺度的畴尺寸，表明表面平衡机制（surface equilibration mechanism）在多组分薄膜中驱动了相分离和粗化过程，直至动力学冻结。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在恒定衬底温度下对共沉积的分子玻璃共混物——TPD（N,N'-bis(3-methylphenyl)-N,N'-diphenylbenzidine）与DO37（Disperse Orange 37）——进行不同速率的沉积。利用原子力显微镜（atomic force microscopy, AFM）图像的功率谱密度（power spectral density, PSD）分析量化形态对沉积速率的依赖关系，并通过共振软X射线散射（Resonant Soft X-ray Scattering, RSoXS）进行体相表征。

Result: 在表面观察到两种不同的沉积速率依赖长度尺度，表明沉积动力学直接影响畴尺寸和薄膜形貌。RSoXS测量结果指出相分离贯穿整个薄膜厚度。这些观察结果与先前描述的均匀气相沉积薄膜的表面平衡机制一致。

Conclusion: 在多元组分共混物中，表面平衡机制使沉积过程中分子部分平衡为不同的表面模板化状态，从而发生相分离和粗化，形成具有多个长度尺度的结构，直至动力学冻结，而冻结程度取决于沉积速率。沉积速率对畴尺寸的精细可调性为设计具有特定形貌的新型有机电子器件提供了策略。

Abstract: The characteristic length scale of phase-separated organic thin film blends is a critical structural parameter governing the performance and functionality of organic electronic devices. The arrested morphologies of vapor-deposited organic thin films result from the interplay between thermodynamic driving forces and kinetic constraints during deposition. Here, we aim to isolate the role of kinetic effects in phase separation by varying the deposition rate at a constant substrate temperature for a co-deposited molecular glass blend of N,N'-bis(3-methylphenyl)-N,N'-diphenylbenzidine (TPD) and Disperse Orange 37 (DO37). The dependence of morphology on deposition rate is quantified using power spectral density (PSD) analysis of atomic force microscopy (AFM) images. Two distinct deposition rate-dependent length scales at the surface reveal how deposition kinetics directly influence domain size and film topography. Complementary Resonant Soft X-ray Scattering (RSoXS) measurements indicate that phase separation extends throughout the film thickness. These observations are consistent with the surface equilibration mechanism previously described for homogeneous vapor-deposited films, in which enhanced surface mobility allows molecules in the growing film to partially equilibrate into distinct surface-templated states during deposition. In the current work, this mechanism allows the multi-component blend to phase separate and coarsen into a structure with multiple length scales before kinetically arresting to an extent that depends on the deposition rate. The demonstration of finely tunable domain size with deposition rate provides strategies to design new organic electronic devices with desired morphologies.

</details>


### [123] [From MLIPs to Microstructure: A High-Throughput Computational Framework to Design Spinodal Alloys in High-Dimensional Composition Spaces via Analytic Derivatives of CALPHAD Model Predictions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20077)
*Courtney Kunselman,Doguhan Sariturk,Siya Zhu,Vahid Attari,Raymundo Arroyave*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于机器学习原子间势（MLIP）和CALPHAD方法的开源工作流，用于高维多组元合金体系的自旋odal分解（spinodal decomposition）稳定性分析与微观结构预测。该工作流通过高通量MLIP弹性常数计算捕捉相干应变效应，利用MLIP生成的热力学模型驱动弹-化学相场模拟，并采用解析推导的Gibbs能Hessian矩阵提升计算效率与精度，最终以Hf-Nb-Ti-V四元系为例进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高维成分空间中识别发生自旋odal分解（spinodal decomposition）的区域是合金设计的关键环节。此外，当设计者希望利用自旋odal微观结构来调控合金性能时，还需预测微观结构的演化与形貌。现有方法在高通量分析与计算效率方面存在不足。

Method: 本文构建了一个结合机器学习原子间势（Machine Learning Interatomic Potential, MLIP）与CALPHAD方法的开源工作流。相干应变贡献通过高通量MLIP弹性常数计算获取；针对感兴趣成分的微观结构形貌，则将MLIP生成的热力学模型输入弹-化学相场（elasto-chemical phase field）模拟。稳定性分析与相场模拟均使用解析推导的Gibbs能Hessian矩阵，以替代有限差分近似，从而提高计算效率与精度。

Result: 该工作流成功应用于Hf-Nb-Ti-V四元体系（quaternary system）的微观结构稳定性分析，验证了其在多组元合金设计中的可行性与有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的MLIP-CALPHAD集成工作流为高维成分空间中自旋odal分解的稳定性分析与微观结构形貌预测提供了一种高通量、高精度的开源方案，有望加速先进合金的设计与开发。

Abstract: Identifying regions of design space subject to spinodal decomposition is a critical component of alloy design in high-dimensional composition spaces. In cases where designers are seeking to exploit spinodal microstructures to tailor alloy properties, prediction of microstructure evolution and morphology is also needed. In this work, we present a Machine Learning Interatomic Potential (MLIP)-trained, CALPHAD-based, open-source workflow for high-throughput microstructure stability analysis and visualization. In this workflow, coherent strain contributions are captured via high-throughput MLIP elastic constant calculations. To predict microstructure morphology for compositions of interest, MLIP-generated thermodynamic models are fed into an elasto-chemical phase field simulation. Both stability analyses and phase-field simulations utilize analytically-derived Gibbs energy Hessians to improve computational efficiency and accuracy over finite difference approximations. We demonstrate this workflow by investigating microstructure stability in the Hf-Nb-Ti-V quaternary system.

</details>


### [124] [Role of Resonant $\mathbf{k}$-Points in the Transient Optical Response of Pumped Germanium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20240)
*Amir Eskandari-asl,Giacomo Inzani,Matteo Lucchini,Adolfo Avella*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过将泵浦诱导的瞬态吸收响应分解为1、2、3光子共振动量空间类别，揭示了在泵浦锗（germanium）中瞬态光学性质主要由共振区域主导，但不同共振类别的光学权重与激发后剩余布居数之间存在显著不对应，表明瞬态光学权重不仅由实电荷动力学决定，还包含显著的虚泵浦诱导贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 泵浦诱导的瞬态光学性质包含整个布里渊区（Brillouin zone）电子态的贡献，但离共振与单光子共振晶体动量（crystal momenta）的相对重要性尚未被探索，本文旨在解决这一问题。

Method: 采用动力学投影算符方法（Dynamical Projective Operatorial Approach）及其广义线性响应理论（generalized linear response theory），将瞬态吸收响应按是否存在1、2、3光子共振分解为动量空间类别，计算介电函数（dielectric function）的微分虚部并评估各类别贡献。

Result: 共振区域几乎贡献了整个光学响应，而非共振点贡献可忽略；2光子共振集虽包含超过98%的激发后剩余布居数，但未能复现完整瞬态光谱；相反，剩余布居极小的共振类别却产生不可忽略的瞬态光学贡献。

Conclusion: 瞬态光学权重并非仅由实电荷动力学（real-charge dynamics）决定，还包含显著的虚泵浦诱导贡献，但其主导光学权重仍来自动量空间共振区域；各类别的振荡相位与全信号相位一致，为多光子共振与瞬态光学可观测量之间提供了动量分辨的联系。

Abstract: Pump-induced transient optical properties combine contributions from electronic states throughout the Brillouin zone, but the relative relevance of off-resonant and l-photon resonant crystal momenta has remained unexplored. We address this issue in pumped germanium by resolving the transient absorptive response into momentum-space classes defined by the presence or absence of 1-, 2-, and 3-photon resonances with respect to the pump. Using the Dynamical Projective Operatorial Approach together with the related generalized linear response theory, we compute the differential imaginary part of the dielectric function and evaluate the contributions of each resonance class. Resonant regions account for nearly the entire optical response, whereas points outside the identified resonance sets contribute only negligibly. Nevertheless, the 2-photon-resonant set, although containing more than 98% of the residual (post-pump) excitation population, does not reproduce the full transient spectrum. Conversely, resonance classes with very small residual populations generate non-negligible contributions to the transient optical properties. This mismatch shows that the transient optical weight is not determined solely by the real-charge dynamics (which results in post-pulse residual excitation population) and is consistent with substantial virtual pump-induced contributions, whose dominant optical weight nevertheless arises from the resonant regions of momentum space. The class-resolved phase of the dominant 2$ω_{\mathrm{pu}}$ oscillations further shows that, whenever a class contributes appreciably, the phase of its oscillatory component follows that of the corresponding full signal. The resulting decomposition provides a momentum-resolved connection among multi-photon resonances and transient optical observables in a realistic material.

</details>


### [125] [Competing ferromagnetic and antiferromagnetic interactions in non-altermagnetic Ru$_{1-x}$Cr$_{x}$O$_{2}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20298)
*David T. Plouff,Nawsher J. Parvez,Subhash Bhatt,Xixiang Zhang,Adam A. Aczel,Jonathan Gaudet,John Q. Xiao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过实验研究了在RuO₂中掺杂Cr离子（hole doping）以诱导交变磁性（altermagnetism）的方案。制备了Ru₁₋ₓCrₓO₂薄膜样品，并通过中子衍射和磁化率测量发现，样品中并未出现长程交变磁序，而是表现为反铁磁耦合的CrO₂铁磁团簇共存，表明空穴局域在Cr离子上，未能掺杂进入Ru能带（Ru bands）以诱导交变磁态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究通过Cr离子对RuO₂进行空穴掺杂（hole doping）以诱导交变磁性（altermagnetism）这一理论方案的实验可行性。

Method: 采用反应磁控共溅射（reactive magnetron co-sputtering）在TiO₂衬底上制备了Ru₁₋ₓCrₓO₂（0 ≤ x ≤ 0.28）薄膜样品；使用X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction）验证外延生长性质，结合X射线光电子能谱（X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy）与Ar刻蚀测定成分深度分布；利用中子衍射（neutron diffraction）和温度依赖磁化率（temperature dependent susceptibility）测量样品的磁结构。

Result: 中子衍射显示x=0和x=0.23样品在低温下均无沿c轴或ab面内的长程交变磁序（long-range altermagnetic order）。x≥0.16样品在T≈20 K以下出现磁化率逐渐下降，暗示反铁磁相互作用（antiferromagnetic interactions），但x≥0.23样品在4 K时同时存在铁磁磁滞（ferromagnetic hysteresis）和剩余磁化（remnant magnetization）。综合磁强计和中子散射测量表明，样品中反铁磁耦合的CrO₂铁磁团簇共存。

Conclusion: Cr离子并未对Ru能带进行空穴掺杂以诱导交变磁态，而是空穴局域在Cr离子上（holes remain localized to the Cr ions），形成CrO₂铁磁团簇并由反铁磁耦合共存。

Abstract: We investigate the proposal of hole doping RuO$_{2}$ via alloying with Cr ions to induce altermagnetism. Thin film samples of Ru$_{1-x}$Cr$_{x}$O$_{2}$ ($0 \leq x \leq 0.28$) were prepared by reactive magnetron co-sputtering on TiO$_{2}$ substrates, with epitaxial nature verified by X-ray diffraction and composition depth profiles determined by X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy combined with Ar etching. Neutron diffraction measurements of samples with $x = 0$ and $x = 0.23$ at low temperatures show no evidence of long-range altermagnetic order with spins oriented along the $c$-axis or within the $ab$-plane. In contrast, temperature dependent susceptibility measurements in samples with $x \geq 0.16$ show a gradual downturn below $T\approx20~$K, suggestive of antiferromagnetic interactions, although this coexists with ferromagnetic hysteresis and remnant magnetization at $4~$K for samples with $x \geq 0.23$. Together, our magnetometry and neutron scattering measurements suggest the coexistence of antiferromagnetically coupled ferromagnetic CrO\textsubscript{2} clusters. This indicates that Cr ions do not hole dope Ru bands to induce an altermagnet state, but rather the holes remain localized to the Cr ions.

</details>

### [126] [Chiral Magnetic Conductivity in the Tight-Binding Model of Dirac Semimetals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19589)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解狄拉克半金属在电磁场共存下的电导率对磁场的依赖关系，并探究其背后的物理机制。

Result: 成功计算了强磁场极限下电导率对磁场的依赖关系，以及杂质散射引起的耗散率。

Abstract: We consider the typical tight - binding model of Dirac semimetal in the presence of both magnetic and electric fields. The electric conductivity reveals dependence on magnetic field. We calculate this dependence in the limit of strong magnetic field, when the given model is described effectively by the one - dimensional SSH model because the dynamics in the plane orthogonal to magnetic field is reduced to that of the lowest Landau level (LLL). Considering the small temperature limit we take into account dissipation due to scattering on impurities. The corresponding dissipation rate is calculated explicitly. The obtained results confirm that the source of the magnetoconductivity in this system is chiral magnetic effect.

### [127] [Coupled-channel approach to scattering of hybrid excitons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19634)
*Yasufumi Nakano,Meera M. Parish,Jesper Levinsen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过从头算构建赝势并求解耦合通道散射积分方程，非微扰计算了二维半导体双层中杂化激子（hybrid excitons）的散射特性，揭示了能量依赖散射、通道混合及电可调性等关键现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解二维半导体双层中由层间电荷载流子隧穿耦合的杂化激子（hybrid excitons）之间的相互作用，超越标准微扰理论的局限。

Method: 从微观电子-空穴描述出发，构建激子-激子相互作用的实际赝势（pseudopotentials），并将其作为输入代入耦合通道散射积分方程（coupled-channel scattering integral equation），实现非微扰（non-perturbative）计算。

Result: 杂化激子的相互作用强度随能量增加而快速增长，该特性继承自其间接激子（indirect-exciton）组分；介电屏蔽（dielectric screening）对直接通道和间接通道的影响不同，导致相互作用强度在不同介电环境中差异显著；杂化激子散射强度可通过斯塔克效应（Stark shift）进行电学调控。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了杂化激子散射中的能量依赖性和通道混合效应，为在实验相关介电环境中理解和调控杂化激子相互作用提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We consider the interactions of hybrid excitons in a two-dimensional semiconductor bilayer, where spatially direct and indirect excitons are hybridized by interlayer charge-carrier tunneling. Starting from a microscopic electron-hole description, we construct realistic pseudopotentials for exciton-exciton interactions and use them as inputs to a coupled-channel scattering integral equation. This enables non-perturbative calculations of hybrid-exciton scattering beyond standard perturbative theories, and highlights the importance of energy-dependent scattering and channel mixing. In particular, we show that the interaction strength of hybrid excitons exhibits a rapid growth with increasing energy, which we find is inherited from their indirect-exciton component. We further demonstrate that dielectric screening affects the direct and indirect channels in distinct ways, leading to markedly different interaction strengths across experimentally relevant dielectric environments. Finally, we show that the hybrid-exciton scattering strength can be electrically tuned via the Stark shift, which controls the direct-indirect detuning and hence the hybridization of the two exciton modes.

### [128] [Majorana bound states in anisotropic and tilted Dirac and Weyl systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19707)
*Abraham Kaleb Plascencia Pérez Páez,Alireza Qaiumzadeh*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文针对拓扑超导体（topological superconductors）中的马约拉纳边界模（Majorana boundary modes），发展了一套解析框架，分析了各向异性准粒子速度和倾斜能带结构对二维狄拉克（Dirac）和三维外尔（Weyl）系统中马约拉纳束缚态的影响，揭示了速度张量、界面几何和倾斜效应对马约拉纳手性、局域化、传播速度及有限尺寸微隙的调控机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管与狄拉克和外尔准粒子相关的马约拉纳束缚态已被广泛研究，但各向异性准粒子速度（anisotropic quasiparticle velocities）和倾斜能带结构（tilted band structures）如何改变其微观性质仍不清楚，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 建立了一套有效二维（2D）Bogoliubov–de Gennes（BdG）狄拉克理论的解析框架，并通过对超导配对（superconducting pairing）建立微观联系，将分析扩展至三维（3D）倾斜外尔体系。

Result: 对各向异性二维狄拉克系统，导出了连续拓扑不变量（topological invariant）、马约拉纳波函数、局域化长度、传播速度和有限尺寸微隙的闭式解析表达式；证明马约拉纳通道的手性由速度矩阵行列式的符号决定，而局域化和色散由速度张量与界面几何共同控制。对于倾斜二维狄拉克锥，发现倾斜不改变旋量本征态、贝里相位（Berry phase）和投影配对对称性，但会强烈抑制马约拉纳传播速度和有限尺寸微隙。在三维倾斜外尔系统中，证明自旋单态s波配对投影到低能外尔带上会自然产生有效手性p_x±ip_y配对对称性，为局域马约拉纳表面态提供微观BdG描述。

Conclusion: 该解析框架系统揭示了各向异性和倾斜效应对马约拉纳边界模微观性质的定量影响，为理解拓扑超导体中马约拉纳束缚态的调控机制提供了理论工具。

Abstract: Topological superconductors host Majorana boundary modes whose robustness is protected by the nontrivial topology of the bulk Bogoliubov quasiparticle spectrum. While Majorana bound states associated with Dirac and Weyl quasiparticles have been extensively investigated, much less is known about how anisotropic quasiparticle velocities and tilted band structures modify their microscopic properties. Here, we develop an analytical framework for Majorana bound states in effective two-dimensional (2D) Bogoliubov--de Gennes Dirac theories describing the surface quasiparticles of topological superconductors and extend the analysis to three-dimensional (3D) tilted Weyl systems by establishing a microscopic connection to the same low-energy description through superconducting pairing. For anisotropic 2D Dirac systems, we derive closed analytical expressions for the continuum topological invariant, Majorana wave function, localization length, propagation velocity, and finite-size minigap for arbitrary interface orientations. We show that the chirality of the Majorana channel is determined by the sign of the velocity-matrix determinant, while its localization and dispersion are governed jointly by the velocity tensor and the interface geometry. For tilted 2D Dirac cones, we demonstrate that the tilt leaves the spinor eigenstates, Berry phase, and projected pairing symmetry unchanged, but strongly suppresses the Majorana propagation velocity and finite-size minigap as the Lifshitz transition between type-I and type-II regimes is approached. Finally, we consider superconducting tilted 3D Weyl systems and show that the projection of a conventional spin-singlet $s$-wave pairing interaction onto the low-energy Weyl bands naturally generates an effective chiral $p_x\pm ip_y$ pairing symmetry, providing a microscopic Bogoliubov--de Gennes description that supports localized Majorana surface states.

</details>


### [129] [Nonreciprocal phonon propagation via spatially asymmetric magnon-phonon coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19788)
*Hiroyuki Moriya,Motoki Asano,Daiki Hatanaka,Yoshitaka Taniyasu,Hajime Okamoto,Hiroshi Yamaguchi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文展示了基于磁振子-声子耦合（magnon-phonon coupling）空间不对称性的表面声波（surface acoustic wave, SAW）非互易传播，其非互易性通过在薄压电薄膜下方形成声学波长尺度的厚磁性层实现，且该非互易性达到了基于单磁性层的SAW器件中的最高水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索基于单磁性层实现表面声波非互易传播的新机制，以克服现有结构复杂性的限制，并追求更高的非互易性水平。

Method: 利用声学波长尺度的厚磁性层置于薄压电薄膜下方，构建空间不对称的磁振子-声子耦合结构；通过偶极-偶极相互作用（dipole-dipole interactions）激活磁振子模式，使其根据表面声波传播方向局域于顶部或底部界面附近。

Result: 磁振子模式与表面声子模式之间的空间重叠（spatial overlap）随表面声波传播方向变化，从而导致方向依赖的显著单向传播；该非互易性达到了基于单磁性层的表面声波器件中的最高水平。

Conclusion: 该发现为在结构简单的磁机械器件（magnomechanical device）中实现非互易声学传播建立了一种新策略。

Abstract: Nonreciprocal propagation of surface acoustic waves (SAWs) based on the spatial asymmetry of magnon-phonon coupling is demonstrated. This nonreciprocity is enabled by an acoustic wavelength scale thick magnetic layer formed under a thin piezoelectric film. In this configuration, magnon modes activated by dipole-dipole interactions are localized near either the top or bottom interface depending on the propagation direction of the SAW. As a result, the spatial overlap between interfacial magnon and surface phonon modes is expected to become direction dependent, in a manner that leads to distinct unidirectional propagation of SAWs. Notably, the resulting nonreciprocity reaches the highest level among those reported for SAW devices based on a single magnetic layer. This finding will establish a new strategy of nonreciprocal acoustic propagation in a structurally simple magnomechanical device.

</details>


### [130] [Microscopic Conversion of Structural Chirality into Electronic Chirality in Artificial Chiral Clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19823)
*Tenchi Endo,Satoru Hayami*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过一个二维团簇模型（triangular-lattice core + rod-like extensions）研究了结构手性（structural chirality）如何转化为电子手性（electronic chirality），发现电环形单极子（ETM）和Edelstein效应均表现出反对称且非单调的结构依赖性，并指出自旋-轨道耦合、表面诱导的宇称混合与结构手性是关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阐明在人工表面纳米结构中，几何结构的手性如何微观地转化为电子系统的手性，并进一步产生手性输运响应（chiral transport responses）。

Method: 构建了一个二维团簇模型，包含三角晶格核心（triangular-lattice core）和三个杆状延伸（rod-like extensions），并在表面诱导的极化场（surface-induced polar field）下进行分析；通过计算电环形单极子（electric toroidal monopole, ETM）和Edelstein效应来量化电子手性，并结合实空间分析与参数分解（parameter-decomposition analysis）。

Result: ETM和Edelstein效应均随结构参数呈反对称、非单调变化；总态密度几乎不变，但ETM分辨谱（ETM-resolved spectrum）显著变化，表明手性编码在电子态对称性中；实空间分析显示ETM集中在顶点和杆部，Edelstein响应则更广泛地扩展到核心区域；参数分解表明自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）、表面诱导宇称混合（surface-induced parity mixing）和结构手性三者缺一不可。

Conclusion: 结构手性通过自旋-轨道耦合和宇称混合等机制被转化为电子手性，并驱动手性输运响应，从而揭示了人工表面纳米结构中微观连接机制。

Abstract: We investigate how structural chirality is converted into electronic chirality in a two-dimensional cluster model consisting of a triangular-lattice core and three rod-like extensions under a surface-induced polar field.
  By evaluating the electric toroidal monopole (ETM) and the Edelstein effect, we show that both quantities exhibit antisymmetric and nonmonotonic dependence
  on the structural parameter controlling the cluster geometry.
  While the total density of states is almost unaffected by the structural deformation, the ETM-resolved spectrum changes significantly, indicating that chirality is encoded in the symmetry character of the electronic states rather than in the overall electronic spectrum.
  Real-space analysis reveals that the induced ETM is concentrated near the vertices and rods, whereas the Edelstein response extends more broadly into the core region.
  Furthermore, a parameter-decomposition analysis identifies spin-orbit coupling, surface-induced parity mixing, and structural chirality as the essential ingredients for both phenomena.
  Our results clarify the microscopic connection between structural chirality, electronic chirality, and chiral transport responses in artificial surface nanostructures.

### [131] [THz-Driven Floquet Spin Valve-Modulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19897)

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在散射矩阵（$S$-matrix）框架结合高频Floquet–Magnus形式论（长度规范）下，研究了一维量子环中具有不对称（π/2）量子点接触构型的自旋相关量子输运。展示了在零静磁场下运行、基于铁磁引线的Datta–Das自旋场效应晶体管的非接触电磁模拟。利用太赫兹（THz）非共振场和电子游标效应，实现了高精度自旋通道切换、选择性自旋相位旋转以及超高对比度电流抑制（“光学快门”）。该架构对多光子泄漏边带具有鲁棒性，提供了一种热免疫、高速的半导体静态自旋晶体管替代方案。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用散射矩阵（$S$-matrix）框架，结合基于长度规范（length gauge）的高频Floquet–Magnus形式论（Floquet–Magnus formalism），对一维量子环（quantum ring）中不对称（π/2）量子点接触（quantum point contacts）构型下的自旋相关量子输运进行理论分析。

Result: 实现了Datta–Das自旋场效应晶体管的非接触电磁模拟，在零静磁场下工作；非共振太赫兹（THz）场可在不改变纳米结构静态参数的情况下实现高精度自旋通道切换；电子游标效应（electronic Vernier effect）诱导的选择性自旋相位旋转和超高对比度电流抑制（“光学快门”）；该架构对多光子泄漏边带（multiphoton leakage sidebands）具有基本鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 提出了一种热免疫（thermally immune）、高速的非接触式自旋晶体管架构，可作为传统半导体静态自旋晶体管的有前景替代方案。

Abstract: Within the scattering matrix ($S$-matrix) framework adapted to the high-frequency Floquet--Magnus formalism based on the length gauge, we investigate spin-dependent quantum transport in a 1D quantum ring with an asymmetric ($π/2$) configuration of quantum point contacts. We demonstrate the realization of a contactless electromagnetic analog of the Datta--Das spin field-effect transistor with ferromagnetic leads operating at zero static magnetic field. It is shown that an off-resonance terahertz (THz) field enables high-precision switching between spin channels without altering the static parameters of the nanostructure. Driven by an electronic Vernier effect, the quantum interference in the asymmetric geometry yields a selective spin phase rotator alongside an ultra-high-contrast current-suppression regime (``optical shutter''). The proposed architecture is fundamentally robust against multiphoton leakage sidebands, offering a thermally immune, high-speed alternative to conventional semiconductor static spin transistors.

### [132] [Spin-wave softening across the uniform-to-stripe domain transition in iron garnet film](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19993)
*Titiksha Srivastava,Victor Leroy,Nessrine Benaziz,Nathaniel Findling,Ludovic Largeau,Jamal Ben Youssef,Jean-Paul Adam,Thibaut Devolder,Joo-Von Kim*

TL;DR: 本文通过微观布里渊光散射（μ-BLS）和磁力显微镜，研究了具有垂直磁各向异性（PMA）的Bi掺杂铁石榴石薄膜中，从均匀相到条纹畴相的相变过程，揭示了自旋波谱的软化现象和附加模式，并建立了相应的理论模型与微磁模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用磁力显微镜进行实空间成像，以及热微观聚焦布里渊光散射（thermal microfocused Brillouin light scattering, μ-BLS）进行倒易空间测量；同时结合色散关系计算、μ-BLS光谱模型和微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulations）。

Result: 观察到由面内磁场驱动的均匀-条纹畴（uniform-to-stripe-domain）转变；在Damon-Eshbach几何（k ⊥ M）下发现了有限波矢（finite-k）软化现象，其波长在转变点与条纹周期匹配；μ-BLS光谱模型成功复现了固定场下的模式频率和相对强度；微磁模拟捕捉了条纹态的形成并复现了实验热μ-BLS谱。

Conclusion: 研究确立了具有垂直磁各向异性的BiYIG薄膜作为低阻尼模型平台，适用于研究自旋波冻结、条纹畴模式以及可重构磁子能带结构（reconfigurable magnonic band structures）。

Abstract: Spin-wave spectra across transitions between uniform and textured phases can offer deep insight into both symmetry-breaking physics and self-assembled magnonic bands. However, experiments require a material platform that combines low damping, well-defined textures, and spectroscopic access. Here, we study a Bi-doped iron-garnet film with perpendicular magnetic anisotropy (PMA), which undergoes a uniform-to-stripe-domain transition as a function of in-plane magnetic field. Real-space imaging by magnetic force microscopy reveals field-reorientable stripe domains aligned with the in-plane field, while reciprocal-space measurements using thermal microfocused Brillouin light scattering ($μ$-BLS) reveal the softening of a low-frequency spin-wave branch near the transition and the appearance of additional modes in the stripe-domain state. Calculated dispersion relations identify finite-$k$ softening in the Damon-Eshbach geometry ($k \perp M$), with the corresponding wavelength matching the stripe periodicity at the transition. In addition, a $μ$-BLS spectral model reproduces the measured mode frequencies and relative intensities at selected fixed fields. Micromagnetic simulations capture the field-driven formation of the stripe state and reproduce the experimental thermal $μ$-BLS spectra. Our findings establish BiYIG with PMA as a model low-damping platform for studying spin-wave freezing, stripe-domain modes, and reconfigurable magnonic band structures.

### [133] [Exact theory of chirality-dependent p-wave magnetism and Edelstein effect in spin spirals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20094)
*Börge Göbel,Tom G. Saunderson,Freia Opfermann,Lennart Schimpf,Ersoy Şaşıoğlu,Samir Lounis*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过解析方法证明，自旋-动量锁定（spin-momentum locking）可以仅由磁手性（magnetic chirality）产生，而非必须依赖于相对论性自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）。基于自旋螺旋（spin spiral）耦合电子的最小紧束缚模型（tight-binding model），作者建立了手性诱导自旋-动量锁定的精确可解模型，并推导了电导率和自旋Edelstein磁化率（spin Edelstein susceptibility）的闭合表达式，揭示了一种无自旋-轨道耦合的自旋极化微观机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋-动量锁定传统上被认为是相对论性自旋-轨道耦合的标志性特征。本文旨在挑战这一固有认知，探索磁手性是否可以独立于自旋-轨道耦合，单独产生自旋-动量锁定及相关的自旋极化现象，从而拓展对自旋-电荷转换（spin-charge conversion）机制的理解。

Method: 采用耦合自旋螺旋电子的最小紧束缚模型，并利用广义布洛赫定理（generalized Bloch theorem）进行解析求解。通过该精确解，推导了依赖于手性的p波磁性（p-wave magnetism）的自旋纹理（spin texture）不对称性（$\boldsymbol{s}(\boldsymbol{k})=-\boldsymbol{s}(-\boldsymbol{k})$），并进一步得到了电导率和自旋Edelstein磁化率的闭合表达式。

Result: 自旋螺旋能够产生手性依赖的p波磁性，其自旋纹理呈现反对称性。在强交换耦合（strong exchange-coupling）极限下，自旋螺旋中的自旋相关物理与电子在非磁性螺旋（non-magnetic helix）中传播时的轨道相关物理存在直接类比。磁手性单独就能生成自旋极化，无需自旋-轨道耦合参与。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个超越传统自旋-轨道耦合范式的手性诱导自旋-动量锁定与自旋-电荷转换的最小精确可解模型，为理解手性诱导自旋选择性（chirality-induced spin selectivity）提供了微观物理基础。

Abstract: Spin-momentum locking is widely regarded as a hallmark of relativistic spin-orbit coupling. Here we demonstrate analytically that it can instead emerge solely from magnetic chirality. Solving the minimal tight-binding model of electrons coupled to a spin spiral using a generalized Bloch theorem, we show that the spiral generates chirality-dependent p-wave magnetism characterized by the antisymmetric spin texture $\boldsymbol{s}(\boldsymbol{k})=-\boldsymbol{s}(-\boldsymbol{k})$. The exact solution further yields closed-form expressions for the electrical conductivity and the spin Edelstein susceptibility, revealing a microscopic mechanism by which magnetic chirality alone can generate spin polarization without spin-orbit coupling, with direct implications also for chirality-induced spin selectivity. In the strong exchange-coupling regime, the spin-dependent physics of the spin spiral becomes directly analogous to the orbital-dependent physics of electrons propagating through a non-magnetic helix. Our work establishes a minimal exactly solvable model of chirality-induced spin-momentum locking and spin-charge conversion beyond the conventional spin-orbit coupled paradigm.

</details>


### [134] [Frequency-Division Multiplexing in Magnonic Waveguides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20102)
*Alina-Cristina Bunea,Laurentiu Stoleriu,Giacomo Talmelli,Dan Neculoiu,Christoph Adelmann,Florin Ciubotaru*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过实验证明，在CoFeB波导中，利用全电激发与检测方式，不同频率和波长的自旋波（spin waves）可在线性区域内同时传播且无明显相互作用，从而验证了自旋波频分复用（frequency-division multiplexing）的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 频分复用是基于波的信息处理的关键功能，允许多个信息通道在同一物理介质中共存。本文旨在实验验证自旋波波导中能否实现多通道独立传播，为未来磁子计算（magnonic computing）和微波信号处理架构提供基础。

Method: 实验采用CoFeB自旋波波导，通过全电激发与检测方式，利用电感天线将两路独立微波信号同时耦合进入同一波导。使用宽带矢量网络分析仪（vector network analyzer）进行表征，采用双扫频（dual-sweep）和扫频加单音（sweep-plus-single-tone）两种激励方案，并结合线性叠加与相敏检测（phase-sensitive detection）理论分析以及微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulations）进行验证。

Result: 单通道与复用操作下的传输谱高度一致，表明不同频率和波长的自旋波在线性区域内同时传播且无可测相互作用。微磁模拟进一步确认了各自旋波模的振幅和波矢在共同传播过程中保持不变，在整个传播距离上均无相互作用。

Conclusion: 研究提供了直接的实验证据，证明独立自旋波通道可在单一波导中共存，支持在未来的磁子计算和微波信号处理架构中实现频分复用。

Abstract: Frequency-division multiplexing is a key functionality for wave-based information processing, enabling multiple information channels to coexist within the same physical medium. Here, we experimentally investigate spin-wave multiplexing in a CoFeB waveguide using all-electrical excitation and detection. Two independently generated microwave signals are simultaneously coupled into the same spin-wave waveguide through inductive antennas and characterized using broadband vector network analyzer measurements. The transmission spectra obtained under single-channel and multiplexed operation exhibit excellent agreement, demonstrating that spin waves with different frequencies and wavelengths propagate simultaneously without measurable interaction in the linear regime. The observation is confirmed using both dual-sweep and sweep-plus-single-tone excitation schemes. A theoretical analysis based on linear superposition and phase-sensitive detection explains the absence of observable inter-channel interference for independent microwave sources. Micromagnetic simulations further confirm that the amplitudes and wavevectors of the individual spin-wave modes remain unchanged during co-propagation, demonstrating the absence of interaction over the entire propagation distance. The results provide direct experimental evidence that independent spin-wave channels can coexist in a single waveguide and support the implementation of frequency-division multiplexing in future magnonic computing and microwave signal-processing architectures.

</details>


### [135] [Frequency-dependent electron-phonon coupling and vibrational responses in tight-binding and continuous Dirac models with nuclear velocity correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20117)
*Paolo Fachin,Francesco Macheda,Paolo Barone,Francesco Mauri*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从埃伦费斯特（Ehrenfest）拉格朗日方法出发，推导了局域原子轨道（LCAO）和紧束缚（tight-binding）方法中任意阶核速度下的运动方程与振动响应线性响应形式，重点评估了玻恩有效电荷（Born effective charges）和力常数矩阵（force-constant matrix）。研究表明，非局域相互作用中出现的核速度依赖的佩尔斯（Peierls-like）相位恢复了频率依赖振动响应的全电子求和规则，并在定性上显著修正了振动响应，对捕捉振动圆二色性（vibrational circular dichroism）等现象至关重要。作者在带隙石墨烯和拓扑时间反演对称性破缺的Haldane模型中验证了该修正，结果与第一性原理（\textit{ab initio}）计算高度一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核运动会诱发电子原子轨道中依赖核速度的相位（即电子平移因子，electron-translation factor），从而修正由局域原子轨道构建的有效哈密顿量。现有模型往往忽略这类修正，而它们对振动响应的定性描述（如振动圆二色性）至关重要。

Method: 采用埃伦费斯特拉格朗日方法（Ehrenfest Lagrangian approach）处理局域原子轨道和紧束缚方法，在线性响应形式下推导出任意阶核速度下的运动方程与振动响应，并重点计算了玻恩有效电荷和力常数矩阵。

Result: 非局域相互作用中出现的核速度依赖的佩尔斯类相位恢复了频率依赖振动响应的全电子求和规则。该修正从定性上改变了紧束缚模型的振动响应，是捕捉振动圆二色性等现象的必要条件。在带隙石墨烯和Haldane模型中的测试结果与第一性原理计算高度一致。

Conclusion: 核速度依赖的佩尔斯类相位修正对紧束缚模型中振动响应的正确描述不可或缺，能恢复求和规则并解释振动圆二色性等效应，在带隙石墨烯和拓扑模型中均获得第一性原理验证。

Abstract: The nuclear motion induces in the electronic atomic orbitals a nuclear-velocity-dependent phase (also known as electron-translation factor), which modifies the effective Hamiltonians constructed from localised atomic orbitals. In this work, using an Ehrenfest Lagrangian approach for the localised atomic orbitals (LCAO) and tight-binding methods, we determine, at any order in the nuclear velocity, the equations of motion and the vibrational responses within a linear response formalism, focusing on the tight-binding assessment of the Born effective charges and the force-constant matrix. The appearance of nuclear-velocity-dependent Peierls-like phases in the non-local part of the interactions restores the all-electron sum rules for frequency-dependent vibrational responses. In tight-binding models these corrections crucially modify the vibrational response from a qualitative point of view, also yielding contributions required to capture phenomena such as vibrational circular dichroism. We test these corrections in the tight-binding model for metallic gapped graphene - finding excellent agreement with \textit{ab initio} calculations - and for the topological time-reversal symmetry breaking Haldane model.

</details>


### [136] [Angular Momentum Quantization of a Charge-flux Composite: Quantum Electrodynamic Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20283)
*Kicheon Kang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过完整的量子电动力学（quantum electrodynamics, QED）方法结合诺特定理（Noether's theorem），论证了二维空间中电荷-通量复合体的总角动量严格遵循整数或半整数量子化规则，其表观分数角动量源于动力学角动量（kinetic angular momentum）与规范不变的相互作用角动量（interaction angular momentum）之间的补偿。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维电荷-通量复合体（charge-flux composite）的分数角动量（fractional angular momentum）是一个公认现象，通常由半经典哈密顿量导出。然而，当该复合体被视为自由二维空间中的孤立系统时，O(2)群的基本旋转和反射对称性要求其总角动量严格量子化。这一概念性矛盾构成了本文的出发点。

Method: 采用完整的量子电动力学（QED）方法，结合诺特定理（Noether's theorem）对电荷-通量复合体进行分析。通过考虑由真空电磁场介导的电荷与通量之间的相互作用，推导出相互作用角动量的具体形式，包括场动量（field momentum）和隐藏相对论动量（hidden relativistic momentum）。

Result: 相互作用角动量精确补偿了动力学角动量的分数部分，使得复合体的净角动量严格遵循整数或半整数量子化规则。传统的分数自旋（fractional spin）对应于微扰QED基态中动力学角动量的期望值。标准经典场角动量定义在二维中失效，原因在于存在非零边界项（non-vanishing boundary terms）。

Conclusion: 二维电荷-通量复合体的表观分数角动量与O(2)对称性要求的量子化总角动量之间并无矛盾；前者是动力学角动量的期望值，后者由动力学与相互作用角动量之和构成。该理论框架澄清了长期存在的概念分歧，并揭示了经典场角动量在二维情形下的局限性。

Abstract: The fractional angular momentum of a two-dimensional charge-flux composite is a well-established phenomenon usually derived from a semiclassical Hamiltonian. However, when the composite is treated as an isolated system in free two-dimensional space, the fundamental rotational and reflection symmetries of the $O(2)$ group demand that its total angular momentum is strictly quantized. We address this conceptual discrepancy by applying a full quantum electrodynamic (QED) approach combined with Noether's theorem. We demonstrate that the interaction between the charge and flux, mediated by the vacuum electromagnetic field, generates an intrinsic interaction angular momentum composed of both field momentum and hidden relativistic momentum. This gauge-invariant interaction angular momentum exactly compensates for the fractional part of the kinetic angular momentum. Consequently, the net angular momentum of the composite strictly follows the integer or half-integer quantization rule. Our formalism clarifies that the conventional fractional spin corresponds to the expectation value of the kinetic angular momentum within the perturbed QED ground state. It also elucidates why the standard classical field angular momentum definition fails to capture this in two dimensions, due to non-vanishing boundary terms.

</details>

### [137] [Probing the temperature dependence of dielectric function of ternary transition metal dichalcogenides: towards thermo-driven ultrathin photonic components](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20344)
*Artsruni Margaryan,Maria Levonyan,Maksim Sargsyan,David Karakhanyan,Meri Hayrapetyan,Kostya S. Novoselov,Davit A. Ghazaryan*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了三元过渡金属硫族化物（transition metal dichalcogenides, TMDs）MoSSe和WSSe在80–670 K宽温区、430–1000 nm光谱范围内的介电函数（dielectric permittivity functions），发现可见光（Vis）区域的介电响应温度演化遵循Varshni公式，并利用WSSe的光学色散（optical dispersion）设计了超薄平凸近红外（NIR）光子透镜，其性能可随温度连续调制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三元过渡金属硫族化物（TMDs）及其衍生物因其在可见光（Vis）和近红外（NIR）波段显著的激子共振（excitonic resonances）而备受关注，但该家族大多数成员的温度依赖光学色散（temperature-dependent optical dispersions）尚未被全面揭示。

Method: 在80–670 K的宽温区范围内，对单轴三元MoSSe和WSSe在430–1000 nm光谱区进行了系统的介电函数（dielectric permittivity functions）测量；利用测得的WSSe光学色散（optical dispersion）设计并制备了超薄平凸近红外（NIR）光子透镜。

Result: 可见光（Vis）区域介电响应的温度演化遵循Varshni公式，进而影响材料在无损近红外（NIR）光谱尾端的高折射率特性；基于WSSe设计的超薄平凸NIR光子透镜展现出随温度变化的连续性能调制。

Conclusion: 该工作为下一代热驱动（thermo-driven）纳米光子学（nanophotonic）和光电器件（optoelectronic devices）的创制提供了关键见解。

Abstract: Transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDs), along with their ternary derivatives, have attracted considerable attention mostly due to pronounced excitonic resonances emerging in visible (Vis) and near-infrared (NIR) spectral regions, enabling strong light-matter interaction. Nevertheless, a comprehensive insight of the temperature-dependent optical dispersions for the most of representatives of the family remains yet unrevealed. Here, we report on systematic studies of dielectric permittivity functions of uniaxial ternary MoSSe and WSSe across 430-1000 nm spectral region over a broad temperature window of 80-670 K. We show that the temperature evolution of their dielectric responses is governed by Varshni's formalism in Vis spectral region further affecting their high refractive index properties at the lossless NIR spectral tails. Furthermore, we exploit the measured optical dispersion of ternary WSSe designing ultrathin plano-convex NIR photonic lenses that demonstrate continuous modulation of performance with temperature variation. Our work provides critical insights for the creation of next-generation thermo-driven nanophotonic and optoelectronic devices.

</details>

### [138] [Fluid Memory Enhances Active Beating via Back-and-Forth Motion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19820)
*Subhajit Gupta,Supravat Dey*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过胶体模型在Jeffreys流体中的随机动力学实验，发现来回拍动（back-and-forth beating）会瞬态对齐驱动力与聚合物力，当流体记忆（fluid memory）与拍动持续时间相当时，拍动频率迅速增加，并在拍动周期涨落（beating-period fluctuations）中达到最大值；而单向旋转运动则随流体记忆增加而减速。该结果揭示了来回拍动是主动振荡器利用流体记忆的通用机制，为聚合物流体中鞭毛拍动增强提供了可能的解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纤毛和鞭毛的拍动常发生在粘弹性流体（viscoelastic fluids）中，周围流体对拍动动力学有强烈影响，但粘弹性效应如何影响拍动动力学仍知之甚少。

Method: 采用Jeffreys流体中实验实现的胶体模型（colloidal models），研究其随机动力学（stochastic dynamics）行为。

Result: 来回拍动瞬态对齐驱动力与聚合物力，当流体记忆与拍动持续时间相当时拍动频率迅速增加；该交叉点以拍动周期涨落最大化为标志。单向旋转运动则随流体记忆增加而减速。

Conclusion: 来回拍动是主动振荡器（active oscillators）利用流体记忆的通用机制，为聚合物流体中鞭毛拍动增强现象提供了可能的解释。

Abstract: Ciliary and flagellar beating often occurs in viscoelastic fluids. The surrounding fluid strongly influences the beating dynamics. Viscoelastic effects on beating dynamics, however, remain poorly understood. Here, we investigate the stochastic dynamics of experimentally realized colloidal models in a Jeffreys fluid. We find that back-and-forth beating transiently aligns the driving and polymeric forces, leading to a rapid increase in the beating frequency once the fluid memory becomes comparable to the stroke duration. The crossover is marked by a maximum in beating-period fluctuations. For unidirectional rotational motion, however, beating slows down with increasing fluid memory. Our results identify back-and-forth beating as a generic mechanism for exploiting fluid memory in active oscillators, providing a possible explanation for enhanced flagellar beating in polymeric fluids.

</details>


### [139] [Effective Complexity Reduction of the Landau-de Gennes Elastic Energy: A Quantitative Framework and Numerical Validation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19920)
*Razvan-Dumitru Ceuca,Simone Rusconi,Arghir-Dani Zarnescu*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文在向列型液晶（nematic liquid crystals）的 Landau-de Gennes 模型中，基于 Rusconi 等人 2025 年提出的广义最优缩放过程（generalized optimal scaling procedure, GOS），识别了多常数弹性能简化至少常数模型的显式参数区间，并通过 openQmin 数值模拟验证了缩放预测的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 Landau-de Gennes 模型中的多常数弹性能（multi-constant elastic energy）参数复杂，缺乏系统性的定量简化判据；本文旨在为从三常数模型到两常数乃至单常数模型的约化提供严格的参数区间依据。

Method: 基于 2025 年提出的广义最优缩放过程（GOS），从解析上推导出三常数模型 $(L_1,L_2,L_3)$ 可约化为 $(L_1,L_2,0)$ 以及两常数模型 $(L_1,L_2,0)$ 可约化为 $(L_1,0,0)$ 的参数临界值；随后利用 openQmin 仿真框架对缩放预测进行数值验证。

Result: 数值实验表明，当 $L_3$ 或 $L_2$ 低于 GOS 给出的临界阈值时，约化模型与完整模型之间的偏差保持在缩放理论所预测的同一量级，证实了解析缩放预测的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究为 Landau-de Gennes 框架下简化弹性模型的适用性提供了定量判据，并建立了最优缩放参数与数值模拟结果之间的直接联系。

Abstract: We revisit the elastic energy formulation of the Landau-de Gennes model for nematic liquid crystals, focusing on quantitative reductions of the multi-constant elastic energy. Building on the generalized optimal scaling procedure (GOS) introduced by Rusconi et al. in 2025, we identify explicit parameter regimes in which the three-constant model $(L_1,L_2,L_3)$ can be reduced to $(L_1,L_2,0)$ and how the two-constant model $(L_1,L_2,0)$ can be reduced to the commonly used one-constant configuration $(L_1,0,0)$. The analytical scaling predictions are tested numerically using the openQmin simulation framework, confirming that below a critical threshold for $L_3$ or $L_2$, given by GOS, the deviation from the reduced model remains of the same order of magnitude as predicted by the scaling theory. These results provide a quantitative criterion for the validity of reduced elastic models and establish a direct connection between optimal scaling arguments and numerical observations within the Landau-de Gennes framework.

</details>


### [140] [Emergence of Hexanematic Order in a Growing Confluent Cell Monolayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19963)
*Hon Lin Too,Farisan Dary,Isaac Si Yuan Ling,Dustin Erhard Theofilusa,Duo Zhang,Haiyi Liang,Ee Hou Yong*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过构建一个随机粒子- Voronoi框架（stochastic particle-Voronoi framework），展示了在上皮细胞集体迁移（collective migration）过程中，边界驱动的运动与密度-速度依赖的细胞分裂规则相结合，如何自发产生从边界到内部的不同细胞形态组织，即外围细胞更大、更细长且更易出现缺陷，而内部细胞保持较小、各向同性且六方密排。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 上皮层集体迁移在伤口愈合到癌症侵袭等过程中至关重要，其一个关键特征是在单个迁移汇合层内出现不同的细胞形态——活跃边界处出现更大、更细长的细胞，而内部则是较小且呈六方有序排列的细胞。现有方法难以在不预先设定目标几何形状或不同细胞类型的情况下捕捉这种六方-向列（hexanematic）组织。

Method: 开发了一种随机粒子-Voronoi框架（stochastic particle-Voronoi framework），该框架无需预设目标几何形状和不同细胞类型，能够自发捕捉六方-向列组织。模型中引入了边界驱动的集体运动，该运动产生向外的速度梯度，并与一个依赖于密度和速度的细胞分裂规则相耦合。

Result: 模型显示，边界驱动的集体运动产生向外的速度梯度。该梯度与密度和速度依赖的分裂规则耦合后，导致外围细胞变得更大、更细长且更易出现缺陷（defect-prone），而内部细胞则保持较小、各向同性（isotropic）且六方密排（hexagonally packed）。

Conclusion: 结果表明，在集体迁移过程中，最小的非平衡力学相互作用（non-equilibrium mechanical interactions）即可自发产生涌现的、自组织的组织尺度图案化（tissue-scale patterning）。

Abstract: Collective migration of epithelial layers underlies processes ranging from wound healing to cancer invasion. A defining yet challenging feature is the emergence of distinct cell morphologies within a single migrating confluent sheet, with larger, elongated cells at the active boundary and smaller, hexatically ordered cells in the bulk. Here, we develop a stochastic particle-Voronoi framework that captures this hexanematic organization without prescribing target geometries and distinct cell types. We show that boundary-driven collective motion generates an outward velocity gradient. This gradient, coupled to a density and velocity-dependent division rule, produces peripheral cells that are larger, more elongated, and more defect-prone, while bulk cells remain smaller, isotropic, and hexagonally packed. These results show how minimal, non-equilibrium mechanical interactions give rise to emergent, self-organized tissue-scale patterning during collective migration.

</details>


### [141] [Inferring activity from fluid flow in continuum models of active matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20100)
*Aditya Mohapatra,Sagarika Adhikary,Rajesh Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出基于深度学习的逆向问题求解框架，通过观测活性流体（active fluids）的流场数据推断活性物质（active matter）系统的模型参数并选择最适模型，分别应用于标量活性物质模型（Active Model H）和活性向列相模型（Active Nematics），利用流场的动能谱（kinetic energy spectrum）保留活性特征来实现高保真参数推断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性物质系统受微观尺度局域能量耗散驱动，远离热力学平衡（thermodynamic equilibrium）。虽然流体力学（hydrodynamic）连续框架在模拟这些非平衡现象（正向问题）方面非常成功，但直接测量活性应力（active stresses）极其困难，严重制约了对真实活性材料的表征，因此需要从可观测流场数据反向推断模型参数与结构。

Method: 构建广义流体力学逆推框架（generalized hydrodynamic inversion framework），采用深度学习（deep learning）方法，以活性流体流场数据为输入，提取流场的动能谱作为保留活性特征的高保真信号（high-fidelity signature），从而推断Active Model H（标量活性物质）和Active Nematics（含取向有序的活性系统）两类核心活性连续物理范例的模型参数，并实现模型选择（model selection）。

Result: 在Active Model H和Active Nematics两种模型中，流场的动能谱均能够保留高保真的活性特征信号，深度学习框架据此实现了对活性参数的准确推断，并支持从流场数据出发进行模型选择。

Conclusion: 该深度学习方法为基于活性物质连续模型流场数据解决模型推断（model inference）与模型选择问题提供了一条原则性（principled）路径，有望突破活性应力直接测量的瓶颈，推动活性材料逆向表征的发展。

Abstract: Active matter systems are driven out of thermodynamic equilibrium by localized, microscale energy dissipation. While hydrodynamic continuum frameworks are highly successful at simulating these non-equilibrium phenomena (the forward problem), characterizing real-world active materials is fundamentally bottlenecked by the difficulty of measuring active stresses directly. This paper addresses the inverse problem using deep learning: model inference and model selection from observable flow field data of active fluids. We formulate a generalized hydrodynamic inversion framework applied to two cornerstone paradigms of active continuum physics: Active Model H (representing scalar active matter) and Active Nematics (representing active systems with orientational order). We demonstrate that the kinetic energy spectrum obtained from the fluid flow fields preserve a high-fidelity signature of activity to infer parameters of active model H and active nematics. Our deep learning method presents a principled way to bear upon questions of model inference and selection given the flow field data in continuum models of active matter.

</details>


### [142] [Let's Stalk About Membranes: Committor-Based Enhanced Sampling of Stalk Formation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20122)
*Giorgia Rossi,Enrico Trizio,Davide Bochicchio,Giulia Rossi,Michele Parrinello*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文采用基于机器学习提交函数（committor function）的增强采样（enhanced sampling）策略，研究两亲性金纳米颗粒介导的膜融合早期步骤——茎状结构形成（stalk formation），获得了收敛的自由能估计和机制性洞察。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 膜融合在细胞通讯与功能中至关重要，但功能化纳米颗粒作为合成融合剂（synthetic fusogens）的分子机制尚不清楚，主要原因在于融合过程需跨越高自由能势垒，传统分子模拟难以捕捉，而增强采样方法依赖集体变量（collective variables）的定义，融合过程涉及大量分子的集体重排，难以简化为直观坐标。

Method: 采用基于提交函数（committor function）的增强采样策略，通过自洽（self-consistent）的机器学习流程学习提交函数，并将其作为有效的集体变量（collective variable），实现对膜融合路径的均匀采样，无需对体系具备大量先验知识。

Result: 从获得的反应轨迹（reactive trajectories）和广泛的过渡区采样中，得到了收敛的自由能估计（converged free-energy estimates）以及关于茎状结构形成（stalk formation）的机制性理解。

Conclusion: 基于机器学习提交函数的增强采样方法能够有效克服膜融合研究中集体变量定义困难的问题，为纳米颗粒介导的膜融合机制研究提供了可行的计算框架。

Abstract: Membrane fusion is essential for cellular communication and function, and understanding how two lipid bilayers merge is key to informing therapeutic strategies. Functionalized nanoparticles have recently emerged as synthetic fusogens, but the molecular mechanisms driving this process remain unclear, partly because fusion involves transitions over high free-energy barriers, difficult to capture in molecular simulations. While enhanced sampling methods can address this problem, they also rely on the definition of collective variables, which are especially hard to define for fusion, as it arises from the collective rearrangement of many molecules and cannot be easily reduced to a simple intuitive coordinate. Here, we study stalk formation, the first step of fusion, mediated by an amphiphilic gold nanoparticle, by employing an enhanced sampling strategy based on the committor function, machine-learned through a self-consistent procedure. This method requires minimal prior knowledge of the system and leverages the learned committor function as an effective collective variable, enabling uniform sampling of the entire pathway. From the resulting reactive trajectories and extensive transition region sampling, we obtain converged free-energy estimates and mechanistic insight into stalk formation.

</details>


### [143] [A Theoretical Framework for the Coupling of Macroscale-Nanoscale Mechanochemical Phenomena in Condensed Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20217)
*Brenden W Hamilton*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出一个非微扰（non-perturbative）理论框架，用于预测凝聚态（condensed matter）中高度非线形形变下共价键机械化学（covalent mechanochemistry）的反应动力学，并通过螺吡喃（spiropyran）实例展示了非线形应变场对力敏团（mechanophore）激活的调控作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 共价键机械化学已从基础科学发展到工程应用，但现有分析模型无法在真实条件下处理宏观应变引起的分子尺度高度非线形形变，缺乏预测凝聚态反应动力学的坚实理论框架。

Method: 该框架是非微扰的，描述了宏观-纳米尺度耦合现象（macroscale-nanoscale coupling），能捕捉高度应变分子中复杂非线形形变下的活化垒变化。表达式基于一般可观测量（general observables）构建，可通过原子模拟（atomistic simulations）参数化，支持从简单结构优化计算实现多尺度预测。

Result: 框架提供了可参数化的通用表达式，允许使用高级量子化学方法进行预测。以力致变色聚合物螺吡喃为示例，展示了非线形应变场如何主导力敏团激活行为。

Conclusion: 该工作为预测机械化学效应建立了一个非微扰理论框架，弥合了宏观应变与分子尺度非线形形变之间的理论缺口，推动了机械化学从经验研究向可预测定量理论的发展。

Abstract: The field of covalent mechanochemistry has transitioned from fundamental science to engineering applications, yet it lacks a robust theoretical framework for predicting reaction kinetics in condensed matter. Existing analytical models fail under realistic conditions where macroscopic strains drive molecular-scale deformations that are highly non-linear. We develop a non-perturbative theoretical framework that captures activation barrier changes in highly strained molecules undergoing complex, non-linear deformations, describing the macroscale-nanoscale coupling of phenomena. The framework yields general expressions, parameterizable from atomistic simulations, enabling multiscale prediction of mechanochemical behavior. By presenting the expressions in terms of general observables, this work enables predictions of mechanochemical effects from simple structure optimization calculations, enabling the use of high level quantum chemical methods. We demonstrate this approach on the mechanochromic polymer spiropyran, showing how non-linear strain fields govern mechanophore activation.

</details>
